::centre
Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa
::

# Khuddakanikāye

## Therāpadānapāḷi

#### (Paṭhamo bhāgo)

### 1. Buddhavaggo

#### 1. Buddhaapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Tathāgataṃ {pb:T:1.0001}{pb:M:1.0001}{pb:V:1.0001} jetavane vasantaṃ, apucchi vedehamunī nataṅgo;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Sabbaññubuddhā kira nāma honti, bhavanti te hetubhi kehi vīra’’.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Tadāha sabbaññuvaro mahesī, ānandabhaddaṃ madhurassarena;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Ye pubbabuddhesu {note:sabbabuddhesu (syā.)} katādhikārā, aladdhamokkhā jinasāsanesu.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Teneva sambodhimukhena dhīrā, ajjhāsayenāpi mahābalena;
::

::gathalast
Paññāya tejena sutikkhapaññā, sabbaññubhāvaṃ anupāpuṇanti.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahampi {pb:T:1.0002}{pb:V:1.0002} pubbabuddhesu, buddhattamabhipatthayiṃ,
::

::gathalast
Manasāyeva hutvāna, dhammarājā asaṅkhiyā.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atha {pb:M:1.0002}{pb:P:1.0001} buddhāpadānāni, suṇātha suddhamānasā;
::

::gathalast
Tiṃsapāramisampuṇṇā, dhammarājā asaṅkhiyā.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sambodhiṃ buddhaseṭṭhānaṃ, sasaṅghe lokanāyake;
::

::gathalast
Dasaṅgulī namassitvā, sirasā abhivādayiṃ {note:abhivādaye (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāvatā buddhakhettesu, ratanā vijjantisaṅkhiyā;
::

::gathalast
Ākāsaṭṭhā ca bhūmaṭṭhā {note:bhummaṭṭhā (sī. syā.)}, manasā sabbamāhariṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha rūpiyabhūmiyaṃ, pāsādaṃ māpayiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nekabhummaṃ ratanamayaṃ, ubbiddhaṃ nabhamuggataṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vicittathambhaṃ sukataṃ, suvibhattaṃ mahārahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kanakamayasaṅghāṭaṃ, kontacchattehi maṇḍitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭhamā veḷuriyā bhūmi, vimalabbhasamā subhā;
::

::gathalast
Naḷinajalajākiṇṇā, varakañcanabhūmiyā.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pavāḷaṃsā pavāḷavaṇṇā, kāci lohitakā subhā;
::

::gathalast
Indagopakavaṇṇābhā, bhūmi obhāsatī disā.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvibhattā gharamukhā, niyyūhā sīhapañjarā;
::

::gathalast
Caturo vedikā jālā, gandhāveḷā manoramā.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nīlā pītā lohitakā, odātā suddhakāḷakā;
::

::gathalast
Kūṭāgāravarūpetā, sattaratanabhūsitā.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Olokamayā {pb:P:1.0002} padumā, vāḷavihaṅgasobhitā;
::

::gathalast
Nakkhattatārakākiṇṇā, candasūrehi {note:candasuriyehi (sī. syā.)} maṇḍitā.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hemajālena {pb:T:1.0003} sañchannā, soṇṇakiṅkiṇikāyutā;
::

::gathalast
Vātavegena kūjanti, soṇṇamālā manoramā.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mañjeṭṭhakaṃ lohitakaṃ, pītakaṃ haripiñjaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nānāraṅgehi sampītaṃ {note:saṃcittaṃ (syā.)}, ussitaddhajamālinī {note:māliniṃ (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na naṃ {note:nānā (sī. syā.)} bahūnekasatā, phalikā rajatāmayā;
::

::gatha2
Maṇimayā lohitaṅgā, masāragallamayā tathā;
::

::gathalast
Nānāsayanavicittā, saṇhakāsikasanthatā.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kampalā {pb:M:1.0003}{pb:V:1.0003} dukūlā cīnā, paṭṭuṇṇā paṇḍupāvurā;
::

::gathalast
Vividhattharaṇaṃ sabbaṃ, manasā paññapesahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāsu tāsveva bhūmīsu, ratanakūṭalaṅkataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maṇiverocanā ukkā, dhārayantā sutiṭṭhare.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sobhanti esikā thambhā, subhā kañcanatoraṇā;
::

::gathalast
Jambonadā sāramayā, atho rajatamayāpi ca.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nekā sandhī suvibhattā, kavāṭaggaḷacittitā;
::

::gathalast
Ubhato puṇṇaghaṭānekā, padumuppalasaṃyutā.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atīte sabbabuddhe ca, sasaṅghe lokanāyake;
::

::gathalast
Pakativaṇṇarūpena, nimminitvā sasāvake.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena dvārena pavisitvā, sabbe buddhā sasāvakā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbasoṇṇamaye pīṭhe, nisinnā ariyamaṇḍalā.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye ca etarahi atthi, buddhā loke anuttarā;
::

::gathalast
Atīte {pb:T:1.0004} vattamānā ca, bhavanaṃ sabbe samāhariṃ.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paccekabuddhenekasate, sayambhū aparājite;
::

::gathalast
Atīte vattamāne ca, bhavanaṃ sabbe samāhariṃ.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kapparukkhā bahū atthi, ye dibbā ye ca mānusā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṃ dussaṃ samāhantā, acchādemi ticīvaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khajjaṃ bhojjaṃ sāyanīyaṃ, sampannaṃ pānabhojanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maṇimaye subhe patte, saṃpūretvā adāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dibbavatthasamā hutvā, maṭṭhā {note:maṭṭā (sī.)} cīvarasaṃyutā;
::

::gathalast
Madhurā sakkharā ceva, telā ca madhuphāṇitā.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tappitā paramannena, sabbe te ariyamaṇḍalā;
::

::gathalast
Ratanagabbhaṃ {pb:P:1.0003} pavisitvā, kesarīva guhāsayā.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahārahamhi sayane, sīhaseyyamakappayuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sampajānā samuṭṭhāya, sayane {note:seyye (syā.)} pallaṅkamābhujuṃ.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gocaraṃ {pb:M:1.0004} sabbabuddhānaṃ, jhānaratisamappitā;
::

::gathalast
Aññe dhammāni desenti, aññe kīḷanti iddhiyā.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññe {pb:V:1.0004} abhiññā appenti, abhiññā vasibhāvitā;
::

::gathalast
Vikubbanā vikubbanti, aññenekasahassiyo.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhāpi buddhe pucchanti, visayaṃ sabbaññumālayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Gambhīraṃ nipuṇaṃ ṭhānaṃ, paññāya vinibujjhare.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāvakā buddhe pucchanti, buddhā pucchanti sāvake;
::

::gathalast
Aññamaññañca {pb:T:1.0005} pucchitvā {note:pucchanti (sī. syā.)}, aññoññaṃ byākaronti te.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhā paccekabuddhā ca, sāvakā paricārakā;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ sakāya ratiyā, pāsādebhiramanti te.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chattā tiṭṭhantu ratanā, kañcanāveḷapantikā;
::

::gathalast
Muttājālaparikkhittā, sabbe dhārentu {note:dhārenti (ka.)} matthake.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavantu ceḷavitānā, soṇṇatārakacittitā;
::

::gathalast
Vicittamalyavitatā, sabbe dhārentu matthake.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vitatā malyadāmehi, gandhadāmehi sobhitā;
::

::gathalast
Dussadāmaparikiṇṇā, ratanadāmabhūsitā.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pupphābhikiṇṇā sucittā, surabhigandhabhūsitā;
::

::gathalast
Gandhapañcaṅgulikatā {note:gandhapañcaṅgulaṃ katā (aṭṭha.)}, hemacchadanachāditā.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catuddisā pokkharañño, padumuppalasanthatā;
::

::gathalast
Sovaṇṇarūpā khāyantu, padmaṃreṇurajuggatā.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pupphantu pādapā sabbe, pāsādassa samantato;
::

::gathalast
Sayañca pupphā muñcitvā, gantvā bhavanamokiruṃ.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sikhino tattha naccantu, dibbahaṃsā pakūjare;
::

::gathalast
Karavīkā ca gāyantu, dijasaṅghā samantato.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bheriyo sabbā vajjantu, vīṇā sabbā rasantu {note:ravantu (sī. syā.)} tā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbā saṅgīti vattantu, pāsādassa samantato.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāvatā {pb:T:1.0006}{pb:M:1.0005}{pb:P:1.0004} buddhakhettamhi, cakkavāḷe tato pare;
::

::gathalast
Mahantā jotisampannā, acchinnā ratanāmayā.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṭṭhantu soṇṇapallaṅkā, dīparukkhā jalantu te;
::

::gathalast
Bhavantu ekapajjotā, dasasahassiparamparā.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gaṇikā lāsikā ceva, naccantu accharāgaṇā;
::

::gathalast
Nānāraṅgā padissantu, pāsādassa samantato.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dumagge {pb:V:1.0005} pabbatagge vā, sinerugirimuddhani;
::

::gathalast
Ussāpemi dhajaṃ sabbaṃ, vicittaṃ pañcavaṇṇikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Narā nāgā ca gandhabbā, sabbe devā upentu te;
::

::gathalast
Namassantā pañjalikā, pāsādaṃ parivārayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci kusalaṃ kammaṃ, kattabbaṃ kiriyaṃ mama;
::

::gathalast
Kāyena vācā manasā, tidase sukataṃ kataṃ.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye sattā saññino atthi, ye ca sattā asaññino;
::

::gathalast
Kataṃ puññaphalaṃ mayhaṃ, sabbe bhāgī bhavantu te.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yesaṃ kataṃ suviditaṃ, dinnaṃ puññaphalaṃ mayā;
::

::gathalast
Ye ca tattha {note:tasmiṃ (sī. ka.)} na jānanti, devā gantvā nivedayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbalokamhi {note:sabbe lokamhi (syā. ka.)} ye sattā, jīvantāhārahetukā;
::

::gathalast
Manuññaṃ bhojanaṃ sabbaṃ {note:sabbe (syā.)}, labhantu mama cetasā.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Manasā dānaṃ mayā dinnaṃ, manasā pasādamāvahiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pūjitā sabbasambuddhā, paccekā jinasāvakā.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:T:1.0007} kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Duve bhave pajānāmi, devatte atha mānuse;
::

::gathalast
Aññaṃ gatiṃ na jānāmi, manasā patthanāphalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devānaṃ adhiko homi, bhavāmi manujādhipo;
::

::gathalast
Rūpalakkhaṇasampanno, paññāya asamo bhave.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhojanaṃ vividhaṃ seṭṭhaṃ, ratanañca anappakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vividhāni ca vatthāni, nabhā {note:nabhasā (syā.)} khippaṃ upenti maṃ.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pathabyā {pb:M:1.0006} pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi, dibbā bhakkhā upenti maṃ.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pathabyā {pb:P:1.0005} pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi, ratanā sabbe upenti maṃ.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pathabyā {pb:V:1.0006} pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi, sabbe gandhā upenti maṃ.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pathabyā pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ yaṃ {note:yattha (syā.), yaññaṃ (ka.)} hatthaṃ pasāremi, sabbe yānā upenti maṃ.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pathabyā pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi, sabbe mālā upenti maṃ.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pathabyā pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi, alaṅkārā upenti maṃ.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pathabyā {pb:T:1.0008} pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi, sabbā kaññā upenti maṃ.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pathabyā pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi, madhusakkharā upenti maṃ.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pathabyā pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi, sabbe khajjā upenti maṃ.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adhane addhika {note:addhike (syā.)} jane, yācake ca pathāvino;
::

::gathalast
Dadāmihaṃ {note:dadāmiha (sī.) dadāmi taṃ (syā.)} dānavaraṃ, sambodhivarapattiyā.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nādento pabbataṃ selaṃ, gajjento bahalaṃ giriṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sadevakaṃ hāsayanto, buddho loke bhavāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disā dasavidhā loke, yāyato natthi antakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tasmiñca disābhāgamhi, buddhakhettā asaṅkhiyā.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabhā pakittitā mayhaṃ, yamakā raṃsivāhanā;
::

::gathalast
Etthantare raṃsijālaṃ, āloko vipulo bhave.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ettake {pb:M:1.0007} lokadhātumhi, sabbe passantu maṃ janā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe maṃ anuvattantu, yāva brahmanivesanaṃ {note:sabbeva sumanā hontu, sabbe maṃ anuvattare (sī. syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Visiṭṭhamadhunādena, amatabherimāhaniṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etthantare janā sabbe, suṇantu madhuraṃ giraṃ.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammameghena vassante, sabbe hontu anāsavā;
::

::gathalast
Yettha pacchimakā sattā, sotāpannā bhavantu te.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Datvā {pb:T:1.0009}{pb:V:1.0007} dātabbakaṃ dānaṃ, sīlaṃ pūretvā asesato;
::

::gathalast
Nekkhammapāramiṃ gantvā, patto sambodhimuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṇḍite {pb:P:1.0006} paripucchitvā, katvā vīriyamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khantiyā pāramiṃ gantvā, patto sambodhimuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Katvā daḷhamadhiṭṭhānaṃ, saccapārami pūriya;
::

::gathalast
Mettāya pāramiṃ gantvā, patto sambodhimuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lābhālābhe sukhe dukkhe, sammāne cāvamānane {note:sammāne ca vimānane (ka.) sammānane vimānane (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha samako hutvā, patto sambodhimuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kosajjaṃ bhayato disvā, vīriyaṃ cāpi khemato;
::

::gathalast
Āraddhavīriyā hotha, esā buddhānusāsanī.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vivādaṃ bhayato disvā, avivādañca khemato;
::

::gathalast
Samaggā sakhilā hotha, esā buddhānusāsanī.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pamādaṃ bhayato disvā, appamādañca khemato;
::

::gathalast
Bhāvethaṭṭhaṅgikaṃ maggaṃ, esā buddhānusāsanī.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samāgatā bahū buddhā, arahantā {note:arahanto (syā.)} ca sabbaso;
::

::gathalast
Sambuddhe arahante ca, vandamānā namassatha.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ acintiyā buddhā, buddhadhammā acintiyā;
::

::gathalast
Acintiye pasannānaṃ, vipāko hoti acintiyo’’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ bhagavā attano buddhacariyaṃ sambhāvayamāno buddhāpadāniyaṃ {note:buddhacariyaṃ (sī.) buddhacaritaṃ (syā.)} nāma dhammapariyāyaṃ abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Buddhāpadānaṃ samattaṃ.
::

#### 2. Paccekabuddhaapadānaṃ

Atha {pb:T:1.0010}{pb:M:1.0008} paccekabuddhāpadānaṃ suṇātha –

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tathāgataṃ {pb:P:1.0007} jetavane vasantaṃ, apucchi vedehamunī nataṅgo;
::

::gathalast
‘Paccekabuddhā kira nāma honti, bhavanti te hetubhi kehi vīra’ {note:dhīra (sī.) dhīrā (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāha {pb:V:1.0008} sabbaññuvaro mahesī, ānandabhaddaṃ madhurassarena;
::

::gathalast
‘Ye pubbabuddhesu {note:sabbabuddhesu (syā. ka.)} katādhikārā, aladdhamokkhā jinasāsanesu.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Teneva saṃvegamukhena dhīrā, vināpi buddhehi sutikkhapaññā;
::

::gathalast
Ārammaṇenāpi parittakena, paccekabodhiṃ anupāpuṇanti.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sabbamhi lokamhi mamaṃ ṭhapetvā, paccekabuddhehi samova natthi;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ imaṃ vaṇṇapadesamattaṃ, vakkhāmahaṃ sādhu mahāmunīnaṃ.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sayameva {pb:T:1.0011} buddhānaṃ mahāisīnaṃ, sādhūni vākyāni madhūva {note:madhuṃva (sī.)} khuddaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anuttaraṃ bhesajaṃ patthayantā, suṇātha sabbesu pasannacittā.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
89\.

::gatha1

::gathalast
Hitvā papañce jitaphanditāni {note:vidiya phanditāni (sī.) jitabandhitāni (ka.)}, tatheva bodhiṃ anupāpuṇiṃsu.
::

::hangnum
90\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum

#### 3-1. Sāriputtattheraapadānaṃ

Atha therāpadānaṃ suṇātha –

::hangnum
141\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Himavantassa {pb:T:1.0022}{pb:P:1.0015} avidūre, lambako nāma pabbato;
::

::gathalast
Assamo sukato mayhaṃ, paṇṇasālā sumāpitā.
::

::hangnum
142\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uttānakūlā nadikā, supatitthā manoramā;
::

::gathalast
Susuddhapuḷinākiṇṇā, avidūre mamassamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
143\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asakkharā apabbhārā, sādu appaṭigandhikā;
::

::gathalast
Sandatī nadikā tattha, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
144\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kumbhīlā makarā cettha, susumārā {note:suṃsumārā (sī. syā. )} ca kacchapā;
::

::gathalast
Caranti nadiyā tattha, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
145\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṭhīnā pāvusā macchā, balajā {note:vajalā (sī. syā.) jalajā (pī.)} muñjarohitā;
::

::gathalast
Vaggaḷā {note:vaggulā (sī.) vagguḷā (syā.) maggurā (theragāthā)} papatāyantā, sobhayanti {note:papatāyanti, sobhayantā (ka.)} mamassamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
146\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubho {pb:M:1.0017} kūlesu nadiyā, pupphino phalino dumā;
::

::gathalast
Ubhato abhilambantā, sobhayanti {note:abhilambanti sobhayantā (ka.)} mamassamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
147\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ambā sālā ca tilakā, pāṭalī sinduvārakā {note:sinduvārikā (bahūsu)};
::

::gathalast
Dibbagandhā sampavanti, pupphitā mama assame.
::

::hangnum
148\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Campakā saḷalā nīpā {note:nimbā (ka.)}, nāgapunnāgaketakā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
149\.
::

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
150\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ketakā {pb:P:1.0016} kandali {note:kadalī (syā.)} ceva, godhukā tiṇasūlikā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
151\.

152\.

153\.

::hangnum
154\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
155\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

159\.

::hangnum

::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbe migā uttasanti, migarājassa gajjato;
::

::gathalast
Tathā hi jātimā eso, pasū tāseti sabbadā.
::

::hangnum
338\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gajjato {pb:T:1.0042} te mahāvīra, vasudhā sampakampati;
::

::gathalast
Bodhaneyyāvabujjhanti, tasanti mārakāyikā.
::

::hangnum
339\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasanti titthiyā sabbe, nadato te mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Kākā senāva vibbhantā, migaraññā yathā migā.
::

::hangnum
340\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye keci gaṇino loke, satthāroti pavuccare;
::

::gathalast
Paramparāgataṃ dhammaṃ, desenti parisāya te.
::

::hangnum
341\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hevaṃ tvaṃ mahāvīra, dhammaṃ desesi pāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sāmaṃ saccāni bujjhitvā, kevalaṃ bodhipakkhiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
342\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āsayānusayaṃ ñatvā, indriyānaṃ balābalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhabbābhabbe viditvāna, mahāmeghova gajjasi.
::

::hangnum
343\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cakkavāḷapariyantā{pb:M:1.0032}, nisinnā parisā bhave;
::

::gathalast
Nānādiṭṭhī vicinantā {note:vicintenti (syā.), vicinantaṃ (ka.)}, vimaticchedanāya taṃ.
::

::hangnum
344\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbesaṃ {pb:P:1.0029} cittamaññāya, opammakusalo muni;
::

::gathalast
Ekaṃ pañhaṃ kathentova, vimatiṃ chindasi {note:chindi (syā. ka.)} pāṇinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
345\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upatissasadiseheva, vasudhā pūritā bhave;
::

::gathalast
Sabbeva te pañjalikā, kittayuṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
346\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kappaṃ vā te kittayantā, nānāvaṇṇehi kittayuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Parimetuṃ na sakkeyyuṃ {note:na kappeyyuṃ (syā.), na pappeyyuṃ (ka.)}, appameyyo tathāgato.
::

::hangnum
347\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathāsakena {pb:V:1.0027} thāmena, kittito hi mayā jino;
::

::gathalast
Kappakoṭīpi kittentā, evameva pakittayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
348\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace {pb:T:1.0043} hi koci devo vā, manusso vā susikkhito;
::

::gathalast
Pametuṃ parikappeyya, vighātaṃva labheyya so.
::

::hangnum
349\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāsane te patiṭṭhāya, sakyaputta mahāyasa;
::

::gathalast
Paññāya pāramiṃ gantvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
350\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Titthiye sampamaddāmi, vattemi jinasāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhammasenāpati ajja, sakyaputtassa sāsane.
::

::hangnum
351\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aparimeyye kataṃ kammaṃ, phalaṃ dassesi me idha;
::

::gathalast
Sukhitto saravegova, kilese jhāpayī mama {note:jhāpayiṃ mama (syā.), jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
352\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo koci manujo bhāraṃ, dhāreyya matthake sadā;
::

::gathalast
Bhārena dukkhito assa, bhārehi bharito tathā.
::

::hangnum
353\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ḍayhamāno tīhaggīhi, bhavesu saṃsariṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bharito bhavabhārena, giriṃ uccārito yathā.
::

::hangnum
354\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Oropito ca me bhāro, bhavā ugghāṭitā mayā;
::

::gathalast
Karaṇīyaṃ kataṃ sabbaṃ, sakyaputtassa sāsane.
::

::hangnum
355\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāvatā buddhakhettamhi, ṭhapetvā sakyapuṅgavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ aggomhi paññāya, sadiso me na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
356\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samādhimhi {pb:M:1.0033} sukusalo, iddhiyā pāramiṃ gato;
::

::gathalast
Icchamāno cahaṃ ajja, sahassaṃ abhinimmine.
::

::hangnum
357\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anupubbavihārassa{pb:P:1.0030}, vasībhūto mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Kathesi sāsanaṃ mayhaṃ, nirodho sayanaṃ mama.
::

::hangnum
358\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dibbacakkhu {pb:T:1.0044} visuddhaṃ me, samādhikusalo ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sammappadhānānuyutto, bojjhaṅgabhāvanārato.
::

::hangnum
359\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāvakena hi pattabbaṃ, sabbameva kataṃ mayā;
::

::gathalast
Lokanāthaṃ ṭhapetvāna, sadiso me na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
360\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samāpattīnaṃ kusalo {note:samāpattinayakusalo (sī.)}, jhānavimokkhāna khippapaṭilābhī;
::

::gathalast
Bojjhaṅgabhāvanārato, sāvakaguṇapāramigatosmi.
::

::hangnum
361\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāvakaguṇenapi {pb:V:1.0028} phussena {note:sāvakaguṇaphussena (syā.)}, buddhiyā parisuttamabhāravā {note:purisuttamagāravā (syā.), purisuttamabhāravā (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ saddhāsaṅgahitaṃ {note:saddhāya saṅgahitaṃ (sī.), saddāsaṅgahitaṃ (syā.)} cittaṃ, sadā sabrahmacārīsu.
::

::hangnum
362\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uddhatavisova sappo, chinnavisāṇova usabho;
::

::gathalast
Nikkhittamānadappova {note:dabbova (ka.)}, upemi garugāravena gaṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
363\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadi rūpinī bhaveyya, paññā me vasumatīpi {note:vasumatī (sī. ka.) vasupatīnaṃ (syā.)} na sameyya;
::

::gathalast
Anomadassissa {note:anomadassi (?)} bhagavato, phalametaṃ ñāṇathavanāya.
::

::hangnum
364\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pavattitaṃ dhammacakkaṃ, sakyaputtena tādinā;
::

::gathalast
Anuvattemahaṃ sammā, ñāṇathavanāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
365\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā me kadāci pāpiccho, kusīto hīnavīriyo;
::

::gathalast
Appassuto anādaro {note:anācāro (sabbattha) theragā. 987 passitabbā}, sameto ahu katthaci.
::

::hangnum
366\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bahussuto ca medhāvī, sīlesu susamāhito;
::

::gathalast
Cetosamathānuyutto, api muddhani tiṭṭhatu.
::

::hangnum
367\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ vo vadāmi bhaddante, yāvantettha samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Appicchā hotha santuṭṭhā, jhāyī jhānaratā sadā.
::

::hangnum
368\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yamahaṃ {pb:T:1.0045}{pb:M:1.0034}{pb:P:1.0031} paṭhamaṃ disvā, virajo vimalo ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
So me ācariyo dhīro, assaji nāma sāvako.
::

::hangnum
369\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassāhaṃ vāhasā ajja, dhammasenāpatī ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha pāramiṃ patvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
370\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo me ācariyo āsi, assaji nāma sāvako;
::

::gathalast
Yassaṃ disāyaṃ vasati, ussīsamhi karomahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
371\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama kammaṃ saritvāna, gotamo sakyapuṅgavo;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapesi maṃ.
::

::hangnum
372\.
::

::gatha1
{note:imā dve gāthāyo syāmapotthake na santi}
::

Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā.

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
373\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, buddhaseṭṭhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ {note:imā dve gāthāro syāmapotthake na santi}.
::

::hangnum
374\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:V:1.0029} catasso {note:catasso ca (sī.)}, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sāriputto thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sāriputtattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 3-2. Mahāmoggallānattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
375\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anomadassī bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
::

::gathalast
Vihāsi himavantamhi, devasaṅghapurakkhato.
::

::hangnum
376\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Varuṇo nāma nāmena, nāgarājā ahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Kāmarūpī vikubbāmi, mahodadhinivāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
377\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅgaṇiyaṃ {pb:T:1.0046} gaṇaṃ hitvā, tūriyaṃ paṭṭhapesahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sambuddhaṃ parivāretvā, vādesuṃ accharā tadā.
::

::hangnum
378\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vajjamānesu {pb:M:1.0035} tūresu, devā tūrāni {note:turiyesu, devā turiyāni (sī. syā.)} vajjayuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ubhinnaṃ saddaṃ sutvāna, buddhopi sampabujjhatha.
::

::hangnum
379\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nimantetvāna sambuddhaṃ, sakaṃ bhavanupāgamiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āsanaṃ paññapetvāna, kālamārocayiṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
380\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khīṇāsavasahassehi, parivuto lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Obhāsento disā sabbā, bhavanaṃ me upāgami.
::

::hangnum
381\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upaviṭṭhaṃ {pb:P:1.0032} mahāvīraṃ, devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabhikkhusaṅghaṃ tappesiṃ {note:santappesiṃ (syā.), tappemi (ka.)}, annapānenahaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
382\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anumodi mahāvīro, sayambhū aggapuggalo;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
383\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo so {note:yaṃ so (ka.)} saṅghaṃ apūjesi, buddhañca lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tena cittappasādena, devalokaṃ gamissati.
::

::hangnum
384\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sattasattatikkhattuñca, devarajjaṃ karissati;
::

::gathalast
Pathabyā rajjaṃ aṭṭhasataṃ, vasudhaṃ āvasissati.
::

::hangnum
385\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Pañcapaññāsakkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Bhogā asaṅkhiyā tassa, uppajjissanti tāvade.
::

::hangnum
386\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Aparimeyye {pb:V:1.0030} ito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena {note:nāmena (sī.)}, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
387\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Nirayā {pb:T:1.0047} so cavitvāna, manussataṃ gamissati;
::

::gathalast
Kolito nāma nāmena, brahmabandhu bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
388\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘So pacchā pabbajitvāna, kusalamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast
Gotamassa bhagavato, dutiyo hessati sāvako.
::

::hangnum
389\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Āraddhavīriyo pahitatto, iddhiyā pāramiṃ gato;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
::

::hangnum
390\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāpamittopanissāya, kāmarāgavasaṃ gato;
::

::gathalast
Mātaraṃ pitarañcāpi, ghātayiṃ duṭṭhamānaso.
::

::hangnum
391\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:M:1.0036} yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, nirayaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pāpakammasamaṅgitā, bhinnasīso marāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
392\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ, carimo vattate bhavo;
::

::gathalast
Idhāpi ediso mayhaṃ, maraṇakāle bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
393\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pavivekamanuyutto, samādhibhāvanārato;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
394\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dharaṇimpi sugambhīraṃ, bahalaṃ duppadhaṃsiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vāmaṅguṭṭhena khobheyyaṃ, iddhiyā pāramiṃ gato.
::

::hangnum
395\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asmimānaṃ na passāmi, māno mayhaṃ na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Sāmaṇere upādāya, garucittaṃ karomahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
396\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aparimeyye ito kappe, yaṃ kammamabhinīhariṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tāhaṃ bhūmimanuppatto, pattomhi āsavakkhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
397\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:T:1.0048}{pb:P:1.0033} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahāmoggallāno thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Mahāmoggallānattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3-3. Mahākassapattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
398\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttarassa {pb:V:1.0031} bhagavato, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Nibbute lokanāthamhi, pūjaṃ kubbanti satthuno.
::

::hangnum
399\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Udaggacittā janatā, āmoditapamoditā;
::

::gathalast
Tesu saṃvegajātesu, pīti me udapajjatha.
::

::hangnum
400\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ñātimitte samānetvā, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ;
::

::gathalast
Parinibbuto mahāvīro, handa pūjaṃ karomase.
::

::hangnum
401\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sādhūti te paṭissutvā, bhiyyo hāsaṃ janiṃsu me;
::

::gathalast
Buddhasmiṃ lokanāthamhi, kāhāma puññasañcayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
402\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Agghiyaṃ {pb:M:1.0037} sukataṃ katvā, satahatthasamuggataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Diyaḍḍhahatthapatthaṭaṃ, vimānaṃ nabhamuggataṃ.
::

::hangnum
403\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Katvāna hammiyaṃ tattha, tālapantīhi cittitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, cetiyaṃ pūjayuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
404\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aggikkhandhova {pb:T:1.0049} jalito, kiṃsuko iva {note:sālarājāva (sī.)} phullito;
::

::gathalast
Indalaṭṭhīva ākāse, obhāseti catuddisā.
::

::hangnum
405\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, katvāna kusalaṃ bahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pubbakammaṃ saritvāna, tidasaṃ upapajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
406\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sahassayuttaṃ {pb:P:1.0034} hayavāhiṃ, dibbayānamadhiṭṭhito;
::

::gathalast
Ubbiddhaṃ bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ, sattabhūmaṃ samuggataṃ.
::

::hangnum
407\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kūṭāgārasahassāni, sabbasoṇṇamayā ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Jalanti sakatejena, disā sabbā pabhāsayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
408\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Santi aññepi niyyūhā, lohitaṅgamayā tadā;
::

::gathalast
Tepi jotanti ābhāya, samantā caturo disā.
::

::hangnum
409\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puññakammābhinibbattā, kūṭāgārā sunimmitā;
::

::gathalast
Maṇimayāpi jotanti, disā dasa {note:disodisaṃ (syā.)} samantato.
::

::hangnum
410\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesaṃ ujjotamānānaṃ, obhāso vipulo ahu;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe deve abhibhomi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
411\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṭṭhikappasahassamhi{pb:V:1.0032}, ubbiddho nāma khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Cāturanto vijitāvī, pathaviṃ āvasiṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
412\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatheva bhaddake kappe, tiṃsakkhattuṃ ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakakammābhiraddhomhi, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
413\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattaratanasampanno, catudīpamhi issaro;
::

::gathalast
Tatthāpi bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ, indalaṭṭhīva uggataṃ.
::

::hangnum
414\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āyāmato {pb:T:1.0050}{pb:M:1.0038} catubbīsaṃ, vitthārena ca dvādasa;
::

::gathalast
Rammaṇaṃ {note:rammakaṃ (sī. syā.)} nāma nagaraṃ, daḷhapākāratoraṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
415\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āyāmato pañcasataṃ, vitthārena tadaḍḍhakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ākiṇṇaṃ janakāyehi, tidasānaṃ puraṃ viya.
::

::hangnum
416\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā sūcighare sūcī, pakkhittā paṇṇavīsati;
::

::gathalast
Aññamaññaṃ paghaṭṭenti, ākiṇṇaṃ hoti laṅkataṃ {note:taṃ tadā (sī.), satatā (syā.), saṅkaraṃ (?)}.
::

::hangnum
417\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evampi nagaraṃ mayhaṃ, hatthissarathasaṃkulaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Manussehi sadākiṇṇaṃ, rammaṇaṃ nagaruttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
418\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha bhutvā pivitvā ca, puna devattanaṃ gato {note:punapi devataṅgato (ka.)}.
::

::gathalast
Bhave pacchimake mayhaṃ, ahosi kulasampadā.
::

::hangnum
419\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Brāhmaññakulasambhūto{pb:P:1.0035}, mahāratanasañcayo;
::

::gathalast
Asītikoṭiyo hitvā, hiraññassāpi pabbajiṃ.
::

::hangnum
420\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahākassapo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Mahākassapattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 3-4. Anuruddhattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
421\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sumedhaṃ {pb:T:1.0051} bhagavantāhaṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vūpakaṭṭhaṃ viharantaṃ, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
422\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upagantvāna sambuddhaṃ, sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, buddhaseṭṭhamayācahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
423\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anukampa {pb:V:1.0033} mahāvīra, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha;
::

::gathalast
Padīpaṃ te padassāmi, rukkhamūlamhi jhāyato.
::

::hangnum
424\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adhivāsesi so dhīro, sayambhū vadataṃ varo;
::

::gathalast
Dumesu vinivijjhitvā, yantaṃ yojiyahaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
425\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sahassavaṭṭiṃ {pb:M:1.0039} pādāsiṃ, buddhassa lokabandhuno;
::

::gathalast
Sattāhaṃ pajjalitvāna, dīpā vūpasamiṃsu me.
::

::hangnum
426\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena cittappasādena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, vimānamupapajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
427\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upapannassa devattaṃ, byamhaṃ āsi sunimmitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samantato pajjalati, dīpadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
428\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samantā {pb:P:1.0036} yojanasataṃ, virocesimahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe deve abhibhomi, dīpadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
429\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṃsakappāni {pb:T:1.0052} devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na maṃ kecītimaññanti, dīpadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
430\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭhavīsatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Divā rattiñca passāmi, samantā yojanaṃ tadā.

::hangnum
431\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sahassalokaṃ ñāṇena, passāmi satthu sāsane;
::

::gathalast
Dibbacakkhumanuppatto, dīpadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
432\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sumedho nāma sambuddho, tiṃsakappasahassito;
::

::gathalast
Tassa dīpo mayā dinno, vippasannena cetasā.
::

::hangnum
433\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā anuruddho thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Anuruddhattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 3-5. Puṇṇamantāṇiputtattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
434\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjhāyako mantadharo, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Purakkhatomhi sissehi, upagacchiṃ naruttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
435\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:V:1.0034} lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Mama kammaṃ pakittesi, saṅkhittena mahāmuni.
::

::hangnum
436\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāhaṃ {pb:M:1.0040} dhammaṃ suṇitvāna, abhivādetvāna satthuno;
::

::gathalast
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, pakkamiṃ {note:pakkāmiṃ (sī. syā.)} dakkhiṇāmukho.
::

::hangnum
437\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅkhittena {pb:T:1.0053} suṇitvāna, vitthārena abhāsayiṃ {note:adesayiṃ (sī. syā.)};
::

::gatha2
Sabbe sissā attamanā, sutvāna mama bhāsato;
::

::gathalast
Sakaṃ diṭṭhiṃ vinodetvā, buddhe cittaṃ pasādayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
438\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅkhittenapi desemi, vitthārena tathevahaṃ {note:desesiṃ vitthārenapi bhāsayiṃ (ka.)};
::

::gatha2
Abhidhammanayaññūhaṃ{pb:P:1.0037}, kathāvatthuvisuddhiyā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbesaṃ viññāpetvāna, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
439\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito pañcasate kappe, caturo suppakāsakā;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampannā, catudīpamhi issarā.
::

::hangnum
440\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā puṇṇo mantāṇiputto thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Puṇṇamantāṇiputtattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 3-6. Upālittheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
441\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare haṃsavatiyā, sujāto nāma brāhmaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Asītikoṭinicayo, pahūtadhanadhaññavā.
::

::hangnum
442\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjhāyako mantadharo, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Lakkhaṇe itihāse ca, sadhamme pāramiṃ gato.
::

::hangnum
443\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paribbājā {pb:T:1.0054} ekasikhā {note:ekabhikkhā (ka.)}, gotamā
::

Buddhasāvakā {note:sabbatthapi evameva dissati}.

::gathalast
Carakā tāpasā ceva, caranti mahiyā tadā.
::

::hangnum
444\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tepi maṃ parivārenti, brāhmaṇo vissuto iti;
::

::gathalast
Bahujjano maṃ pūjeti, nāhaṃ pūjemi kiñcanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
445\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pūjārahaṃ {pb:M:1.0041} na passāmi, mānatthaddho ahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Buddhoti vacanaṃ natthi, tāva nuppajjate jino.
::

::hangnum
446\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Accayena {pb:V:1.0035} ahorattaṃ, padumuttaranāmako {note:nāyako (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṃ tamaṃ vinodetvā, loke uppajji cakkhumā.
::

::hangnum
447\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vitthārike bāhujaññe, puthubhūte ca sāsane;
::

::gathalast
Upāgami tadā buddho, nagaraṃ haṃsasavhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
448\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pitu atthāya {pb:P:1.0038} so buddho, dhammaṃ desesi cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast
Tena kālena parisā, samantā yojanaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
449\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sammato manujānaṃ so, sunando nāma tāpaso;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
450\.

::gatha1
‘‘Catusaccaṃ pakāsente, seṭṭhe ca {note:heṭṭhā ca (ka.)} pupphamaṇḍape;
::

::gathalast
Koṭisatasahassānaṃ, dhammābhisamayo ahu.

::hangnum
451\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

452\.

::gatha1

::

453\.

456\.

::hangnum
507\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassupādāya, tāhaṃ paricare muni;
::

::gathalast
Sāyaṃ pātaṃ namassāmi, devā āsāvatiṃ yathā.

::hangnum
508\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

509\.

::gatha1

::gatha1

594\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, buddhaseṭṭhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
595\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā upāli thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Upālittherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 3-7. Aññāsikoṇḍaññattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
596\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttarasambuddhaṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ vināyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Buddhabhūmimanuppattaṃ, paṭhamaṃ addasaṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
597\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāvatā {pb:V:1.0046} bodhiyā mūle, yakkhā sabbe samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Sambuddhaṃ parivāretvā, vandanti pañjalīkatā.
::

::hangnum
598\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbe {pb:M:1.0053}{pb:P:1.0049} devā tuṭṭhamanā, ākāse sañcaranti te;
::

::gathalast
Buddho ayaṃ anuppatto, andhakāratamonudo.
::

::hangnum
599\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesaṃ {pb:T:1.0070} hāsaparetānaṃ, mahānādo avattatha;
::

::gathalast
Kilese jhāpayissāma, sammāsambuddhasāsane.
::

::hangnum
600\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devānaṃ giramaññāya, vācāsabhimudīrihaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, ādibhikkhamadāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
601\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, satthā loke anuttaro;
::

::gathalast
Devasaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
602\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sattāhaṃ abhinikkhamma, bodhiṃ ajjhagamaṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Idaṃ me paṭhamaṃ bhattaṃ, brahmacārissa yāpanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
603\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tusitā hi idhāgantvā, yo me bhikkhaṃ upānayi;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇotha mama bhāsato.
::

::hangnum
604\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassāni {note:tiṃsamatte kappasagasse (syā. ka.)}, devarajjaṃ karissati;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe deve abhibhotvā, tidivaṃ āvasissati.
::

::hangnum
605\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Devalokā cavitvāna, manussattaṃ gamissati;
::

::gathalast
Sahassadhā cakkavattī, tattha rajjaṃ karissati.
::

::hangnum
606\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
607\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tidasā so cavitvāna, manussattaṃ gamissati;
::

::gathalast
Agārā pabbajitvāna, chabbassāni vasissati.
::

::hangnum
608\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tato sattamake vasse, buddho saccaṃ kathessati;
::

::gathalast
Koṇḍañño nāma nāmena, paṭhamaṃ sacchikāhiti’.
::

::hangnum
609\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nikkhantenānupabbajiṃ{pb:T:1.0071}, padhānaṃ sukataṃ mayā;
::

::gathalast
Kilese jhāpanatthāya, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
610\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhigantvāna sabbaññū, buddho loke sadevake;
::

::gathalast
Isināme migāraññe {note:iminā me mahāraññaṃ (syā.), iminā me migāraññaṃ (ka.)}, amatabherimāhani.
::

::hangnum
611\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So {pb:M:1.0054}{pb:V:1.0047} dāni patto amataṃ, santipadamanuttaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
612\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:P:1.0050} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā aññāsikoṇḍañño {note:aññātakoṇḍañño (sī.), aññā koṇḍañño (syā.)} thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Aññāsikoṇḍaññattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 3-8. Piṇḍolabhāradvājattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
613\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sayambhū aggapuggalo;
::

::gathalast
Purato himavantassa, cittakūṭe vasī tadā.
::

::hangnum
614\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhītarūpo tatthāsiṃ, migarājā catukkamo;
::

::gathalast
Tassa saddaṃ suṇitvāna, vikkhambhanti bahujjanā.
::

::hangnum
615\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suphullaṃ padumaṃ gayha, upagacchiṃ narāsabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vuṭṭhitassa samādhimhā, buddhassa abhiropayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
616\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cātuddisaṃ {pb:T:1.0072} namassitvā, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ naruttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, sīhanādaṃ nadiṃ ahaṃ {note:tadā (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
617\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Sakāsane nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
618\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Buddhassa giramaññāya, sabbe devā samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Āgato vadataṃ seṭṭho, dhammaṃ sossāma taṃ mayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
619\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tesaṃ hāsaparetānaṃ, purato lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Mama saddaṃ {note:kammaṃ (?)} pakittesi, dīghadassī mahāmuni’.
::

::hangnum
620\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yenidaṃ padumaṃ dinnaṃ, sīhanādo ca nādito;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
::

::hangnum
621\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ito {pb:M:1.0055} aṭṭhamake kappe, cakkavattī bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampanno catudīpamhi issaro.
::

::hangnum
622\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kārayissati issariyaṃ {note:issaraṃ (syā. ka.)}, mahiyā catusaṭṭhiyā;
::

::gathalast
Padumo nāma nāmena, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
623\.
::

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
624\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Brahmaññā abhinikkhamma, pabbajissati tāvade’.
::

::hangnum
625\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padhānapahitatto so, upasanto nirūpadhi;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.

::hangnum
626\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vijane {pb:T:1.0073} pantaseyyamhi, vāḷamigasamākule;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.

::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā piṇḍolabhāradvājo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Piṇḍolabhāradvājattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 3-9. Khadiravaniyarevatattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
628\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gaṅgā bhāgīrathī nāma, himavantā pabhāvitā;
::

::gathalast
Kutitthe nāviko āsiṃ, orime ca tariṃ {note:orimaṃ ca tare (syā.)} ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
629\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro nāyako, sambuddho dvipaduttamo;
::

::gathalast
Vasī satasahassehi, gaṅgātīramupāgato {note:pubbe mayhaṃ sutaṃ āsi,§‘‘padumuttaranāyako; vasīsatasahassehi, gaṅgāsotaṃ tarissati‘‘; (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
630\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bahū nāvā samānetvā, vaḍḍhakīhi {note:cammakehi (ka.)} susaṅkhataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nāvāya {note:nāvānaṃ (ka.)} chadanaṃ katvā, paṭimāniṃ narāsabhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
631\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āgantvāna {pb:M:1.0056} ca sambuddho, ārūhi tañca nāvakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vārimajjhe ṭhito satthā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
632\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo so tāresi sambuddhaṃ, saṅghañcāpi anāsavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tena cittappasādena, devaloke ramissati.
::

::hangnum
633\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Nibbattissati te byamhaṃ, sukataṃ nāvasaṇṭhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ākāse pupphachadanaṃ, dhārayissati sabbadā.
::

::hangnum
634\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Aṭṭhapaññāsakappamhi{pb:T:1.0074}, tārako {note:tāraṇo (syā.)} nāma khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Cāturanto vijitāvī, cakkavattī bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
635\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sattapaññāsakappamhi{pb:V:1.0049}{pb:P:1.0052}, cammako {note:campako (sī.), cambako (syā.)} nāma khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Uggacchantova sūriyo, jotissati mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
636\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
638\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Agārā nikkhamitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast
Gotamassa bhagavato, sāsane pabbajissati.
::

::hangnum
639\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘So pacchā pabbajitvāna, yuttayogo vipassako;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
::

::hangnum
640\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vīriyaṃ {note:viriyaṃ (sī. syā.)} me dhuradhorayhaṃ, yogakkhemādhivāhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāsane.
::

::hangnum
641\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahasse kataṃ kammaṃ, phalaṃ dassesi me idha;
::

::gathalast
Sumutto saravegova, kilese jhāpayī mama.
::

::hangnum
642\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato maṃ vananirataṃ, disvā lokantagū muni;
::

::gathalast
Vanavāsibhikkhūnaggaṃ, paññapesi mahāmati.
::

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

Itthaṃ {pb:M:1.0057} sudaṃ āyasmā khadiravaniyo revato thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

#### 3-10. Ānandattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
644\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ārāmadvārā {pb:T:1.0075} nikkhamma, padumuttaro mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Vassento amataṃ vuṭṭhiṃ, nibbāpesi mahājanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
645\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassaṃ te dhīrā, chaḷabhiññā mahiddhikā;
::

::gathalast
Parivārenti sambuddhaṃ, chāyāva anapāyinī {note:anupāyinī (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
646\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthikkhandhagato āsiṃ, setacchattaṃ varuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sucārurūpaṃ disvāna, vitti me udapajjatha.
::

::hangnum
647\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Oruyha {pb:V:1.0050} hatthikhandhamhā, upagacchiṃ narāsabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ratanāmayachattaṃ me, buddhaseṭṭhassa dhārayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
648\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama {pb:P:1.0053} saṅkappamaññāya, padumuttaro mahāisi;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ kathaṃ ṭhapayitvāna, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
649\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo so chattamadhāresi, soṇṇālaṅkārabhūsitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇotha mama bhāsato.
::

::hangnum
650\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ito gantvā ayaṃ poso, tusitaṃ āvasissati;
::

::gathalast
Anubhossati sampattiṃ, accharāhi purakkhato.
::

::hangnum
651\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Catuttiṃsatikkhattuñca, devarajjaṃ karissati;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
652\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Aṭṭhapaññāsakkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
653\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi{pb:T:1.0076}, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
654\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sakyānaṃ {pb:M:1.0058} kulaketussa, ñātibandhu bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Ānando nāma nāmena, upaṭṭhāko mahesino.
::

::hangnum
655\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ātāpī nipako cāpi, bāhusacce sukovido;
::

::gathalast
Nivātavutti atthaddho, sabbapāṭhī bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
656\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Padhānapahitatto so, upasanto nirūpadhi;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.
::

::hangnum
657\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Santi āraññakā nāgā, kuñjarā saṭṭhihāyanā;
::

::gathalast
Tidhāpabhinnā mātaṅgā, īsādantā urūḷhavā.
::

::hangnum
658\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Anekasatasahassā, paṇḍitāpi mahiddhikā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe te buddhanāgassa, na hontu paṇidhimhi te’ {note:na honti parivimbhitā (syā.), na honti paṇidhimhi te (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
659\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ādiyāme namassāmi, majjhime atha pacchime;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto sumano, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ upaṭṭhahiṃ.
::

::hangnum
660\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ātāpī nipako cāpi, sampajāno patissato;
::

::gathalast
Sotāpattiphalaṃ patto, sekhabhūmīsu kovido.
::

::hangnum
661\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito {pb:V:1.0051} kappe, yaṃ kammamabhinīhariṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tāhaṃ bhūmimanuppatto, ṭhitā saddhammamācalā {note:ṭhito saddhammamācalo (sī.), ṭhitā saddhā mahapphalā (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
662\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ {pb:P:1.0054} vata me āsi, buddhaseṭṭhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
663\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:T:1.0077} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ānando thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ānandattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Buddho {pb:M:1.0059} paccekabuddho ca, sāriputto ca kolito;
::

::gathalast
Kassapo anuruddho ca, puṇṇatthero upāli ca.
::

::gatha1
Aññāsikoṇḍañño piṇḍolo, revatānandapaṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Chasatāni ca paññāsa, gāthāyo sabbapiṇḍitā.
::

::centre
Apadāne buddhavaggo paṭhamo.
::

### 2. Sīhāsaniyavaggo

#### 1. Sīhāsanadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nibbute {pb:M:1.0060}{pb:V:1.0052}{pb:P:1.0055} lokanāthamhi, siddhatthe dvipaduttame {note:dipaduttame (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Vitthārike pāvacane, bāhujaññamhi sāsane.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, sīhāsanamakāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sīhāsanaṃ karitvāna, pādapīṭhamakāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīhāsane ca vassante, gharaṃ tattha akāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tena cittappasādena, tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āyāmena {pb:T:1.0078} catubbīsa, yojanaṃ āsi {note:yojanāsiṃsu (syā. ka.)} tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Vimānaṃ sukataṃ mayhaṃ, vitthārena catuddasa.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sataṃ {note:satta (syā.)} kaññāsahassāni, parivārenti maṃ sadā;
::

::gathalast
Soṇṇamayañca pallaṅkaṃ, byamhe āsi sunimmitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ, dibbayānaṃ upaṭṭhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pāsādā sivikā ceva, nibbattanti yadicchakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maṇimayā ca pallaṅkā, aññe sāramayā bahū;
::

::gathalast
Nibbattanti mamaṃ sabbe, sīhāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Soṇṇamayā rūpimayā, phalikāveḷuriyāmayā;
::

::gathalast
Pādukā abhirūhāmi, pādapīṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito {note:catunavute ito (sī. syā.)} kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesattatimhito kappe, indanāmā tayo janā;
::

::gathalast
Dvesattatimhito kappe, tayo sumananāmakā.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samasattatito kappe, tayo varuṇanāmakā;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampannā, catudīpamhi issarā.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:M:1.0061}{pb:V:1.0053} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sīhāsanadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sīhāsanadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Ekatthambhikattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Siddhatthassa {pb:T:1.0079}{pb:P:1.0056} bhagavato, mahāpūgagaṇo ahu;
::

::gathalast
Saraṇaṃ gatā ca te buddhaṃ, saddahanti tathāgataṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbe saṅgamma mantetvā, māḷaṃ kubbanti satthuno;
::

::gathalast
Ekatthambhaṃ alabhantā, vicinanti brahāvane.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tehaṃ araññe disvāna, upagamma gaṇaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, paripucchiṃ gaṇaṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te me puṭṭhā viyākaṃsu, sīlavanto upāsakā;
::

::gathalast
Māḷaṃ mayaṃ kattukāmā, ekatthambho na labbhati.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekatthambhaṃ mamaṃ detha, ahaṃ dassāmi satthuno;
::

::gathalast
Āharissāmahaṃ thambhaṃ, appossukkā bhavantu te {note:bhavantu vo (sī.), bhavātha vo (?)}.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te me thambhaṃ pavecchiṃsu, pasannā tuṭṭhamānasā;
::

::gathalast
Tato paṭinivattitvā, agamaṃsu sakaṃ gharaṃ.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aciraṃ gate pūgagaṇe, thambhaṃ ahāsahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, paṭhamaṃ ussapesahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena cittappasādena, vimānaṃ upapajjahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ubbiddhaṃ bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ, sattabhūmaṃ {note:satabhūmaṃ (sī. ka.)} samuggataṃ.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vajjamānāsu bherīsu, paricāremahaṃ sadā;
::

::gathalast
Pañcapaññāsakappamhi, rājā āsiṃ yasodharo.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatthāpi {pb:T:1.0080}{pb:M:1.0062} bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ, sattabhūmaṃ samuggataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kūṭāgāravarūpetaṃ, ekatthambhaṃ manoramaṃ.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekavīsatikappamhi, udeno nāma khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Tatrāpi bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ, sattabhūmaṃ samuggataṃ.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:V:1.0054} yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anubhomi sukhaṃ sabbaṃ {note:sabbametaṃ (syā.)}, ekatthambhassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito {pb:P:1.0057} kappe, yaṃ thambhamadadaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ekatthambhassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekatthambhiko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ekatthambhikattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 3. Nandattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttarassa bhagavato, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Vatthaṃ khomaṃ mayā dinnaṃ, sayambhussa mahesino.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ me buddho viyākāsi, jalajuttaranāmako;
::

::gathalast
‘Iminā vatthadānena, hemavaṇṇo bhavissasi.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Dve {pb:T:1.0081} sampattī anubhotvā, kusalamūlehi codito;
::

::gathalast
Gotamassa bhagavato, kaniṭṭho tvaṃ bhavissasi.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Rāgaratto sukhasīlo, kāmesu gedhamāyuto;
::

::gathalast
Buddhena codito santo, tadā {note:tato (syā.)} tvaṃ pabbajissasi.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Pabbajitvāna tvaṃ tattha, kusalamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissasināsavo’.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satta {pb:M:1.0063} {note:sata (syā.)} kappasahassamhi, caturo ceḷanāmakā;
::

::gathalast
Saṭṭhi kappasahassamhi, upacelā catujjanā.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañca kappasahassamhi, ceḷāva caturo janā;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampannā, catudīpamhi issarā.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nando thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Nandattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 4. Cūḷapanthakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:V:1.0055}{pb:P:1.0058} nāma jino, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Gaṇamhā vūpakaṭṭho so, himavante vasī tadā.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahampi {pb:T:1.0082} himavantamhi, vasāmi assame tadā;
::

::gathalast
Acirāgataṃ mahāvīraṃ, upesiṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pupphacchattaṃ gahetvāna, upagacchiṃ narāsabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samādhiṃ samāpajjantaṃ, antarāyamakāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubho hatthehi paggayha, pupphacchattaṃ adāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paṭiggahesi bhagavā, padumuttaro mahāmuni.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbe devā attamanā, himavantaṃ upenti te;
::

::gathalast
Sādhukāraṃ pavattesuṃ, anumodissati cakkhumā.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna te devā, upagacchuṃ naruttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ākāse dhārayantassa {note:dhārayantaṃ me (ka), dhārayato me (?)}, padumacchattamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satapattachattaṃ paggayha, adāsi tāpaso mama;
::

::gathalast
‘Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Pañcavīsatikappāni, devarajjaṃ karissati;
::

::gathalast
Catuttiṃsatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yaṃ {pb:M:1.0064} yaṃ yoniṃ saṃsarati, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Abbhokāse patiṭṭhantaṃ, padumaṃ dhārayissati’.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena {note:nāmena (sī. ka.)}, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Pakāsite pāvacane, manussattaṃ labhissati;
::

::gathalast
Manomayamhi kāyamhi, uttamo so bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Dve {pb:T:1.0083} bhātaro bhavissanti, ubhopi panthakavhayā;
::

::gathalast
Anubhotvā uttamatthaṃ, jotayissanti sāsanaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sohaṃ {pb:V:1.0056} aṭṭhārasavasso {note:so aṭṭhārasavassohaṃ (syā.)}, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Visesāhaṃ na vindāmi, sakyaputtassa sāsane.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dandhā mayhaṃ gatī āsi, paribhūto pure ahuṃ {note:ahaṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Bhātā ca maṃ paṇāmesi, gaccha dāni sakaṃ gharaṃ.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sohaṃ paṇāmito santo, saṅghārāmassa koṭṭhake;
::

::gathalast
Dummano tattha aṭṭhāsiṃ, sāmaññasmiṃ apekkhavā.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhagavā {pb:P:1.0059} tattha {note:athettha satthā (sī. syā.)} āgacchi, sīsaṃ mayhaṃ parāmasi;
::

::gathalast
Bāhāya maṃ gahetvāna, saṅghārāmaṃ pavesayi.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anukampāya me satthā, adāsi pādapuñchaniṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ suddhaṃ adhiṭṭhehi, ekamantamadhiṭṭhahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthehi tamahaṃ gayha, sariṃ kokanadaṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tattha cittaṃ vimucci me, arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Manomayesu kāyesu, sabbattha pāramiṃ gato;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā cūḷapanthako {note:cullapanthako (sī. syā.)} thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Cūḷapanthakattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Pilindavacchattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nibbute {pb:T:1.0084}{pb:M:1.0065} lokanāthamhi, sumedhe aggapuggale;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto sumano, thūpapūjaṃ akāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye ca khīṇāsavā tattha, chaḷabhiññā mahiddhikā;
::

::gathalast
Tehaṃ tattha samānetvā, saṅghabhattaṃ akāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sumedhassa bhagavato, upaṭṭhāko tadā ahu;
::

::gathalast
Sumedho nāma nāmena, anumodittha so tadā.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena cittappasādena, vimānaṃ upapajjahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷāsītisahassāni, accharāyo ramiṃsu me.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mameva {pb:V:1.0057} anuvattanti, sabbakāmehi tā sadā;
::

::gathalast
Aññe deve abhibhomi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcavīsatikappamhi, varuṇo nāma khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Visuddhabhojano {note:susuddhabhojano (sī.)} āsiṃ, cakkavattī ahaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na te bījaṃ pavapanti, napi nīyanti naṅgalā;
::

::gathalast
Akaṭṭhapākimaṃ sāliṃ, paribhuñjanti mānusā.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha {pb:P:1.0060} rajjaṃ karitvāna, devattaṃ puna gacchahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tadāpi edisā mayhaṃ, nibbattā bhogasampadā.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na maṃ mittā amittā vā, hiṃsanti sabbapāṇino;
::

::gathalast
Sabbesampi piyo homi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi{pb:T:1.0085}, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, gandhālepassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imasmiṃ bhaddake kappe, eko āsiṃ janādhipo;
::

::gathalast
Mahānubhāvo rājāhaṃ {note:rājīsi (syā. ka.)}, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sohaṃ pañcasu sīlesu, ṭhapetvā janataṃ bahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pāpetvā sugatiṃyeva, devatānaṃ piyo ahuṃ.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:M:1.0066} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast

#### 6. Rāhulattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttarassa bhagavato, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khīṇāsavasahassehi, parikiṇṇo mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Upāgami gandhakuṭiṃ, dvipadindo {note:dipadindo (sī. syā.)} narāsabho.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Virocento {note:virocayaṃ (syā.)} gandhakuṭiṃ, devadevo narāsabho;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satthā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yenāyaṃ {pb:T:1.0086}{pb:V:1.0058} jotitā seyyā, ādāsova susanthato;

::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Soṇṇamayā rūpimayā, atho veḷuriyāmayā;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Catusaṭṭhikkhattuṃ {pb:P:1.0061} devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati;

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ekavīsatikappamhi, vimalo nāma khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Cāturanto vijitāvī, cakkavattī bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Nagaraṃ reṇuvatī nāma, iṭṭhakāhi sumāpitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āyāmato tīṇi sataṃ, caturassasamāyutaṃ.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sudassano nāma pāsādo, vissakammena māpito {note:visukammena§māpito (ka.), vissakammena nimmito (sī.)};

::gathalast
Kūṭāgāravarūpeto, sattaratanabhūsito.

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Dasasaddāvivittaṃ {pb:M:1.0067} taṃ {note:avivittaṃ (sī.)}, vijjādharasamākulaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sudassanaṃva nagaraṃ, devatānaṃ bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Pabhā niggacchate tassa, uggacchanteva sūriye;
::

::gathalast
Virocessati taṃ niccaṃ, samantā aṭṭhayojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tusitā so cavitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast
Gotamassa bhagavato, atrajo so bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sace {pb:T:1.0087} vaseyya {note:sacā’vaseyya (?)} agāraṃ, cakkavattī bhaveyya so;
::

::gathalast
Aṭṭhānametaṃ yaṃ tādī, agāre ratimajjhagā.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Nikkhamitvā agāramhā, pabbajissati subbato;
::

::gathalast
Rāhulo nāma nāmena, arahā so bhavissati’.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kikīva aṇḍaṃ rakkheyya, cāmarī viya vāladhiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nipako sīlasampanno, mamaṃ rakkhi mahāmuni {note:evaṃ rakkhiṃ mahāmuni (sī. ka.), mamaṃ dakkhi mahāmuni (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassāhaṃ dhammamaññāya, vihāsiṃ sāsane rato;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:V:1.0059} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā rāhulo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

#### 7. Upasenavaṅgantaputtattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
86\.

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaraṃ {pb:P:1.0062} bhagavantaṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kaṇikārapupphaṃ {pb:M:1.0068} {note:kaṇikāraṃ pupphitaṃ (sī. syā.)} disvā, vaṇṭe chetvānahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Alaṅkaritvā chattamhi, buddhassa abhiropayiṃ.

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piṇḍapātañca {pb:T:1.0088} pādāsiṃ, paramannaṃ subhojanaṃ;

::gathalast

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena cittappasādena, sampattimanubhossasi;

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekavīsatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati {note:yaṃ vadanti sumedhoti, bhūripaññaṃ sumedhasaṃ; kappeto satasahasse, esa buddho bhavissati; (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāsane dibbamānamhi, manussattaṃ gamissati;
::

::gathalast
Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upasenoti nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako;
::

::gathalast
{note:idaṃ pādadvayaṃ theragāthāaṭṭhakathāyameva dissati} Samantapāsādikattā, aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapessati
::

{note:idaṃ pādadvayaṃ theragāthāaṭṭhakathāyameva dissati}.

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Carimaṃ vattate mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, jetvā māraṃ savāhanaṃ {note:savāhiniṃ (?)}.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ {pb:V:1.0060} sudaṃ āyasmā upaseno vaṅgantaputto thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Upasenavaṅgantaputtattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

::centre
Tatiyabhāṇavāraṃ.
::

#### 8. Raṭṭhapālattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttarassa {pb:T:1.0089}{pb:M:1.0069}{pb:P:1.0063} bhagavato, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Varanāgo mayā dinno, īsādanto urūḷhavā.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Setacchatto pasobhito, sakappano sahatthipo;
::

::gathalast
Agghāpetvāna taṃ sabbaṃ, saṅghārāmaṃ akārayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catupaññāsasahassāni, pāsāde kārayiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mahoghadānaṃ {note:mahābhattaṃ (sī.), mahoghañca (ka.), mahādānaṃ (?)} karitvāna, niyyādesiṃ mahesino.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anumodi mahāvīro, sayambhū aggapuggalo;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe jane hāsayanto, desesi amataṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ me buddho viyākāsi, jalajuttaranāmako;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Catupaññāsasahassāni, pāsāde kārayī ayaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Aṭṭhārasasahassāni, kūṭāgārā bhavissare;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Paññāsakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘So pacchā pabbajitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
108\.

#### 9. Sopākattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
113\.

::

::gathalast

114\.

::gatha1
‘‘Pupphāsane nisīditvā, siddhattho lokanāyako;

::gathalast

115\.

::gatha1
‘‘‘Aniccā vata saṅkhārā, uppādavayadhammino;
::

::gathalast

116\.

::gatha1

::hangnum

::hangnum
118\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
119\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
120\.

::gathalast

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Sīhāsanī {pb:M:1.0073} ekathambhī, nando ca cūḷapanthako;
::

::gathalast
Pilindarāhulo ceva, vaṅganto raṭṭhapālako.
::

::gatha1
Sopāko maṅgalo ceva, daseva dutiye vagge;
::

::gathalast
Satañca aṭṭhatiṃsa ca, gāthā cettha pakāsitā.
::

::centre
Sīhāsaniyavaggo dutiyo.

### 3. Subhūtivaggo

#### 1. Subhūtittheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre{pb:M:1.0074}{pb:V:1.0064}{pb:P:1.0067}, nisabho nāma pabbato;
::

::gathalast
Assamo sukato mayhaṃ, paṇṇasālā sumāpitā.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kosiyo nāma nāmena, jaṭilo uggatāpano;
::

::gathalast
Ekākiyo {note:ekākiko (ka.)} adutiyo, vasāmi nisabhe tadā.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Phalaṃ mūlañca paṇṇañca, na bhuñjāmi ahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Pavattaṃva supātāhaṃ {note:pavattapaṇḍupattāni (sī.)}, upajīvāmi tāvade.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhaṃ {pb:T:1.0095} kopemi ājīvaṃ, cajamānopi jīvitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ārādhemi sakaṃ cittaṃ, vivajjemi anesanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rāgūpasaṃhitaṃ cittaṃ, yadā uppajjate mama;
::

::gathalast
Sayaṃva paccavekkhāmi, ekaggo taṃ damemahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Rajjase rajjanīye ca, dussanīye ca dussase;
::

::gathalast
Muyhase mohanīye ca, nikkhamassu vanā tuvaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Visuddhānaṃ ayaṃ vāso, nimmalānaṃ tapassinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mā kho visuddhaṃ dūsesi, nikkhamassu vanā tuvaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Agāriko bhavitvāna, yadā puttaṃ {note:sadāyuttaṃ (sī.), yadāyuttaṃ (syā.)}, labhissasi;
::

::gathalast
Ubhopi mā virādhesi, nikkhamassu vanā tuvaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Chavālātaṃ yathā kaṭṭhaṃ, na kvaci kiccakārakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Neva gāme araññe vā, na hi taṃ kaṭṭhasammataṃ.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Chavālātūpamo tvaṃsi, na gihī nāpi saññato;
::

::gathalast
Ubhato muttako ajja, nikkhamassu vanā tuvaṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Siyā nu kho tava etaṃ, ko pajānāti te idaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saddhādhuraṃ vahisi {note:saddhādhuraṃ jahasi (sī.), sīghaṃ dhuraṃ vahisi (syā.)} me, kosajjabahulāya ca.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Jigucchissanti {pb:M:1.0075}{pb:V:1.0065} taṃ viññū, asuciṃ nāgariko yathā;
::

::gathalast
Ākaḍḍhitvāna isayo, codayissanti taṃ sadā.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Taṃ viññū pavadissanti, samatikkantasāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṃvāsaṃ alabhanto hi, kathaṃ jīvihisi {note:jīvissasi (sī.)} tuvaṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tidhāpabhinnaṃ {pb:T:1.0096}{pb:P:1.0068} mātaṅgaṃ, kuñjaraṃ saṭṭhihāyanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Balī nāgo upagantvā, yūthā nīharate gajaṃ.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yūthā vinissaṭo santo, sukhaṃ sātaṃ na vindati;
::

::gathalast
Dukkhito vimano hoti, pajjhāyanto pavedhati.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tatheva jaṭilā tampi, nīharissanti dummatiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tehi tvaṃ nissaṭo santo, sukhaṃ sātaṃ na lacchasi.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Divā vā yadi vā rattiṃ, sokasallasamappito;
::

::gathalast
Ḍayhasi pariḷāhena, gajo yūthāva nissaṭo.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Jātarūpaṃ yathā kūṭaṃ, neva jhāyati {note:yāyati (syā.)} katthaci;
::

::gathalast
Tathā sīlavihīno tvaṃ, na jhāyissasi {note:yārissati (syā.)} katthaci.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Agāraṃ vasamānopi, kathaṃ jīvihisi tuvaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mattikaṃ pettikañcāpi, natthi te nihitaṃ dhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sayaṃ kammaṃ karitvāna, gatte sedaṃ pamocayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ jīvihisi gehe, sādhu te taṃ na ruccati.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Evāhaṃ tattha vāremi, saṃkilesagataṃ manaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nānādhammakathaṃ katvā, pāpā cittaṃ nivārayiṃ’.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ me viharantassa, appamādavihārino;
::

::gathalast
Tiṃsavassasahassāni, vipine me atikkamuṃ.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Appamādarataṃ disvā, uttamatthaṃ gavesakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Padumuttarasambuddho, āgacchi mama santikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Timbarūsakavaṇṇābho{pb:T:1.0097}, appameyyo anūpamo;
::

::gathalast
Rūpenāsadiso buddho, ākāse caṅkamī tadā.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suphullo {pb:M:1.0076} sālarājāva, vijjūvabbhaghanantare;
::

::gathalast
Ñāṇenāsadiso buddho, ākāse caṅkamī tadā.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīharājā {pb:V:1.0066} vasambhīto {note:chambhito (ka.)},
::

Gajarājāva dappito {note:dammito (ka.)}.

::gathalast
Lāsito {note:abhīto (syā.)} byaggharājāva, ākāse caṅkamī tadā.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Siṅgīnikkhasavaṇṇābho, khadiraṅgārasannibho;
::

::gathalast
Maṇi yathā jotiraso, ākāse caṅkamī tadā.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Visuddhakelāsanibho{pb:P:1.0069}, puṇṇamāyeva candimā;
::

::gathalast
Majjhanhikeva {note:majjhantikeva (sabbattha)} sūriyo, ākāse caṅkamī tadā.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvā nabhe caṅkamantaṃ, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
‘Devo nu kho ayaṃ satto, udāhu manujo ayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Na me suto vā diṭṭho vā, mahiyā ediso naro;
::

::gathalast
Api mantapadaṃ atthi, ayaṃ satthā bhavissati’.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna, sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nānāpupphañca gandhañca, sannipātesahaṃ {note:sannipātetvāhaṃ (sī.)} tadā.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pupphāsanaṃ paññapetvā, sādhucittaṃ manoramaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Narasārathinaṃ aggaṃ, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Idaṃ me āsanaṃ vīra, paññattaṃ tavanucchavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Hāsayanto mamaṃ cittaṃ, nisīda kusumāsane’.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nisīdi {pb:T:1.0098} tattha bhagavā, asambhītova {note:achambhitova (ka.)} kesarī;
::

::gathalast
Sattarattindivaṃ buddho, pavare kusumāsane.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Namassamāno aṭṭhāsiṃ, sattarattindivaṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Vuṭṭhahitvā samādhimhā, satthā loke anuttaro;
::

::gathalast
Mama kammaṃ pakittento, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Bhāvehi buddhānussatiṃ, bhāvanānamanuttaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Imaṃ satiṃ bhāvayitvā, pūrayissasi mānasaṃ.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassāni, devaloke ramissasi;
::

::gatha2
Asītikkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjaṃ karissasi;
::

::gathalast
Sahassakkhattuṃ cakkavattī, rājā raṭṭhe bhavissasi.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Padesarajjaṃ {pb:M:1.0077} vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anubhossasi taṃ sabbaṃ, buddhānussatiyā phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Bhavābhave {pb:V:1.0067} saṃsaranto, mahābhogaṃ labhissasi;
::

::gathalast
Bhoge te ūnatā natthi, buddhānussatiyā phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Asītikoṭiṃ chaḍḍetvā, dāse kammakare bahū;
::

::gathalast
Gotamassa bhagavato, sāsane pabbajissasi.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ārādhayitvā sambuddhaṃ, gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Subhūti nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Bhikkhusaṅghe {pb:T:1.0099}{pb:P:1.0070} nisīditvā, dakkhiṇeyyaguṇamhi taṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tathāraṇavihāre ca, dvīsu agge ṭhapessati’.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho, jalajuttamanāmako;
::

::gathalast
Nabhaṃ abbhuggamī vīro, haṃsarājāva ambare.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāsito lokanāthena, namassitvā tathāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sadā bhāvemi mudito, buddhānussatimuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asītikkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anubhomi susampattiṃ, buddhānussatiyā phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavābhave saṃsaranto, mahābhogaṃ labhāmahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhoge me ūnatā natthi, buddhānussatiyā phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhānussatiyā phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:M:1.0078} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā subhūti thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Subhūtittherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Upavānattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:T:1.0100}{pb:V:1.0068} nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Jalitvā aggikkhandhova, sambuddho parinibbuto.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahājanā samāgamma, pūjayitvā tathāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Citaṃ katvāna sukataṃ, sarīraṃ abhiropayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sarīrakiccaṃ katvāna, dhātuṃ tattha samānayuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sadevamānusā sabbe, buddhathūpaṃ akaṃsu te.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭhamā {pb:P:1.0071} kañcanamayā, dutiyāsi maṇīmayā;
::

::gathalast
Tatiyā rūpiyamayā, catutthī phalikāmayā.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tathā {note:tattha (syā. ka.)} pañcamiyā bhūmi {note:nemi (sī.)}, lohitaṅgamayā ahu;
::

::gathalast
Chaṭṭhā masāragallassa, sabbaratanamayūpari.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jaṅghā maṇimayā āsi, vedikā ratanamayā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbasoṇṇamayo thūpo, uddhaṃ yojanamuggato.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devā tattha samāgantvā, ekato mantayuṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Mayampi thūpaṃ kassāma, lokanāthassa tādino.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhātu āveṇikā natthi, sarīraṃ ekapiṇḍitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Imamhi buddhathūpamhi, kassāma kañcukaṃ mayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devā sattahi ratnehi {note:sattaratanehi (sī.)}, aññaṃ vaḍḍhesu yojanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Thūpo dviyojanubbedho, timiraṃ byapahanti so.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāgā {pb:T:1.0101} tattha samāgantvā, ekato mantayuṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Manussā ceva devā ca, buddhathūpaṃ akaṃsu te.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā {pb:M:1.0079} no pamattā assumha {note:assumhā (sī. syā.), āsimhā (?)}, appamattā sadevakā;
::

::gathalast
Mayampi thūpaṃ kassāma, lokanāthassa tādino.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Indanīlaṃ mahānīlaṃ, atho jotirasaṃ maṇiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ekato sannipātetvā, buddhathūpaṃ achādayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbaṃ maṇimayaṃ āsi, tāvatā buddhacetiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tiyojanasamubbiddhaṃ {note:tīṇi yojanamubbiddhaṃ (sī. ka.)}, ālokakaraṇaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Garuḷā {pb:V:1.0069} ca samāgantvā, ekato mantayuṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Manussā devā nāgā ca, buddhathūpaṃ akaṃsu te.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Mā no pamattā assumha, appamattā sadevakā;
::

::gathalast
Mayampi thūpaṃ kassāma, lokanāthassa tādino’.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbaṃ maṇimayaṃ thūpaṃ, akaruṃ te ca kañcukaṃ {note:sabbamaṇimayaṃ thūpe, akaruttarakañcukaṃ (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Yojanaṃ tepi vaḍḍhesuṃ, āyataṃ buddhacetiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catuyojanamubbiddho, buddhathūpo virocati;
::

::gathalast
Obhāseti disā sabbā, sataraṃsīva uggato.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kumbhaṇḍā ca samāgantvā, ekato mantayuṃ tadā;
::

::gatha2
Manussā ceva devā ca, nāgā ca garuḷā tathā.
::

::gathalast
Paccekaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa, akaṃsu thūpamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Mā no pamattā assumha, appamattā sadevakā;
::

::gatha2
Mayampi thūpaṃ kassāma, lokanāthassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Ratanehi chādessāma, āyataṃ buddhacetiyaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yojanaṃ tepi vaḍḍhesuṃ, āyataṃ buddhacetiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pañcayojanamubbiddho, thūpo obhāsate tadā.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yakkhā {pb:P:1.0072} tattha samāgantvā, ekato mantayuṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Manussā devā nāgā ca, garuḷā kumbhaaṇḍakā.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paccekaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa, akaṃsu thūpamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
‘Mā no pamattā assumha, appamattā sadevakā.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Mayampi {pb:T:1.0102}{pb:M:1.0080} thūpaṃ kassāma, lokanāthassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Phalikāhi chādessāma, āyataṃ buddhacetiyaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yojanaṃ tepi vaḍḍhesuṃ, āyataṃ buddhacetiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cha yojanāni ubbiddho, thūpo obhāsate tadā.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gandhabbā ca samāgantvā, ekato mantayuṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
‘Manujā devatā nāgā, garuḷā kumbhayakkhakā.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sabbekaṃsu buddhathūpaṃ, mayamettha akārakā;
::

::gathalast
Mayampi thūpaṃ kassāma, lokanāthassa tādino’.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vediyo {pb:V:1.0070} satta katvāna, chattamāropayiṃsu te;
::

::gathalast
Sabbasoṇṇamayaṃ thūpaṃ, gandhabbā kārayuṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattayojanamubbiddho, thūpo obhāsate tadā;
::

::gathalast
Rattindivā na ñāyanti, āloko hoti {note:ālokā honti (syā. ka.)} sabbadā.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhibhonti {pb:T:1.0103} na tassābhā, candasūrā satārakā;
::

::gathalast
Samantā yojanasate, padīpopi na pajjali.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kālena ye keci, thūpaṃ pūjenti mānusā;
::

::gathalast
Na te thūpamāruhanti, ambare ukkhipanti te.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devehi ṭhapito yakkho, abhisammatanāmako;
::

::gathalast
Dhajaṃ vā pupphadāmaṃ vā, abhiropeti uttari.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na te passanti taṃ yakkhaṃ, dāmaṃ passanti gacchato;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ passitvā gacchantā, sabbe gacchanti suggatiṃ.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Viruddhā {note:visaddhā (sī.)} ye pāvacane, pasannā ye ca sāsane;
::

::gathalast
Pāṭiheraṃ daṭṭhukāmā, thūpaṃ pūjenti mānusā.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare haṃsavatiyā, ahosiṃ bhatako {note:varako (syā. ka.)} tadā;
::

::gathalast
Āmoditaṃ janaṃ disvā, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Uḷāro bhagavā heso, yassa dhātudharedisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Imā ca janatā tuṭṭhā, kāraṃ kubbaṃ na tappare {note:kubbantanappakaṃ (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ahampi {pb:M:1.0081} kāraṃ kassāmi, lokanāthassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, bhavissāmi anāgate’.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sudhotaṃ {pb:P:1.0073} rajakenāhaṃ, uttareyyapaṭaṃ mama;
::

::gathalast
Veḷagge ālagetvāna, dhajaṃ ukkhipimambare.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhisammatako gayha, ambarehāsi me dhajaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vāteritaṃ dhajaṃ disvā, bhiyyo hāsaṃ janesahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha {pb:T:1.0104} cittaṃ pasādetvā, samaṇaṃ upasaṅkamiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ bhikkhuṃ abhivādetvā, vipākaṃ pucchahaṃ dhaje.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So me kathesi ānanda, pītisañjananaṃ mama;
::

::gathalast
‘Tassa dhajassa vipākaṃ, anubhossasi sabbadā.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Hatthī {pb:V:1.0071} assā rathā pattī, senā ca caturaṅginī;
::

::gathalast
Parivāressanti taṃ niccaṃ, dhajadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

95\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::gatha1
