#### 3. Tisaraṇagamaniyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare candavatiyā {note:bandhumatiyā (aṭṭha.)}, mātuupaṭṭhāko {note:mātupaṭṭhāyako (sī.), mātupaṭṭhānako (syā.)} ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Andhā mātā pitā mayhaṃ, te posemi ahaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rahogato {pb:T:1.0106} nisīditvā, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Posento mātāpitaro, pabbajjaṃ na labhāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahandhakārapihitā {note:tamandhakārapihitā (syā.)}, tividhaggīhi ḍayhare;
::

::gathalast
Etādise bhave {note:bhaye (sī.)} jāte, natthi koci vināyako.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddho loke samuppanno, dippati {note:dibbati (ka.)} {note:jinasāsanaṃ (sī.)} dāni sāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakkā uddharituṃ attā, puññakāmena jantunā.
::

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uggayha tīṇi saraṇe, paripuṇṇāni gopayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tena kammena sukatena, paṭimokkhāmi duggatiṃ.
::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nisabho {pb:M:1.0083} nāma samaṇo, buddhassa aggasāvako;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ upagantvāna, saraṇagamanaṃ gahiṃ.
::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vassasatasahassāni, āyu vijjati tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Tāvatā saraṇagamanaṃ, paripuṇṇaṃ agopayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Carime vattamānamhi, saraṇaṃ taṃ anussariṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tena kammena sukatena, tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
114\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devalokagato santo, puññakammasamāhito;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ desaṃ {note:yaṃ yaṃ desaṃ (syā.)} upapajjāmi {note:upagacchāmi (sī.)}, aṭṭha hetū labhāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
115\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disāsu {pb:P:1.0075} pūjito homi, tikkhapañño bhavāmahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe devānuvattanti, amitabhogaṃ labhāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
116\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo sabbattha, paṭikanto bhavāmahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mittānaṃ acalo homi, yaso abbhuggato mamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
117\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asītikkhattu {pb:T:1.0107} devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dibbasukhaṃ anubhaviṃ, accharāhi purakkhato.
::

::hangnum
118\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcasattatikkhattuñca{pb:V:1.0073}, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
119\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pacchime bhave sampatte, puññakammasamāhito;
::

::gathalast
Pure sāvatthiyaṃ jāto, mahāsāle suaḍḍhake.
::

::hangnum
120\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagarā nikkhamitvāna, dārakehi purakkhato;
::

::gathalast
Hasakhiḍḍasamaṅgīhaṃ {note:sāhaṃ khiḍḍasamaṅgī (syā.)}, saṅghārāmaṃ upāgamiṃ.
::

::hangnum
121\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatthaddasāsiṃ {note:tatthaddasāhaṃ (ka.)} samaṇaṃ, vippamuttaṃ nirūpadhiṃ;
::

::gathalast
So me dhammamadesesi, saraṇañca adāsi me.
::

::hangnum
122\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sohaṃ sutvāna saraṇaṃ, saraṇaṃ me anussariṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ekāsane nisīditvā, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
124\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
125\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
126\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ {note:atthaṃ (syā.)} vo kathayissāmi, sāmaṃ diṭṭhaṃ padaṃ mama.
::

::hangnum
127\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum

::hangnum

::gathalast

131\.

::

#### 10. Khomadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
184\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare {pb:M:1.0090}{pb:V:1.0079} bandhumatiyā, ahosiṃ vāṇijo tadā;
::

::gathalast
Teneva dāraṃ posemi, ropemi bījasampadaṃ.
::

::hangnum
185\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rathiyaṃ paṭipannassa, vipassissa mahesino;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
186\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito {pb:P:1.0081} kappe, yaṃ khomamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
187\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattarase {note:sattavīse (sī. syā.)} ito kappe, eko sindhavasandhano;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampanno, catudīpamhi issaro.
::

::hangnum
188\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:T:1.0116} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā khomadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Khomadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Susūti upavāno ca, saraṇo sīlagāhako;
::

::gathalast
Annasaṃsāvako khomadāyī ca, daseva tatiye gaṇe;
::

::gatha1
Añjalī khomadāyī ca, daseva tatiye gaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Pañcālīsītisataṃ vuttā, gāthāyo sabbapiṇḍitā.
::

::centre
Subhūtivaggo tatiyo.
::

::centre
Catutthabhāṇavāraṃ.
::

### 4. Kuṇḍadhānavaggo

#### 1. Kuṇḍadhānattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattāhaṃ {pb:M:1.0091}{pb:V:1.0080} paṭisallīnaṃ, sayambhuṃ aggapuggalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto sumano, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ upaṭṭhahiṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vuṭṭhitaṃ kālamaññāya, padumuttaraṃ mahāmuniṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mahantiṃ kadalīkaṇṇiṃ, gahetvā upagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭiggahetvā {pb:T:1.0117} {note:paṭiggahesi (syā. ka.)} bhagavā, sabbaññū {note:taṃ phalaṃ (sī.)} lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Mama cittaṃ pasādento, paribhuñji mahāmuni.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paribhuñjitvā sambuddho, satthavāho anuttaro;
::

::gathalast
Sakāsane nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ye {pb:P:1.0082} ca santi samitāro {note:ye vasanti sametāro (sī.)}, yakkhā imamhi pabbate;
::

::gathalast
Araññe bhūtabhabyāni {note:bhūtagaṇā sabbe (syā.)}, suṇantu vacanaṃ mama’.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo so buddhaṃ upaṭṭhāsi, migarājaṃva kesariṃ {note:migarājāva kesarī (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ekādasañcakkhattuṃ, so {note:soyamekādasakkhattuṃ (sī.)} devarājā bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Catutiṃsatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Akkositvāna samaṇe, sīlavante anāsave;
::

::gathalast
Pāpakammavipākena, nāmadheyyaṃ labhissati {note:bhavissati (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
::

::gathalast
Kuṇḍadhānoti nāmena, sāvako so bhavissati’.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pavivekamanuyutto, jhāyī jhānarato ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tosayitvāna satthāraṃ, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāvakehi {pb:M:1.0092}{pb:V:1.0081} {note:sāvakaggehi (sī.)} parivuto, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, salākaṃ gāhayī jino.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekaṃsaṃ {pb:T:1.0118} cīvaraṃ katvā, vanditvā lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vadataṃ varassa purato, paṭhamaṃ aggahesahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena bhagavā, dasasahassīkampako;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapesi maṃ.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vīriyaṃ me dhuradhorayhaṃ, yogakkhemādhivāhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāsane.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kuṇḍadhāno thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Kuṇḍadhānattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Sāgatattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sobhito {pb:P:1.0083} nāma nāmena, ahosiṃ brāhmaṇo tadā;
::

::gathalast
Purakkhato sasissehi, ārāmaṃ agamāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhagavā tamhi samaye, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato;
::

::gathalast
Ārāmadvārā nikkhamma, aṭṭhāsi purisuttamo.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, dantaṃ dantapurakkhataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye keci pādapā sabbe, mahiyā te virūhare;
::

::gathalast
Buddhimanto {pb:T:1.0119} tathā sattā, ruhanti jinasāsane.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satthavāhosi sappañño, mahesi bahuke jane;
::

::gathalast
Vipathā uddharitvāna, pathaṃ ācikkhase tuvaṃ.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Danto {pb:M:1.0093} dantaparikiṇṇo {note:purakkhato (syā.)}, jhāyī jhānaratehi ca;
::

::gathalast
Ātāpī pahitattehi, upasantehi tādibhi.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Alaṅkato parisāhi, puññañāṇehi sobhati;
::

::gathalast
Pabhā niddhāvate tuyhaṃ, sūriyodayane yathā.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pasannacittaṃ {pb:V:1.0082} disvāna, mahesī padumuttaro;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satthā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo so hāsaṃ janetvāna, mamaṃ kittesi brāhmaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, devaloke ramissati.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tusitā hi cavitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast
Gotamassa bhagavato, sāsane pabbajissati.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, arahattaṃ {note:tuṭṭhahaṭṭhaṃ (syā. ka.)} labhissati;
::

::gathalast
Sāgato nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabbajitvāna kāyena, pāpakammaṃ vivajjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vacīduccaritaṃ hitvā, ājīvaṃ parisodhayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ {pb:P:1.0084} viharamānohaṃ, tejodhātūsu kovido;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:T:1.0120} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sāgato thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sāgatattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Mahākaccānattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaranāthassa, padumaṃ nāma cetiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ratanāmayachattañca, paggayha vāḷabījaniṃ {note:vāḷabījanī (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Buddhassa abhiropesiṃ, lokabandhussa tādino.
::

::hangnum
33\.

::gatha1
‘‘Yāvatā {pb:M:1.0094} devatā bhummā {note:bhūmā (ka.)}, sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tañca sabbaṃ suṇissāma, kathayantassa satthuno;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hemāsane nisīditvā, sayambhū aggapuggalo;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::hangnum

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Manussalokamāgantvā, cakkavattī bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Pabhassaroti nāmena, uggatejo bhavissati.

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Divā vā yadi vā rattiṃ, sataraṃsīva uggato;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘So pacchā pabbajitvāna, arahā hessatināsavo;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Kathayanto ca taṃ pañhaṃ, ajjhāsayaṃ {note:ajjhāsaṃ (sī.), abbhāsaṃ (ka.)} pūrayissati’.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aḍḍhe kule abhijāto, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū;
::

::gathalast
Ohāya dhanadhaññāni, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṃkhittenapi pucchante, vitthārena kathemahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ajjhāsayaṃ tesaṃ pūremi, tosemi dvipaduttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1

#### 4. Kāḷudāyittheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa{pb:V:1.0084}, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Addhānaṃ paṭipannassa, carato cārikaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suphullaṃ padumaṃ gayha, uppalaṃ mallikañcahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paramannaṃ gahetvāna, adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paribhuñji mahāvīro, paramannaṃ subhojanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tañca pupphaṃ gahetvāna, janassa sampadassayi.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iṭṭhaṃ kantaṃ {note:kantayidaṃ (syā.)}, piyaṃ loke, jalajaṃ pupphamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sudukkaraṃ kataṃ tena, yo me pupphaṃ adāsidaṃ.

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1

::hangnum
53\.

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Assa {pb:T:1.0123} puññavipākena, dibbagandhasamāyutaṃ;

::gathalast

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Pañcavīsatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati;

56\.

58\.

59\.

#### 5. Mogharājattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthadassī {pb:P:1.0087} tu bhagavā, sayambhū aparājito;

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sissehi samparivuto, gharamhā abhinikkhamiṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1

::hangnum
67\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1

69\.

::gatha1

70\.

71\.

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tuvaṃ cakkhūsi sabbesaṃ, mahātamapanūdano;

::hangnum
73\.

::gatha1

75\.

::gatha1

76\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
77\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
78\.

79\.

::hangnum
80\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum

82\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

#### 6. Adhimuttattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nibbute lokanāthamhi, atthadassīnaruttame;
::

::gathalast
Upaṭṭhahiṃ bhikkhusaṅghaṃ, vippasannena cetasā.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nimantetvā {pb:V:1.0087} bhikkhusaṅghaṃ {note:saṃgharatanaṃ (sī. syā.)}, ujubhūtaṃ samāhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ucchunā maṇḍapaṃ katvā, bhojesiṃ saṅghamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe satte abhibhomi {note:atibhomi (sī. ka.)}, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ucchudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::gathalast
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā adhimutto thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
::

::centre
Adhimuttattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 7. Lasuṇadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre{pb:P:1.0089}, tāpaso āsahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Lasuṇaṃ upajīvāmi, lasuṇaṃ mayhabhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khāriyo {pb:M:1.0099} pūrayitvāna, saṅghārāmamagacchahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, saṅghassa lasuṇaṃ adaṃ.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vipassissa naraggassa, sāsane niratassahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṅghassa lasuṇaṃ datvā, kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, lasuṇaṃ yamadaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, lasuṇassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::gathalast
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā lasuṇadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
::

::centre
Lasuṇadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 8. Āyāgadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
94\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vaḍḍhakīhi {pb:V:1.0088} kathāpetvā, mūlaṃ datvānahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, āyāgaṃ kārapesahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭha kappāni devesu, abbokiṇṇaṃ {note:abbocchinnaṃ (sī.)} vasiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Avasesesu kappesu, vokiṇṇaṃ saṃsariṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāye visaṃ na kamati, satthāni na ca hanti me;
::

::gathalast
Udakehaṃ na miyyāmi, āyāgassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadicchāmi ahaṃ vassaṃ, mahāmegho pavassati;
::

::gathalast
Devāpi me vasaṃ enti, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattaratanasampanno, tisakkhattuṃ ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na maṃ kecāvajānanti, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekattiṃse {pb:P:1.0090} ito kappe, āyāgaṃ yamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, āyāgassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:M:1.0100} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre

#### 9. Dhammacakkikattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
102\.

::gatha1
‘‘Siddhatthassa {pb:T:1.0129} bhagavato, sīhāsanassa sammukhā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cāruvaṇṇova sobhāmi, sayoggabalavāhano;
::

::gathalast
Parivārenti maṃ niccaṃ, anuyantā bahujjanā.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṭṭhitūriyasahassehi, paricāremahaṃ sadā;
::

::gathalast
Parivārena sobhāmi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ cakkaṃ ṭhapayiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, dhammacakkassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito ekādase kappe, aṭṭhāsiṃsu janādhipā;
::

::gathalast
Sahassarājanāmena, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
107\.

::gatha1

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhammacakkiko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Dhammacakkikattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 10. Kapparukkhiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Siddhatthassa bhagavato, thūpaseṭṭhassa sammukhā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:T:1.0130}{pb:M:1.0101} yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sobhayanto mama dvāraṃ, kapparukkho patiṭṭhati.
::

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahañca {pb:P:1.0091} parisā ceva, ye keci mama vassitā {note:nissitā (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Tamhā dussaṃ gahetvāna, nivāsema mayaṃ sadā {note:tadā (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ rukkhaṃ ṭhapayiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito ca sattame kappe, suceḷā aṭṭha khattiyā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kapparukkhiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Kapparukkhiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Kuṇḍadhānavaggo catuttho.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Kuṇḍasāgatakaccānā, udāyī mogharājako;
::

::gatha2
Adhimutto lasuṇado, āyāgī dhammacakkiko;
::

::gathalast
Kapparukkhī ca dasamo, gāthā dvayadasasataṃ {note:gāthāyo dvādasasataṃ (sī.)}.
::

### 5. Upālivaggo

#### 1. Bhāgineyyupālittheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khīṇāsavasahassehi{pb:T:1.0131}{pb:M:1.0102}, parivuto {note:pareto (ka. aṭṭha)} lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Vivekamanuyutto so, gacchate paṭisallituṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajinena nivatthohaṃ, tidaṇḍaparidhārako;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghaparibyūḷhaṃ, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekaṃsaṃ {pb:P:1.0092} ajinaṃ katvā, sire katvāna añjaliṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathāṇḍajā ca saṃsedā, opapātī jalābujā;
::

::gathalast
Kākādipakkhino sabbe, antalikkhacarā sadā.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye keci pāṇabhūtatthi, saññino vā asaññino;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe te tava ñāṇamhi, anto honti samogadhā.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gandhā ca pabbateyyā ye, himavantanaguttame;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe te tava sīlamhi, kalāyapi na yujjare.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mohandhakārapakkhando, ayaṃ loko sadevako;
::

::gathalast
Tava ñāṇamhi jotante, andhakārā vidhaṃsitā.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā atthaṅgate sūriye, honti sattā tamogatā;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ buddhe anuppanne, hoti loko tamogato.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathodayanto ādicco, vinodeti tamaṃ sadā;
::

::gathalast
Tatheva tvaṃ buddhaseṭṭha, viddhaṃsesi tamaṃ sadā.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padhānapahitattosi{pb:T:1.0132}, buddho loke sadevake;
::

::gathalast
Tava kammābhiraddhena, tosesi janataṃ bahuṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ sabbaṃ anumoditvā, padumuttaro mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Nabhaṃ abbhuggamī dhīro, haṃsarājāva ambare.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abbhuggantvāna {pb:V:1.0091} sambuddho, mahesi padumuttaro;
::

::gathalast
Antalikkhe ṭhito satthā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yenidaṃ {pb:M:1.0103} thavitaṃ ñāṇaṃ, opammehi samāyutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Aṭṭhārasañca khattuṃ so, devarājā bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Pathabyā rajjaṃ tisataṃ, vasudhaṃ āvasissati.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Pañcavīsatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tusitā hi cavitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast
Hīnova jātiyā santo, upāli nāma hessati.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘So {pb:P:1.0093} pacchā pabbajitvāna, virājetvāna pāpakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tuṭṭho ca gotamo buddho, sakyaputto mahāyaso;
::

::gathalast
Vinayādhigataṃ tassa, etadagge ṭhapessati’.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhāyāhaṃ {pb:T:1.0133} pabbajito, katakicco anāsavo;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhagavā cānukampī maṃ, vinayehaṃ visārado;
::

::gathalast
Sakakammābhiraddho ca, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṃvuto pātimokkhamhi, indriyesu ca pañcasu;
::

::gathalast
Dhāremi vinayaṃ sabbaṃ, kevalaṃ ratanākaraṃ {note:ratanaggharaṃ (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mamañca guṇamaññāya, satthā loke anuttaro;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā upālithero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Bhāgineyyupālittherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Soṇakoḷivisattheraapadānaṃ

27\.

::hangnum
30\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Imassa {pb:P:1.0094} maccukālamhi, puññakammasamaṅgino;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tena yānenayaṃ poso, devalokaṃ gamissati;
::

::

33\.

34\.

35\.

::

::hangnum
36\.
::

37\.

38\.

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Soḷasitthisahassānaṃ, sabbāsaṃ pavarā ca sā {note:pavarāva yā (syā.), pavarā piyā (?)};
::

::gathalast
Abhijātā khattiyānī, nava putte janessati.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Nava putte janetvāna, khattiyānī marissati;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Okkākaṃ tosayitvāna, varaṃ kaññā labhissati;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Pabbājitā ca te sabbe, gamissanti naguttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Jātibhedabhayā sabbe, bhaginīhi vasissare {note:saṃvasissare (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ekā ca kaññā byādhīhi, bhavissati parikkhatā {note:purakkhatā (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Mā no jāti pabhijjīti, nikhaṇissanti khattiyā.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Khattiyo nīharitvāna, tāya saddhiṃ vasissati;
::

::gathalast
Bhavissati tadā bhedo, okkākakulasambhavo.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tesaṃ {pb:P:1.0095} pajā bhavissanti, koḷiyā nāma jātiyā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tamhā kāyā cavitvāna, devalokaṃ gamissati;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Devalokā {pb:T:1.0136} cavitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Āraddhavīriyo pahitatto, padahaṃ satthu sāsane;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Anantadassī bhagavā, gotamo sakyapuṅgavo;
::

::gathalast
Visesaññū mahāvīro, aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapessati’.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vuṭṭhamhi {pb:M:1.0106} deve caturaṅgulamhi, tiṇe anileritaaṅgaṇamhi;
::

::gathalast
Ṭhatvāna yogassa payuttatādino, tatottariṃ pāramatā na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uttame damathe danto, cittaṃ me supaṇīhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhāro me ohito sabbo, nibbutomhi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṅgīraso {pb:V:1.0094} mahānāgo, abhijātova kesarī;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā soṇo koḷiviso {note:koḷiyavesso (sī. syā.), koṭikaṇṇo (ka.)} thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Soṇakoḷivisattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Kāḷigodhāputtabhaddiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttarasambuddhaṃ{pb:T:1.0137}, mettacittaṃ mahāmuniṃ;
::

::gathalast
Upeti janatā sabbā, sabbalokagganāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattukañca baddhakañca {note:vatthaṃ senāsanañceva (sī.), sattukañca padakañca (sī. aṭṭha.), sattukañca pavākañca (syā.)}, āmisaṃ pānabhojanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dadanti satthuno sabbe, puññakkhette anuttare.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahampi {pb:P:1.0096} dānaṃ dassāmi, devadevassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ nimantetvā, saṅghampi ca anuttaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uyyojitā mayā cete, nimantesuṃ tathāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kevalaṃ bhikkhusaṅghañca, puññakkhettaṃ anuttaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassapallaṅkaṃ, sovaṇṇaṃ gonakatthataṃ;
::

::gatha2
Tūlikāpaṭalikāya, khomakappāsikehi ca;
::

::gathalast
Mahārahaṃ paññāpayiṃ, āsanaṃ buddhayuttakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:M:1.0107} lokavidū, devadevo narāsabho;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghaparibyūḷho, mama dvāramupāgami.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paccuggantvāna sambuddhaṃ, lokanāthaṃ yasassinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto sumano, abhināmayiṃ saṅgharaṃ {note:sakaṃ gharaṃ (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhikkhūnaṃ satasahassaṃ, buddhañca lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto sumano, paramannena tappayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe {pb:T:1.0138} nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yenidaṃ āsanaṃ dinnaṃ, sovaṇṇaṃ gonakatthataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Catusattatikkhattuṃ {pb:V:1.0095} so, devarajjaṃ karissati;
::

::gathalast
Anubhossati sampattiṃ, accharāhi purakkhato.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Padesarajjaṃ sahassaṃ, vasudhaṃ āvasissati;
::

::gathalast
Ekapaññāsakkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sabbāsu bhavayonīsu, uccākulī {note:uccākule (ka.)} bhavissati;
::

::gatha2
So ca pacchā pabbajitvā, sukkamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast
Bhaddiyo nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Vivekamanuyuttomhi, pantasenanivāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Phalañcādhigataṃ sabbaṃ, cattaklesomhi ajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Mama sabbaṃ {note:kammaṃ (?)} abhiññāya, sabbaññū lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ’.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ {pb:P:1.0097} sudaṃ āyasmā bhaddiyo kāḷigodhāya putto thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Bhaddiyassa kāḷigodhāya puttattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 4. Sanniṭṭhāpakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Araññe {pb:T:1.0139}{pb:M:1.0108} kuṭikaṃ katvā, vasāmi pabbatantare;
::

::gathalast
Lābhālābhena santuṭṭho, yasena ayasena ca.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Vasīsatasahassehi {note:bhikkhusatasahassehi (syā.)}, āgacchi mama santikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upāgataṃ mahānāgaṃ {note:mahāvīraṃ (sī.)}, jalajuttamanāmakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tiṇasantharaṃ {note:tiṇattharaṃ (ka.)} paññāpetvā, adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, āmaṇḍaṃ pānīyañcahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Adāsiṃ ujubhūtassa, vippasannena cetasā.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito kappe {note:satasahasse ito kappe (sī.)}, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, āmaṇḍassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekatālīsakappamhi, eko āsiṃ arindamo;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:V:1.0096} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sanniṭṭhāpako {note:sannidhāpako (sī.)} thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sanniṭṭhāpakattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 5. Pañcahatthiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sumedho {pb:T:1.0140} nāma sambuddho, gacchate antarāpaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Okkhittacakkhu {note:khittacakkhu (ka. sī. ka.)} mitabhāṇī, satimā saṃvutindriyo.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañca uppalahatthāni, āveḷatthaṃ ahaṃsu me;
::

::gathalast
Tena buddhaṃ apūjesiṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āropitā {pb:P:1.0098} ca te pupphā, chadanaṃ assu satthuno;
::

::gathalast
Samādhiṃsu {note:saṃsāviṃsu (sī.)} mahānāgaṃ, sissā ācariyaṃ yathā.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi{pb:M:1.0109}, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito vīsakappasate, ahesuṃ pañca khattiyā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1

#### 9. Subhaddattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

102\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nibbāyante ca sambuddhe, dasasahassi kampatha;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Candanaṃ pūrayitvāna, tagarāmallikāhi ca;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, satthā loke anuttaro;
::

::gathalast
Nipannakova sambuddho, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo {pb:T:1.0144} me pacchimake kāle, gandhamālena {note:gandhamallena (syā. ka.) napuṃsakekattaṃ manasikātabbaṃ} chādayi;

::gathalast

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ito cuto ayaṃ poso, tusitakāyaṃ gamissati;
::

::gathalast
Tattha rajjaṃ karitvāna, nimmānaṃ so gamissati.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Eteneva upāyena, datvā mālaṃ {note:malyaṃ (sī.), mallaṃ (syā. ka.)} varuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakakammābhiraddho so, sampattiṃ anubhossati.
::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Punāpi {pb:V:1.0099} tusite kāye, nibbattissatiyaṃ naro;

::gathalast

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sakyaputto mahānāgo, aggo loke sadevake;

110\.

113\.

114\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

116\.

117\.

118\.

119\.

120\.

121\.

::gatha1

133\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
134\.

::gatha1
‘‘‘Dujjayo {pb:V:1.0101} nāma nāmena, hessati manujādhipo;

‘‘‘Vinipātaṃ {pb:M:1.0114} agantvāna, manussattaṃ gamissati;

136\.

::gatha1
‘‘‘Nibbattissati yonimhi, brāhmaṇe so bhavissati;

::hangnum
137\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘So ca pacchā pabbajitvā, aṅgīrasassa sāsane;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
138\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sāmaṇerova so santo, khīṇāsavo bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
::

::hangnum
139\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upaṭṭhahiṃ mahāvīraṃ, aññe ca pesale bahū;
::

::gathalast
Bhātaraṃ me cupaṭṭhāsiṃ, uttamatthassa pattiyā.
::

::hangnum
140\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhātaraṃ me upaṭṭhitvā, dhātuṃ pattamhi ohiya {note:opiya (sī.), ociya (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Sambuddhaṃ upanāmesiṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
141\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubho {pb:P:1.0103} hatthehi paggayha, buddho loke sadevake;
::

::gathalast
Sandassayanto taṃ dhātuṃ, kittayi aggasāvakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
142\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cittañca {pb:T:1.0148} suvimuttaṃ me, saddhā mayhaṃ patiṭṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
143\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidānuppattā, vimokkhāpi ca phassitā {note:paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā cundo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Cundattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Upālivaggo pañcamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Upāli soṇo bhaddiyo, sanniṭṭhāpakahatthiyo;
::

::gatha2
Chadanaṃ seyyacaṅkamaṃ, subhaddo cundasavhayo;
::

::gathalast
Gāthāsataṃ satālīsaṃ {note:ca tālīsaṃ (sī. syā.)}, catasso ca taduttari.
::

### 6. Bījanivaggo

#### 1. Vidhūpanadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa{pb:M:1.0115}{pb:V:1.0102}, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Bījanikā {note:vījanikā (sī. syā.)} mayā dinnā, dvipadindassa tādino.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, paggahetvāna añjaliṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sambuddhamabhivādetvā, pakkamiṃ uttarāmukho.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bījaniṃ {pb:T:1.0149} paggahetvāna, satthā lokagganāyako {note:loke anuttaro (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito santo, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Iminā bījanidānena, cittassa paṇidhīhi {note:cetanāpaṇidhīhi (aññattha)} ca;
::

::gathalast
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, vinipātaṃ na gacchati’.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āraddhavīriyo pahitatto, cetoguṇasamāhito;
::

::gathalast
Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ, arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṭṭhikappasahassamhi, bījamānasanāmakā;
::

::gathalast
Soḷasāsiṃsu rājāno, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:P:1.0104} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vidhūpanadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Vidhūpanadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Sataraṃsittheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubbiddhaṃ selamāruyha, nisīdi purisuttamo;
::

::gathalast
Pabbatassāvidūramhi, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upaviṭṭhaṃ {pb:V:1.0103} mahāvīraṃ, devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Esa {pb:T:1.0150}{pb:M:1.0116} buddho mahāvīro, varadhammappakāsako;
::

::gathalast
Jalati aggikhandhova, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Mahāsamuddova‘kkhubbho {note:’kkhobho (sī. syā.)}, aṇṇavova duruttaro;
::

::gathalast
Migarājāvasambhīto {note:chambhito (ka.)}, dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā’.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, padumuttaranāyako;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satthā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yenāyaṃ {note:yenāhaṃ (ka.)} añjalī dinno, buddhaseṭṭho ca thomito;
::

::gathalast
Tiṃsakappasahassāni, devarajjaṃ karissati.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, aṅgīrasasanāmako;
::

::gathalast
Vivaṭṭacchado {note:vivatthacchaddo (sī.)} sambuddho, uppajjissati tāvade.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
::

::gathalast
Sataraṃsīti nāmena, arahā so bhavissati’.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sataraṃsimhi nāmena, pabhā niddhāvate mama.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā, jhāyī jhānarato ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāsane.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṭṭhikappasahassamhi, caturo rāmanāmakā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:P:1.0105} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ {pb:T:1.0151} sudaṃ āyasmā sataraṃsi thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sataraṃsittherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

26\.

::

::hangnum
27\.

::gatha1

30\.

#### 5. Opavayhattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
34\.

::gatha1
‘‘Devalo nāma nāmena, satthuno aggasāvako;

::gathalast

35\.

::gatha1
‘‘Sapattabhāro bhagavā, ājāneyyo na kappati;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Agghāpetvā vātajavaṃ, sindhavaṃ sīghavāhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Padumuttarabuddhassa, khamanīyamadāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Khamanīyaṃ vātajavaṃ, cittaṃ nibbattate {note:ājānīyā vātajavā, vitti nibbattare (syā.), khamanīyā vātajavā, cittā nibbattare (sī.)} mama.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast
Punapi payirupāseyyaṃ, buddho loke sace bhave.

::hangnum
39\.

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1

::hangnum
41\.

#### 6. Saparivārāsanattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
43\.

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa, piṇḍapātaṃ adāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Gantvā kiliṭṭhakaṃ ṭhānaṃ {note:taṃ bhojanaṭṭhānaṃ (sī.)}, mallikāhi parikkhitaṃ {note:parikkhipiṃ (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamhāsanamhi {pb:V:1.0106} āsīno, buddho lokagganāyako;
::

::gathalast
Akittayi piṇḍapātaṃ, ujubhūto samāhito.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathāpi bhaddake khette, bījaṃ appampi ropitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sammā dhāraṃ pavecchante, phalaṃ toseti kassakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tathevāyaṃ piṇḍapāto, sukhette ropito tayā;
::

::gathalast
Bhave nibbattamānamhi, phalaṃ te {note:nibbattamānaṃ hi, phalato (sī.)} tosayissati {note:tappayissati (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho, jalajuttamanāmako;
::

::gathalast
Piṇḍapātaṃ gahetvāna, pakkāmi uttarāmukho.
::

::hangnum
48\.

::gatha1
‘‘Saṃvuto pātimokkhasmiṃ, indriyesu ca pañcasu;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:T:1.0155}{pb:P:1.0108} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.

#### 8. Dhajadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
57\.

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa, bodhiyā pādaputtame;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Patitapattāni gaṇhitvā, bahiddhā chaḍḍayiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ, avandiṃ bodhimuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
61\.

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, duggatiṃ so na gacchati;
::

::hangnum

::

::gathalast
Gotamassa bhagavato, sāsanebhiramissati’.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padhānapahitattomhi, upasanto nirūpadhi;
::

::gathalast
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāsane.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekapaññāsasahasse, kappe uggatasavhayo {note:savhayā (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Paññāsasatasahasse, khattiyo meghasavhayo {note:khattiyā khemasavhayā (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhajadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Dhajadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Padumattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catusaccaṃ {pb:V:1.0108} pakāsento, varadhammappavattako;
::

::gathalast
Vassate {note:vasseti (?)} amataṃ vuṭṭhiṃ, nibbāpento mahājanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sadhajaṃ {note:sadaṇḍaṃ (sī.)} padumaṃ gayha, aḍḍhakose ṭhito ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Padumuttaramunissa, pahaṭṭho ukkhipimambare.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āgacchante ca padume, abbhuto āsi tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, paggaṇhi vadataṃ varo.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Karaseṭṭhena {pb:T:1.0158} paggayha, jalajaṃ pupphamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satthā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yenidaṃ padumaṃ khittaṃ, sabbaññumhi vināyake {note:sabbaññutamanāyake (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappāni {pb:M:1.0122}{pb:P:1.0110} devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati;
::

::gathalast
Pathabyā rajjaṃ sattasataṃ, vasudhaṃ āvasissati.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tattha pattaṃ gaṇetvāna, cakkavattī bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Ākāsato pupphavuṭṭhi, abhivassissatī tadā.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma nāmena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nikkhamitvāna kucchimhā, sampajāno patissato;
::

::gathalast
Jātiyā pañcavassohaṃ, arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padumo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Padumattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 10. Asanabodhiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jātiyā {pb:T:1.0159}{pb:V:1.0109} sattavassohaṃ, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto sumano, upagacchiṃ naruttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tissassāhaṃ bhagavato, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asano nāmadheyyena, dharaṇīruhapādapo;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pupphitaṃ pādapaṃ disvā, abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakaṃ kammaṃ pakittento, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ upāgamiṃ.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tisso tadā so sambuddho, sayambhū aggapuggalo;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yenāyaṃ {pb:M:1.0123} ropitā bodhi, buddhapūjā ca sakkatā;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappāni devesu, devarajjaṃ karissati;
::

::gathalast
Catusaṭṭhi cakkhattuṃ so, cakkavattī bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tusitā {pb:P:1.0111} hi cavitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast
Dve sampattī anubhotvā, manussatte ramissati.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Padhānapahitatto so, upasanto nirūpadhi;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vivekamanuyuttohaṃ{pb:T:1.0160}, upasanto nirūpadhi;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, bodhiṃ ropesahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catusattatito kappe, daṇḍasenoti vissuto;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesattatimhito kappe, sattāhesuṃ mahīpatī;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṇṇavīsatito {pb:V:1.0110} kappe, puṇṇako nāma khattiyo;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
92\.

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā asanabodhiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Asanabodhiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Bījanivaggo chaṭṭho.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Bījanī sataraṃsī ca, sayanodakivāhiyo;
::

::gatha2
Parivāro padīpañca, dhajo padumapūjako;
::

::gathalast
Bodhi ca dasamo vutto, gāthā dvenavuti tathā.
::

### 7. Sakacintaniyavaggo

#### 1. Sakacintaniyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pavanaṃ {pb:T:1.0161}{pb:M:1.0124}{pb:V:1.0111} kānanaṃ disvā, appasaddamannāvilaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Isīnaṃ anuciṇṇaṃva, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Thūpaṃ katvāna pulinaṃ {note:veḷunā (aṭṭha.), veḷinaṃ (syā.)}, nānāpupphaṃ samokiriṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ, nimmitaṃ abhivandahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattaratanasampanno{pb:P:1.0112}, rājā raṭṭhamhi issaro;
::

::gathalast
Sakakammābhiraddhohaṃ, pupphapūjāyidaṃ {note:thūpapūjāyidaṃ (sī.)} phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pupphapūjāyidaṃ {note:thūpapūjāyidaṃ (sī.)} phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asītikappenantayaso, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampanno, catudīpamhi issaro.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sakacintaniyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sakacintaniyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 8. Ambadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

54\.

::gatha1
‘‘Kapi ahaṃ tadā āsiṃ, himavante naguttame;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Damena uttamenāhaṃ, damitomhi mahesinā;

::hangnum

::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ {pb:T:1.0169} sudaṃ āyasmā ambadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ambadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 9. Sumanattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sumano {pb:M:1.0130}{pb:V:1.0117} nāma nāmena, mālākāro ahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, lokāhutipaṭiggahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubho hatthehi paggayha, sumanaṃ pupphamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Buddhassa abhiropesiṃ, sikhino lokabandhuno.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imāya pupphapūjāya, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekattiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ {note:pupphapūjāyidaṃ (sī.)} phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chabbīsatimhi kappamhi, cattārosuṃ mahāyasā;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampannā, rājāno cakkavattino.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sumano thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sumanattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 10. Pupphacaṅkoṭiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhītarūpaṃ {pb:T:1.0170}{pb:P:1.0118} sīhaṃva, garuḷaggaṃva pakkhinaṃ;

::gathalast
Byagghūsabhaṃva pavaraṃ, abhijātaṃva kesariṃ.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sikhiṃ tilokasaraṇaṃ, anejaṃ aparājitaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Caṅkoṭake {note:caṅgoṭake (sī.)} ṭhapetvāna, anojaṃ pupphamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saha caṅkoṭakeneva, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ samokiriṃ.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena cittappasādena, dvipadinda narāsabha;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekattiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sampuṇṇe {pb:M:1.0131}{pb:V:1.0118} tiṃsakappamhi, devabhūtisanāmakā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pupphacaṅkoṭiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Pupphacaṅkoṭiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Sakacintaniyavaggo sattamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Sakacintī {pb:T:1.0171} avopupphī, sapaccāgamanena ca;
::

::gathalast
Parappasādī bhisado, sucinti vatthadāyako.
::

::gatha1
Ambadāyī ca sumano, pupphacaṅkoṭakīpi ca;
::

::gathalast
Gāthekasattati vuttā, gaṇitā atthadassibhi.
::

### 8. Nāgasamālavaggo

#### 1. Nāgasamālattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Apāṭaliṃ {pb:M:1.0132}{pb:V:1.0119}{pb:P:1.0119} ahaṃ pupphaṃ, ujjhitaṃ sumahāpathe;

::gathalast

2\.

::gathalast

#### 10. Tipadumiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
48\.

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:M:1.0137}{pb:P:1.0124} nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Danto dantaparivuto, nagarā nikkhamī tadā.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare {pb:V:1.0124} haṃsavatiyaṃ, ahosiṃ māliko tadā;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ tattha uttamaṃ toṇi, padmapupphāni {note:uttamaṃ pupphaṃ, tīṇi pupphāni (sī.)} aggahiṃ.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, paṭimaggantarāpaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Saha {note:sohaṃ (sī.)} disvāna sambuddhaṃ, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ me imehi pupphehi, rañño upanitehi me;
::

::gathalast
Gāmaṃ vā gāmakhettaṃ vā, sahassaṃ vā labheyyahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adantadamanaṃ {pb:T:1.0179} vīraṃ, sabbasattasukhāvahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Lokanāthaṃ pūjayitvā, lacchāmi amataṃ dhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna, sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tīṇi lohitake gayha, ākāse ukkhipiṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mayā ukkhittamattamhi, ākāse patthariṃsu te;
::

::gathalast
Dhāriṃsu matthake tattha, uddhaṃvaṇṭā adhomukhā.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye keci manujā disvā, ukkuṭṭhiṃ sampavattayuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Devatā antalikkhamhi, sādhukāraṃ pavattayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Accheraṃ loke uppannaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhassa vāhasā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe dhammaṃ suṇissāma, pupphānaṃ vāhasā mayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Vīthiyañhi ṭhito santo, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo so buddhaṃ apūjesi, rattapadmehi {note:rattapadumehi (sī. syā.)} māṇavo;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassāni, devaloke ramissati;
::

::gathalast
Tiṃsakappāni {note:tiṃsakkhattuñca (syā.)} devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Mahāvitthārikaṃ {pb:M:1.0138} nāma, byamhaṃ hessati tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Tiyojanasatubbiddhaṃ, diyaḍḍhasatavitthataṃ.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Cattārisatasahassāni{pb:P:1.0125}, niyyūhā ca sumāpitā;
::

::gathalast
Kūṭāgāravarūpetā, mahāsayanamaṇḍitā.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Koṭisatasahassiyo{pb:T:1.0180}{pb:V:1.0125}, parivāressanti accharā;
::

::gathalast
Kusalā naccagītassa, vāditepi padakkhiṇā.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Etādise byamhavare, nārīgaṇasamākule;
::

::gathalast
Vassissati pupphavasso, dibbo {note:pada (ka.)} lohitako sadā.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Bhittikhīle nāgadante, dvārabāhāya toraṇe;
::

::gathalast
Cakkamattā lohitakā, olambissanti tāvade.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Pattena pattasañchanne, antobyamhavare imaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Attharitvā pārupitvā, tuvaṭṭissanti tāvade.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Bhavanaṃ parivāretvā, samantā satayojane;
::

::gathalast
Tepi padmā {note:te visuddhā (sī. syā.)} lohitakā, dibbagandhaṃ pavāyare.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Pañcasattatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sampattiyo duve bhutvā, anīti anupaddavo;
::

::gathalast
Sampatte pariyosāne, nibbānaṃ pāpuṇissati’ {note:phassayissati (sī.), passayissati (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sudiṭṭho vata me buddho, vāṇijjaṃ supayojitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Padmāni tīṇi pūjetvā, anubhosiṃ tisampadā {note:anubhūyanti sampadā (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajja me dhammappattassa, vippamuttassa sabbaso;
::

::gathalast
Supupphitaṃ lohitakaṃ, dhārayissati matthake.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama kammaṃ kathentassa, padumuttarasatthuno;
::

::gathalast
Satapāṇasahassānaṃ, dhammābhisamayo ahu.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito {pb:T:1.0181} kappe, yaṃ buddhamabhipūjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, tipadumānidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:M:1.0139} jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:V:1.0126}{pb:P:1.0126} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tipadumiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Tipadumiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Nāgasamālavaggo aṭṭhamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Nāgasamālo padasaññī, saññakāluvadāyako;
::

::gatha2
Ekasaññī tiṇasanthāro, sūcipāṭalipupphiyo;
::

::gathalast
Ṭhitañjalī tipadumī, gāthāyo pañcasattati.
::

### 9. Timiravaggo

#### 1. Timirapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Candabhāgānadītīre{pb:T:1.0182}{pb:M:1.0140}{pb:V:1.0127}, anusotaṃ vajāmahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nisinnaṃ samaṇaṃ disvā, vippasannamanāvilaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā {note:pasādesiṃ (syā.)}, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Tārayissati tiṇṇoyaṃ, dantoyaṃ damayissati.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Assāsissati assattho, santo ca samayissati;
::

::gathalast
Mocayissati mutto ca, nibbāpessati nibbuto.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna, siddhatthassa mahesino;
::

::gathalast
Gahetvā timirapupphaṃ, matthake okiriṃ ahaṃ {note:tadā (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vanditvā satthuno pāde, pakkāmiṃ aparaṃ disaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aciraṃ gatamattaṃ maṃ, migarājā viheṭhayi;
::

::gathalast
Papātamanugacchanto, tattheva papatiṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pupphapūjāyidaṃ {note:buddhapūjāyidaṃ (sī. syā.)} phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chappaññāsamhi {pb:P:1.0127} kappamhi, sattevāsuṃ mahāyasā {note:mahārahā (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā {pb:T:1.0183} sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā timirapupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Timirapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Gatasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jātiyā {pb:M:1.0141}{pb:V:1.0128} sattavassohaṃ, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Avandiṃ satthuno pāde, vippasannena cetasā.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattanaṅgalakīpupphe, ākāse ukkhipiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tissaṃ buddhaṃ samuddissa, anantaguṇasāgaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sugatānugataṃ maggaṃ, pūjetvā haṭṭhamānaso;
::

::gathalast
Añjaliñca {note:añjalissa (ka.)} tadākāsiṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito aṭṭhamake kappe, tayo aggisikhā ahu;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gatasaññako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Gatasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 3. Nipannañjalikattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rukkhamūle {pb:T:1.0184}{pb:P:1.0128} nisinnohaṃ, byādhito paramena ca;
::

::gathalast
Paramakāruññapattomhi, araññe kānane ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anukampaṃ upādāya, tisso satthā upesi maṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sohaṃ nipannako santo, sire katvāna añjaliṃ.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, sabbasattānamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ vandiṃ purisuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, vandanāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
20\.

::gatha1
‘‘Ito {pb:M:1.0142} pañcamake kappe, pañcevāsuṃ mahāsikhā;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gathalast

::hangnum
23\.

::gatha1
‘‘Ahampi {pb:T:1.0185} himavantamhi, ramaṇīyassame isi;
::

::gathalast
Vasāmi appamaññāsu, iddhīsu ca tadā vasī.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pakkhijāto viyākāse, pabbataṃ adhivattayiṃ {note:abhipatthayiṃ (syā.), abhimatthayiṃ (ka.), adhivatthayinti pabbatassa upari gacchintiattho};
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
25\.

::gatha1
‘‘Satta pupphāni gaṇhitvā, matthake okiriṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ālokite {note:ālokito (syā.)} ca vīrena, pakkāmiṃ pācināmukho.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Khāribhāraṃ gahetvāna, pāyāsiṃ {note:pāvisiṃ (sī.)} pabbatantaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajagaro maṃ pīḷesi, ghorarūpo mahabbalo;
::

::gathalast

28\.

::gatha1

#### 10. Padumapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
51\.

‘‘Pokkharavanaṃ {pb:V:1.0132}{pb:P:1.0132} paviṭṭho, bhañjanto padumānihaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tatthaddasaṃ phussaṃ buddhaṃ {note:addasaṃ phussasambuddhaṃ (sī. syā.)}, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇaṃ.

::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabbajitvāna kāyena, manasā saṃvutena ca;
::

::gathalast
Vacīduccaritaṃ hitvā, ājīvaṃ parisodhayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumābhāsanāmā ca, aṭṭhārasa mahīpatī;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:T:1.0190}{pb:M:1.0146} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.

::gathalast
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padumapupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
::

::centre
Padumapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Timiravaggo navamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Timiranaṅgalīpuppha, nippannañjaliko adho;
::

::gatha2
Dve raṃsisaññī phalado, saddasaññī ca secako;
::

::gathalast
Padmapupphī ca gāthāyo, chappaññāsa pakittitā.
::

### 10. Sudhāvaggo

#### 1. Sudhāpiṇḍiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pūjārahe {pb:M:1.0147}{pb:V:1.0133}{pb:P:1.0133} pūjayato, buddhe yadi va sāvake;
::

::gathalast
Papañcasamatikkante, tiṇṇasokapariddave.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te tādise pūjayato, nibbute akutobhaye;
::

::gathalast
Na sakkā puññaṃ saṅkhātuṃ, imettamapi {note:idammattanti (sī.), imetthamapi (ka.)} kenaci.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnamapi dīpānaṃ, issaraṃ yodha kāraye;
::

::gathalast
Ekissā pūjanāyetaṃ, kalaṃ nāgghati soḷasiṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Siddhatthassa {pb:T:1.0191} naraggassa, cetiye phalitantare;
::

::gathalast
Sudhāpiṇḍo mayā dinno, vippasannena cetasā.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, paṭisaṅkhārassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito tiṃsatikappamhi, paṭisaṅkhārasavhayā;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampannā, terasa cakkavattino.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sudhāpiṇḍiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sudhāpiṇḍiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Sucintikattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tissassa lokanāthassa, suddhapīṭhamadāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, buddhassādiccabandhuno.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭhārase {pb:V:1.0134} {note:aṭṭhatiṃse (sī. syā.)} ito kappe, rājā āsiṃ mahāruci;
::

::gathalast
Bhogo ca vipulo āsi, sayanañca anappakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pīṭhaṃ {pb:M:1.0148} buddhassa datvāna, vippasannena cetasā;
::

::gathalast
Anubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ, pubbe sukatamattano.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvenavute {pb:T:1.0192} ito kappe, yaṃ pīṭhamadadiṃ tadā;

::centre

::

::centre
Sudhāvaggo dasamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Sudhā {pb:V:1.0139} sucinti ceḷañca, sūcī ca gandhamāliyo;
::

::gatha2
Tipupphiyo madhusenā, veyyāvacco cupaṭṭhako;
::

::gathalast
Samasaṭṭhi ca gāthāyo, asmiṃ vagge pakittitā.
::

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Buddhavaggo hi paṭhamo, sīhāsani subhūti ca;
::

::gatha2
Kuṇḍadhāno upāli ca, bījanisakacinti ca.
::

::gatha3
Nāgasamālo {pb:T:1.0200} timiro, sudhāvaggena te dasa;
::

::gathalast
Catuddasasatā gāthā, pañcapaññāsameva ca.
::

::centre
Buddhavaggadasakaṃ.
::

::centre
Paṭhamasatakaṃ samattaṃ.
::

### 11. Bhikkhadāyivaggo

#### 1. Bhikkhadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ {pb:M:1.0154}{pb:V:1.0140}{pb:P:1.0140} sambuddhaṃ, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pavarā {note:pavanā (syā.)} abhinikkhantaṃ, vanā nibbanamāgataṃ {note:vānā nibbānamāgataṃ (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ pādāsiṃ, siddhatthassa mahesino;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
3\.
::

‘‘Padenānupadāyantaṃ {note:padenānupadāyanto (sī. syā.)}, nibbāpente mahājanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Uḷārā vitti me jātā, buddhe ādiccabandhune {note:vitti me pāhunā tāva, buddhassādiccabandhuno (syā.)}.

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

Itthaṃ {pb:T:1.0201} sudaṃ āyasmā bhikkhadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

#### 5. Muṭṭhipupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::gatha1
‘‘Sudassanoti nāmena, mālākāro ahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jātipupphaṃ gahetvāna, pūjayiṃ padumuttaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Visuddhacakkhu sumano, dibbacakkhuṃ samajjhagaṃ.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etissā pupphapūjāya, cittassa paṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Soḷasāsiṃsu {pb:T:1.0204} rājāno, devuttarasanāmakā;
::

::gathalast
Chattiṃsamhi ito kappe, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā muṭṭhipupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Muṭṭhipupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 6. Udakapūjakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ {pb:M:1.0157}{pb:V:1.0143} sambuddhaṃ, gacchantaṃ anilañjase;
::

::gathalast
Ghatāsanaṃva jalitaṃ, ādittaṃva hutāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṇinā udakaṃ gayha, ākāse ukkhipiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sampaṭicchi mahāvīro, buddho kāruṇiko isi {note:mayi (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Antalikkhe {pb:P:1.0143} ṭhito satthā, padumuttaranāmako;
::

::gathalast
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Iminā dakadānena, pītiuppādanena ca;
::

::gathalast
Kappasatasahassampi, duggatiṃ nupapajjati’ {note:nupapajjasi (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena dvipadinda, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha;
::

::gathalast
Pattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ, hitvā jayaparājayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sahassarājanāmena{pb:T:1.0205}, tayo te cakkavattino;
::

::gathalast
Pañcasaṭṭhikappasate, cāturantā janādhipā.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā udakapūjako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Udakapūjakattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 7. Naḷamāliyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Tiṇatthare nisinnassa, upasantassa tādino.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Naḷamālaṃ gahetvāna, bandhitvā {note:bījitvā (ka.)} bījaniṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Buddhassa upanāmesiṃ, dvipadindassa tādino.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭiggahetvā sabbaññū, bījaniṃ lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yathā {pb:M:1.0158} me kāyo nibbāti, pariḷāho na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Tatheva tividhaggīhi, cittaṃ tava vimuccatu’.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbe {pb:V:1.0144} devā samāgacchuṃ, ye keci vananissitā;
::

::gathalast
Sossāma buddhavacanaṃ, hāsayantañca dāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nisinno {pb:T:1.0206} bhagavā tattha, devasaṅghapurakkhato;
::

::gathalast
Dāyakaṃ sampahaṃsento, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Iminā bījanidānena, cittassa paṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Subbato nāma nāmena, cakkavattī bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tena {pb:P:1.0144} kammāvasesena, sukkamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast
Māluto nāma nāmena, cakkavattī bhavissati’.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Iminā bījanidānena, sammānavipulena ca;
::

::gathalast
Kappasatasahassampi, duggatiṃ nupapajjati.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, subbatā aṭṭhatiṃsa te;
::

::gathalast
Ekūnatiṃsasahasse, aṭṭha mālutanāmakā.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā naḷamāliyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Naḷamāliyattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

::centre
Sattamabhāṇavāraṃ.
::

#### 8. Āsanupaṭṭhāhakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kānanaṃ vanamogayha, appasaddaṃ nirākulaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sīhāsanaṃ mayā dinnaṃ, atthadassissa tādino.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mālāhatthaṃ {pb:T:1.0207} gahetvāna, katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Satthāraṃ payirupāsitvā, pakkāmiṃ uttarāmukho.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:M:1.0159} kammena dvipadinda, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭhārasakappasate, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, sīhāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito {pb:V:1.0145} sattakappasate, sannibbāpaka {note:sanniṭṭho nāma (ka.)} khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.

#### 9. Biḷālidāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre{pb:P:1.0145}, vasāmi paṇṇasanthare;
::

::gathalast
Ghāsesu gedhamāpanno, seyyasīlo cahaṃ {note:seyasīlovahaṃ (syā. ka.)} tadā.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khaṇantālu {note:khaṇamālu (syā.)} kalambāni, biḷālitakkalāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Kolaṃ bhallātakaṃ billaṃ, āhatvā paṭiyāditaṃ.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:T:1.0208} lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, āgacchi mama santikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upāgataṃ mahānāgaṃ, devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Biḷāliṃ paggahetvāna, pattamhi okiriṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paribhuñji mahāvīro, tosayanto mamaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Paribhuñjitvāna sabbaññū, imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, biḷāliṃ me adā tuvaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, duggatiṃ nupapajjasi’.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Carimaṃ {pb:M:1.0160} vattate mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāsane.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catupaññāsito kappe, sumekhaliyasavhayo;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.

::centre

::

#### 10. Reṇupūjakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ {pb:T:1.0209}{pb:V:1.0146}{pb:P:1.0146} sambuddhaṃ, sataraṃsiṃva bhāṇumaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Obhāsentaṃ disā sabbā, uḷurājaṃva pūritaṃ.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Purakkhataṃ sāvakehi, sāgareheva medaniṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nāgaṃ paggayha reṇūhi, vipassissābhiropayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ reṇumabhiropayiṃ;

::gathalast

65\.

::centre
Reṇupūjakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Bhikkhadāyivaggo ekādasamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Bhikkhadāyī ñāṇasaññī, hatthiyo padapūjako;
::

::gatha2
Muṭṭhipupphī udakado, naḷamāli upaṭṭhako;
::

::gathalast
Biḷālidāyī reṇu ca, gāthāyo cha ca saṭṭhi ca.
::

### 12. Mahāparivāravaggo

#### 1. Mahāparivārakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vipassī {pb:T:1.0210}{pb:M:1.0161}{pb:V:1.0147} nāma bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
::

::gathalast
Aṭṭhasaṭṭhisahassehi, pāvisi bandhumaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagarā abhinikkhamma, agamaṃ dīpacetiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cullāsītisahassāni, yakkhā mayhaṃ upantike;
::

::gathalast
Upaṭṭhahanti sakkaccaṃ {note:maṃ niccaṃ (ka.)}, indaṃva tidasā gaṇā.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavanā {pb:P:1.0147} abhinikkhamma, dussaṃ paggayhahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Sirasā abhivādesiṃ, tañcādāsiṃ mahesino.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aho buddho aho dhammo, aho no satthu sampadā;
::

::gathalast
Buddhassa ānubhāvena, vasudhāyaṃ pakampatha.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tañca acchariyaṃ disvā, abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Buddhe cittaṃ pasādemi, dvipadindamhi tādine.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sohaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, dussaṃ datvāna satthuno;
::

::gathalast
Saraṇañca upāgacchiṃ, sāmacco saparijjano.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito pannarase kappe, soḷasāsuṃ suvāhanā {note:soḷasāsiṃsu vāhano (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:T:1.0211} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahāparivārako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Mahāparivārakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Sumaṅgalattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthadassī {pb:M:1.0162}{pb:V:1.0148} jinavaro, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
::

::gathalast
Vihārā abhinikkhamma, taḷākaṃ upasaṅkami.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nhatvā pitvā ca sambuddho, uttaritvekacīvaro;
::

::gathalast
Aṭṭhāsi bhagavā tattha, vilokento disodisaṃ.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavane upaviṭṭhohaṃ, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, apphoṭesiṃ ahaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sataraṃsiṃva jotantaṃ, pabhāsantaṃva kañcanaṃ {note:iminā pādadvayena purimapādadvayassa purato bhavitabbaṃ};
::

::gathalast
Naccagīte payuttohaṃ, pañcaṅgatūriyamhi ca.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe satte abhibhomi, vipulo hoti me yaso {note:ayañca gāthā pariggahetigāthāya anantarameva ṭhātuṃ yuttā}.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Namo {pb:P:1.0148} te purisājañña, namo te purisuttama;
::

::gathalast
Attānaṃ tosayitvāna, pare tosesi tvaṃ muni.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pariggahe {pb:T:1.0212} {note:pariggayha (sī.), pariggahitvā (syā.), pariggahena (ka.)} nisīditvā, hāsaṃ katvāna subbate;
::

::gathalast
Upaṭṭhahitvā sambuddhaṃ, tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Soḷaseto kappasate, dvinavaekacintitā;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
19\.

::gatha1

::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sumaṅgalo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sumaṅgalattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Saraṇagamaniyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

‘‘Ubhinnaṃ devarājūnaṃ, saṅgāmo samupaṭṭhito;

::gathalast

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:M:1.0163} lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;

‘‘Sabbe {pb:V:1.0149} devā attamanā, nikkhittakavacāvudhā;

::hangnum
23\.

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paduṭṭhacitto {pb:T:1.0213} manujo, ekapāṇaṃ viheṭhayaṃ;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅgāmasīse nāgova, bahū pāṇe viheṭhayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nibbāpetha sakaṃ cittaṃ, mā haññittho punappunaṃ.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvinnampi yakkharājūnaṃ, senā sā vimhitā ahu {note:senāyo vimhitā ahū (sī.), senāpi samitā ahu (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Saraṇañca upāgacchuṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ sutādinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saññāpetvāna {pb:P:1.0149} janataṃ, padamuddhari {note:uddhari pana (sī. syā.)} cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast
Pekkhamānova devehi, pakkāmi uttarāmukho.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭhamaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchiṃ, dvipadindassa tādino;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahādundubhināmā ca, soḷasāsuṃ rathesabhā;
::

::gathalast
Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, rājāno cakkavattino.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

#### 4. Ekāsaniyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Varuṇo nāma nāmena, devarājā ahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nibbute {pb:T:1.0214}{pb:M:1.0164} lokanāthamhi, atthadassīnaruttame;
::

::gathalast
Tūriyaṃ sabbamādāya, agamaṃ bodhimuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vāditena ca naccena, sammatāḷasamāhito;
::

::gathalast
Sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ, upaṭṭhiṃ bodhimuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upaṭṭhahitvā {pb:V:1.0150} taṃ bodhiṃ, dharaṇīruhapādapaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvāna, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakakammābhiraddhohaṃ, pasanno bodhimuttame;
::

::gathalast
Tena cittappasādena, nimmānaṃ upapajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṭṭhitūriyasahassāni, parivārenti maṃ sadā;
::

::gathalast
Manussesu ca devesu, vattamānaṃ bhavābhave.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tividhaggī nibbutā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāsane {note:ayañca gāthā paṭisambhidā catassetigāthāya ekasambandhā bhavitaṃ yuttā}.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Subāhū {pb:P:1.0150} nāma nāmena, catuttiṃsāsu khattiyā;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampannā, pañcakappasate ito.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekāsaniyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ekāsaniyattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 5. Suvaṇṇapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vipassī {pb:T:1.0215} nāma bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
::

::gathalast
Nisinno janakāyassa, desesi amataṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassāhaṃ dhammaṃ sutvāna, dvipadindassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Soṇṇapupphāni cattāri, buddhassa abhiropayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvaṇṇacchadanaṃ āsi, yāvatā parisā tadā;
::

::gathalast
Buddhābhā ca suvaṇṇābhā, āloko vipulo ahu.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Udaggacitto {pb:M:1.0165} sumano, vedajāto katañjalī;
::

::gathalast
Vittisañjanano tesaṃ, diṭṭhadhammasukhāvaho.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āyācitvāna sambuddhaṃ, vanditvāna ca subbataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pāmojjaṃ janayitvāna, sakaṃ bhavanupāgamiṃ.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavane upaviṭṭhohaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ anussariṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tena cittappasādena, tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito {pb:V:1.0151} kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Soḷasāsiṃsu rājāno, nemisammatanāmakā;
::

::gathalast
Tetālīse ito kappe, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ {pb:T:1.0216} sudaṃ āyasmā suvaṇṇapupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Suvaṇṇapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 6. Citakapūjakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
49\.

::gatha1
‘‘Vasāmi {pb:P:1.0151} rājāyatane, sāmacco saparijjano;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, citakaṃ agamāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tūriyaṃ tattha vādetvā, gandhamālaṃ samokiriṃ.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Citamhi pūjaṃ katvāna, vanditvā citakaṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavane upaviṭṭhohaṃ, citapūjaṃ anussariṃ;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anubhotvāna sampattiṃ, devesu mānusesu ca;
::

::gathalast
Pattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ, hitvā jayaparājayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
54\.

::gatha1

::hangnum

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā citakapūjako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

#### 7. Buddhasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadā {pb:V:1.0152} vipassī lokaggo, āyusaṅkhāramossaji;
::

::gathalast
Pathavī sampakampittha, medanī jalamekhalā.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Otataṃ vitthataṃ {note:otataṃ vitataṃ (syā.)} mayhaṃ, suvicittavaṭaṃsakaṃ {note:sucicittaṃ papañcakaṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Bhavanampi pakampittha, buddhassa āyusaṅkhaye.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāso {pb:P:1.0152} mayhaṃ samuppanno, bhavane sampakampite;
::

::gathalast
Uppādo {note:uppāto (?)} nu kimatthāya, āloko vipulo ahu.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vessavaṇo idhāgamma, nibbāpesi mahājanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pāṇabhūte {note:pāṇabhutaṃ (syā.), pāṇabhūnaṃ (sī. ka.)} bhayaṃ natthi, ekaggā hotha saṃvutā {note:sagāravā (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aho buddho aho dhammo, aho no satthu sampadā;
::

::gathalast
Yasmiṃ uppajjamānamhi, pathavī {note:paṭhavī (sī. syā.)} sampakampati.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhānubhāvaṃ kittetvā, kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Avasesesu kappesu, kusalaṃ caritaṃ {note:karitaṃ (sī. syā.), kāritaṃ (ka.)} mayā.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito {pb:T:1.0218} kappe, yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito {pb:M:1.0167} cuddasakappamhi, rājā āsiṃ patāpavā;

::gathalast

65\.

::gatha1

::centre

#### 8. Maggasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

::gatha1
‘‘Atthadassimhi sugate, nibbute samanantarā;
::

::gathalast
Yakkhayoniṃ upapajjiṃ, yasaṃ patto cahaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dulladdhaṃ {pb:M:1.0168} vata me āsi, duppabhātaṃ duruṭṭhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ me bhoge vijjamāne, parinibbāyi cakkhumā.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, sāgaro nāma sāvako;
::

::gathalast
Mamuddharitukāmo so, āgacchi mama santikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ nu socasi mā bhāyi, cara dhammaṃ sumedhasa;
::

::gathalast
Anuppadinnā buddhena, sabbesaṃ bījasampadā.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So ce pūjeyya sambuddhaṃ, tiṭṭhantaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhātuṃ sāsapamattampi, nibbutassāpi pūjaye.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Same {pb:T:1.0220} cittappasādamhi, samaṃ puññaṃ mahaggataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā thūpaṃ karitvāna, pūjehi jinadhātuyo.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāgarassa vaco sutvā, buddhathūpaṃ akāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pañcavasse paricariṃ, munino thūpamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:V:1.0154} kammena dvipadinda, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha;
