#### 10. Jātipūjakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jāyantassa {pb:P:1.0154} vipassissa, āloko vipulo ahu;
::

::gathalast
Pathavī ca pakampittha, sasāgarā sapabbatā.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nemittā ca viyākaṃsu, buddho loke bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Aggo ca sabbasattānaṃ, janataṃ uddharissati.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nemittānaṃ {pb:T:1.0221}{pb:M:1.0169} suṇitvāna, jātipūjamakāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Edisā pūjanā natthi, yādisā jātipūjanā.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅkharitvāna {note:saṃharitvāna (sī. syā.), saṅkaritvāna (ka.)}
::

Kusalaṃ, sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.

::gathalast
Jātipūjaṃ karitvāna, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe satte abhibhomi, jātipūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhātiyo maṃ upaṭṭhanti, mama cittavasānugā;
::

::gathalast
Na tā sakkonti kopetuṃ, jātipūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ pūjamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, jātipūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Supāricariyā nāma, catuttiṃsa janādhipā;
::

::gathalast
Ito tatiyakappamhi, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:V:1.0155} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā jātipūjako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Jātipūjakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Mahāparivāravaggo dvādasamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Parivārasumaṅgalā, saraṇāsanapupphiyā;
::

::gatha2
Citapūjī buddhasaññī, maggupaṭṭhānajātinā;
::

::gathalast
Gāthāyo {pb:T:1.0222} navuti vuttā, gaṇitāyo vibhāvihi.
::

### 13. Sereyyavaggo

#### 1. Sereyyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjhāyako {pb:M:1.0170}{pb:V:1.0156}{pb:P:1.0155} mantadharo, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Abbhokāse ṭhito santo, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīhaṃ yathā vanacaraṃ, byaggharājaṃva nittasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tidhāpabhinnamātaṅgaṃ, kuñjaraṃva mahesinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sereyyakaṃ gahetvāna, ākāse ukkhipiṃ {note:nikkhipiṃ (ka.)} ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Buddhassa ānubhāvena, parivārenti sabbaso {note:sabbato (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adhiṭṭhahi mahāvīro, sabbaññū lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Samantā pupphacchadanā, okiriṃsu narāsabhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato sā pupphakañcukā, antovaṇṭā bahimukhā;
::

::gathalast
Sattāhaṃ chadanaṃ katvā, tato antaradhāyatha.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tañca acchariyaṃ disvā, abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Buddhe cittaṃ pasādesiṃ, sugate lokanāyake.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena cittappasādena, sukkamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pannarasasahassamhi{pb:T:1.0223}, kappānaṃ pañcavīsati;
::

::gathalast
Vītamalā {note:cittamālā (sī.), vilāmālā (syā.)} samānā ca, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sereyyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sereyyakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Pupphathūpiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre{pb:M:1.0171}{pb:V:1.0157}, kukkuro nāma {note:kukkuṭo nāma (sī.)} pabbato;
::

::gathalast
Vemajjhe tassa vasati, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañca sissasahassāni, parivārenti maṃ sadā;
::

::gathalast
Pubbuṭṭhāyī ca te āsuṃ, mantesu ca visāradā.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddho {pb:P:1.0156} loke samuppanno, taṃ vijānātha no bhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asītibyañjanānassa, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇā.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Byāmappabho jinavaro, ādiccova virocati;
::

::gathalast
Sissānaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Assamā abhinikkhamma, disaṃ pucchati sissake {note:brāhmaṇo (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Yamhi dese mahāvīro, vasati lokanāyako.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāhaṃ disaṃ namassissaṃ, jinaṃ appaṭipuggalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Udaggacitto sumano, pūjesiṃ taṃ tathāgataṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etha {pb:T:1.0224} sissā gamissāma, dakkhissāma tathāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vanditvā satthuno pāde, sossāma jinasāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekāhaṃ abhinikkhamma, byādhiṃ paṭilabhiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Byādhinā pīḷito santo, sālaṃ vāsayituṃ gamiṃ.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbe sisse samānetvā, apucchiṃ te tathāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kīdisaṃ lokanāthassa, guṇaṃ paramabuddhino.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te me puṭṭhā viyākaṃsu, yathā dassāvino tathā;
::

::gathalast
Sakkaccaṃ buddhaseṭṭhaṃ taṃ, desesuṃ {note:dassesuṃ (sī. syā.)} mama sammukhā.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesāhaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pupphehi thūpaṃ katvāna, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te me sarīraṃ jhāpetvā, agamuṃ buddhasantikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, satthāramabhivādayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pupphehi thūpaṃ katvāna, sugatassa mahesino;
::

::gathalast
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cattālīsasahassamhi{pb:M:1.0172}{pb:V:1.0158}, kappe soḷasa khattiyā;
::

::gathalast
Nāmenaggisamā nāma, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vīsakappasahassamhi, rājāno cakkavattino;
::

::gathalast
Ghatāsanasanāmāva, aṭṭhattiṃsa mahīpatī.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ {pb:T:1.0225} sudaṃ āyasmā pupphathūpiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Pupphathūpiyattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 3. Pāyasadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo {pb:P:1.0157} sambuddho, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Pavanā {note:padhāno (ka.)} abhinikkhanto, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato {note:suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ …pe… purakkhataṃ-evaṃ dutiyantavasena sī. syā. potthakesu dissati}.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahaccā {note:sahatthā (syā. ka.)} kaṃsapātiyā, vaḍḍhetvā pāyasaṃ {note:pāyāsaṃ (syā. ka.)} ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āhutiṃ yiṭṭhukāmo so, upanesiṃ baliṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhagavā tamhi samaye, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
::

::gathalast
Caṅkamaṃ susamārūḷho, ambare anilāyane.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tañca acchariyaṃ disvā, abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ṭhapayitvā kaṃsapātiṃ, vipassiṃ abhivādayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tuvaṃ devosi {note:buddhosi (syā.)} sabbaññū, sadeve sahamānuse;
::

::gathalast
Anukampaṃ upādāya, paṭigaṇha mahāmuni.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭiggahesi bhagavā, sabbaññū lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, satthā loke mahāmuni {note:anuttaro (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pāyasassa {note:pāyāsassa (syā. ka.)} idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekatālīsito {pb:M:1.0173} kappe, buddho nāmāsi khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:T:1.0226} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pāyasadāyako {note:pāyāsadāyako (syā. ka.)} thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Pāyasadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 4. Gandhodakiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
35\.

::gatha1
‘‘Nisajja {pb:V:1.0159} pāsādavare, vipassiṃ addasaṃ jinaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāsādassāvidūre ca, gacchati lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
37\.

::gatha1

::hangnum

::hangnum

::gatha1

81\.

::

::gathalast

::gathalast

#### 10. Padumapūjakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre{pb:M:1.0179}, gotamo nāma pabbato;

::gathalast

::

100\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evanti te paṭissutvā, padumaṃ āhariṃsu me;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sisse tadā samānetvā, sādhukaṃ anusāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

103\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
104\.

::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:V:1.0165} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::gathalast

::

::centre
Padumapūjakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Sereyyavaggo terasamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Sereyyako pupphathūpi, pāyaso gandhathomako;
::

::gatha2
Āsani phalasaññī ca, gaṇṭhipadumapupphiyo;
::

::gathalast
Pañcuttarasatā gāthā, gaṇitā atthadassibhi.
::

### 14. Sobhitavaggo

#### 1. Sobhitattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:T:1.0236}{pb:M:1.0180}{pb:V:1.0166} nāma jino, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
::

::gathalast
Mahato janakāyassa, deseti amataṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassāhaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, vācāsabhimudīritaṃ {note:vācāsabhimudīrayiṃ (?)};
::

::gathalast
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, ekaggo āsahaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā {pb:P:1.0164} samuddo udadhīnamaggo, nerū nagānaṃ pavaro siluccayo;
::

::gathalast
Tatheva ye cittavasena vattare, na buddhañāṇassa kalaṃ upenti te.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammavidhiṃ {note:dhamme vidhiṃ (sī.)} ṭhapetvāna, buddho kāruṇiko isi;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo so ñāṇaṃ pakittesi, buddhamhi lokanāyake;
::

::gathalast
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, duggatiṃ na gamissati.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kilese jhāpayitvāna, ekaggo susamāhito;
::

::gathalast
Sobhito nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paññāse {pb:T:1.0237} kappasahasse, sattevāsuṃ yasuggatā {note:samuggatā (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sobhito thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sobhitattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Sudassanattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vinatā {pb:M:1.0181}{pb:V:1.0167} nadiyā {note:vitthatāya nadiyā (syā.)} tīre, pilakkhu {note:pilakkho (sī. theragāthā aṭṭha.)} phalito ahu;
::

::gathalast
Tāhaṃ rukkhaṃ gavesanto, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ketakaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā, vaṇṭe chetvānahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Buddhassa abhiropesiṃ, sikhino lokabandhuno.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yena ñāṇena pattosi, accutaṃ amataṃ padaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ ñāṇaṃ abhipūjemi, buddhaseṭṭha mahāmuni.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ñāṇamhi pūjaṃ katvāna, pilakkhumaddasaṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paṭiladdhomhi taṃ paññaṃ {note:taṃ saññaṃ (syā.), taṃ puññaṃ (ka.)}, ñāṇapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekattiṃse {pb:P:1.0165} ito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ñāṇapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito {pb:T:1.0238} terasakappamhi, dvādasāsuṃ phaluggatā;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahapphalā.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sudassano thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sudassanattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 3. Candanapūjanakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
17\.

‘‘Candabhāgānadītīre, ahosiṃ kinnaro tadā;

::gathalast

::hangnum
18\.

::gatha1
‘‘Atthadassī tu bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;

::gathalast

::hangnum
19\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

21\.

::gathalast

::hangnum
22\.

23\.

::hangnum

::gathalast

#### 4. Pupphacchadaniyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
26\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::gathalast

28\.

::gatha1
‘‘Caṅkamitvāna sambuddho, sabbaññū lokanāyako;

::hangnum

::centre
Sobhitavaggo cuddasamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Sobhitasudassano ca, candano pupphachadano;
::

::gathalast
Raho campakapupphī ca, atthasandassakena ca.
::

::gatha1
Ekapasādī {note:ekaraṃsi (syā.)} sāladado, dasamo phaladāyako;
::

::gathalast
Gāthāyo sattati dve ca, gaṇitāyo vibhāvibhi.
::

### 15. Chattavaggo

#### 1. Atichattiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Parinibbute {pb:T:1.0247}{pb:M:1.0188}{pb:V:1.0173} bhagavati, atthadassīnaruttame;
::

::gathalast
Chattātichattaṃ {note:chattādhichattaṃ (sī.)} kāretvā, thūpamhi abhiropayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kālena kālamāgantvā, namassiṃ lokanāyakaṃ {note:satthu cetiyaṃ (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Pupphacchadanaṃ katvāna, chattamhi abhiropayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattarase kappasate, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Manussattaṃ na gacchāmi, thūpapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā atichattiyo {note:adhichattiyo (sī. syā.)} thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Atichattiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Thambhāropakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nibbute {pb:P:1.0171} lokanāthamhi, dhammadassīnarāsabhe;
::

::gathalast
Āropesiṃ dhajatthambhaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhassa cetiye.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nisseṇiṃ māpayitvāna, thūpaseṭṭhaṃ samāruhiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Jātipupphaṃ gahetvāna, thūpamhi abhiropayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aho {pb:T:1.0248} buddho aho dhammo, aho no satthu sampadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, thūpapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, thūpasīkhasanāmakā;
::

::gathalast
Soḷasāsiṃsu rājāno, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:M:1.0189}{pb:V:1.0174} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā thambhāropako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Thambhāropakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 3. Vedikārakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nibbute lokanāthamhi, piyadassīnaruttame;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto sumano, muttāvedimakāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maṇīhi parivāretvā, akāsiṃ vedimuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vedikāya mahaṃ katvā, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maṇī dhārenti ākāse, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Soḷasito kappasate, maṇippabhāsanāmakā;
::

::gathalast
Chattiṃsāsiṃsu {note:bāttiṃsāsiṃsu (sī. syā.)} rājāno, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:T:1.0249} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vedikārako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

#### 4. Saparivāriyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:P:1.0172} nāma jino, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nibbute ca mahāvīre, thūpo vitthāriko ahu;
::

::gathalast
Dūratova {note:ahorattaṃ (sī.), thūpadattaṃ (syā.)} upaṭṭhenti, dhātugehavaruttame.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, akaṃ candanavedikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dissati thūpakhandho ca {note:dīyati dhūmakkhandho ca (sī.), dīyati dhūpagandho ca (syā.)}, thūpānucchaviko tadā.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhave {pb:M:1.0190} nibbattamānamhi, devatte atha mānuse;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcadasakappasate{pb:V:1.0175}, ito aṭṭha janā ahuṃ;
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1

::

::centre
Chattavaggo pannarasamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Chattaṃ thambho ca vedi ca, parivārumapupphiyo;
::

::gatha2
Anulepo ca maggo ca, phalako ca vaṭaṃsako;
::

::gathalast
Pallaṅkadāyī ca gāthāyo, chappaññāsa pakittitāti.
::

### 16. Bandhujīvakavaggo

#### 1. Bandhujīvakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Candaṃva {pb:T:1.0256}{pb:M:1.0194}{pb:V:1.0179} vimalaṃ suddhaṃ, vippasannamanāvilaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nandībhavaparikkhīṇaṃ, tiṇṇaṃ loke visattikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nibbāpayantaṃ janataṃ, tiṇṇaṃ {note:disvā (?)} tārayataṃ varaṃ {note:tārayataṃ muniṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Muniṃ vanamhi jhāyantaṃ {note:vanasmiṃ jhāyamānaṃ taṃ (sī. syā.)}, ekaggaṃ susamāhitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bandhujīvakapupphāni, lagetvā suttakenahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Buddhassa abhiropayiṃ, sikhino lokabandhuno.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekattiṃse {pb:P:1.0176} ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito sattamake kappe, manujindo mahāyaso;
::

::gathalast
Samantacakkhu nāmāsi, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bandhujīvako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Bandhujīvakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 6. Kadambapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

::

::gatha1
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre{pb:V:1.0182}, kukkuṭo nāma pabbato;
::

::gathalast
Tamhi pabbatapādamhi, satta buddhā vasanti te.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kadambaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā, dīparājaṃva uggataṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, sattāsuṃ pupphanāmakā;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::gathalast
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kadambapupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
::

::centre
Kadambapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

::centre
Bandhujīvakavaggo soḷasamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Bandhujīvo tambapupphī, vīthikakkārupupphiyo;
::

::gatha2
Mandāravo kadambī ca, sūlako nāgapupphiyo;
::

::gathalast
Punnāgo komudī gāthā, chappaññāsa pakittitāti.
::

### 17. Supāricariyavaggo

#### 1. Supāricariyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumo {pb:T:1.0265}{pb:M:1.0201}{pb:V:1.0185} nāma nāmena, dvipadindo narāsabho;
::

::gathalast
Pavanā abhinikkhamma, dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yakkhānaṃ samayo āsi, avidūre mahesino;
::

::gathalast
Yena kiccena sampattā, ajjhāpekkhiṃsu tāvade.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhassa giramaññāya, amatassa ca desanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto sumano, apphoṭetvā upaṭṭhahiṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suciṇṇassa phalaṃ passa, upaṭṭhānassa satthuno;
::

::gathalast
Tiṃsakappasahassesu, duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ūnatiṃse kappasate, samalaṅkatanāmako;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā supāricariyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Supāricariyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

::

::gathalast
Apasaddo ca sambuddhe, pañcaṅgulimadāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ gandhamabhiropayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pañcaṅgulissidaṃ {note:pañcaṅguliyidaṃ (sī.)} phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvesattatimhito {pb:T:1.0273} kappe, rājā āsiṃ sayampabho;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::gathalast
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pañcaṅguliyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
::

::centre
Pañcaṅguliyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Supāricariyavaggo sattarasamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Supāricari kaṇaverī, khajjako desapūjako;
::

::gatha2
Kaṇikāro sappidado, yūthiko dussadāyako;
::

::gathalast
Māḷo ca pañcaṅguliko, catupaññāsa gāthakāti.
::

### 18. Kumudavaggo

#### 1. Kumudamāliyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabbate {pb:T:1.0274}{pb:M:1.0207}{pb:V:1.0191} himavantamhi, mahājātassaro ahu;
::

::gathalast
Tatthajo rakkhaso āsiṃ, ghorarūpo mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kumudaṃ pupphate tattha, cakkamattāni jāyare;
::

::gathalast
Ocināmi ca taṃ pupphaṃ, balino samitiṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthadassī {pb:P:1.0187} tu bhagavā, dvipadindo narāsabho;
::

::gathalast
Pupphasaṅkocitaṃ {note:pupphaṃ saṅkocitaṃ (sī. syā.), pupphaṃ samocitaṃ (?)} disvā, āgacchi mama santikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upāgatañca sambuddhaṃ, devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbañca pupphaṃ paggayha, buddhassa abhiropayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāvatā himavantantā, parisā sā {note:himavantasmiṃ, yāva mālā (syā.)} tadā ahu;
::

::gathalast
Tāvacchadanasampanno, agamāsi tathāgato.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito pannarase kappe, sattāhesuṃ janādhipā;
::

::gathalast
Sahassarathanāmā te, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ {pb:T:1.0275} sudaṃ āyasmā kumudamāliyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Kumudamāliyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 5. Isimuggadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::

::gatha1
‘‘Udentaṃ sataraṃsiṃva, pītaraṃsiṃva {note:sitaraṃsiṃva (sī.)} bhāṇumaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kakudhaṃ vilasantaṃva, padumuttaranāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Isimuggāni pisitvā {note:isisuggāni piṃsetvā (sī.), isimuggaṃ nimantetvā (syā.)}, madhukhudde anīḷake;
::

::gathalast
Pāsādeva ṭhito santo, adāsiṃ lokabandhuno.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭhasatasahassāni, ahesuṃ buddhasāvakā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbesaṃ pattapūrentaṃ {note:pattapūraṃ taṃ (sī.)}, tato cāpi bahuttaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena cittappasādena, sukkamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cattālīsamhi {pb:T:1.0286}{pb:P:1.0194} sahasse, kappānaṃ aṭṭhatiṃsa te;
::

::gathalast
Isimuggasanāmā {note:mahisamantanāmā (syā.)} te, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:M:1.0216} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā isimuggadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Isimuggadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 6. Bodhiupaṭṭhākattheraapadānaṃ

#### 7. Ekacintikattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadā {pb:T:1.0287} devo {note:devā (ka.)} devakāyā, cavate {note:cavanti (ka.)} āyusaṅkhayā;
::

::gathalast
Tayo saddā niccharanti, devānaṃ anumodataṃ.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘Ito bho sugatiṃ gaccha, manussānaṃ sahabyataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Manussabhūto saddhamme, labha saddhaṃ anuttaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sā te saddhā niviṭṭhāssa, mūlajātā patiṭṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Yāvajīvaṃ asaṃhīrā, saddhamme suppavedite.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kāyena {pb:M:1.0217}{pb:P:1.0195} kusalaṃ katvā, vācāya kusalaṃ bahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Manasā kusalaṃ katvā, abyāpajjaṃ {note:abyāpajjhaṃ (syā.), appamāṇaṃ (itivuttake 83)} nirūpadhiṃ.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tato opadhikaṃ puññaṃ, katvā dānena taṃ bahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aññepi macce saddhamme, brahmacariye nivesaya’.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imāya anukampāya, devā devaṃ yadā vidū;
::

::gathalast
Cavantaṃ anumodanti, ehi deva punappunaṃ {note:devapuraṃ puna (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṃvego me {note:saṃviggohaṃ (syā.)} tadā āsi, devasaṅghe samāgate;
::

::gathalast
Kaṃsu nāma ahaṃ yoniṃ, gamissāmi ito cuto.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama {pb:V:1.0201} saṃvegamaññāya, samaṇo bhāvitindriyo;
::

::gathalast
Mamuddharitukāmo so, āgacchi mama santikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sumano nāma nāmena, padumuttarasāvako;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassāhaṃ {pb:T:1.0288} vacanaṃ sutvā, buddhe cittaṃ pasādayiṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum

::gathalast

::

::centre
Kuṭajapupphiyavaggo ekūnavīsatimo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Kuṭajo {pb:T:1.0291} bandhujīvī ca, koṭumbarikahatthiyo;
::

::gatha2
Isimuggo ca bodhi ca, ekacintī tikaṇṇiko;
::

::gathalast
Ekacārī tivaṇṭi ca, gāthā dvāsaṭṭhi kittitāti.

### 20. Tamālapupphiyavaggo

#### 1. Tamālapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cullāsītisahassāni{pb:M:1.0220}{pb:V:1.0204}, thambhā sovaṇṇayā ahū;
::

::gathalast
Devalaṭṭhipaṭibhāgaṃ, vimānaṃ me sunimmitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamālapupphaṃ paggayha, vippasannena cetasā;
::

::gathalast
Buddhassa abhiropayiṃ, sikhino lokabandhuno.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekattiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito vīsatime kappe, candatittoti ekako;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ {pb:T:1.0292} sudaṃ āyasmā tamālapupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Tamālapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
37\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Khīṇāsavasahassehi, āgacchi mama santikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāmojjaṃ {pb:M:1.0224} janayitvāna, phalahattho upāgamiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paṭiggahesi bhagavā, sabbaññū vadataṃ varo.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito {pb:T:1.0297}{pb:V:1.0208}{pb:P:1.0201} kappe, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattapaññāsakappamhi, upanandasanāmako;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tindukadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Tindukadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 8. Muṭṭhipūjakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::

::gatha1

#### 10. Yūthikapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Pavanā nikkhamitvāna, vihāraṃ yāti cakkhumā.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubho hatthehi paggayha, yūthikaṃ pupphamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Buddhassa abhiropayiṃ, mettacittassa tādino.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena cittappasādena, anubhotvāna sampadā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito paññāsakappesu, eko āsiṃ janādhipo;
::

::gathalast
Samittanandano nāma, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.

::gathalast
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā yūthikapupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
::

::centre
Yūthikapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Tamālapupphiyavaggo vīsatimo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ {pb:M:1.0226} –

::gatha1
Tamālatiṇasanthāro{pb:T:1.0300}, khaṇḍaphulli asokiyo;
::

::gatha2
Aṅkolakī kisalayo, tinduko nelapupphiyo;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃkaṇiko yūthiko ca, gāthā paññāsa aṭṭha cāti.
::

Atha {pb:P:1.0203} vagguddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Bhikkhādāyī {pb:V:1.0210} parivāro, sereyyo sobhito tathā;
::

::gathalast
Chattañca bandhujīvī ca, supāricariyopi ca.
::

::gatha1
Kumudo kuṭajo ceva, tamāli dasamo kato;
::

::gathalast
Chasatāni ca gāthāni, chasaṭṭhi ca tatuttari.
::

::centre
Bhikkhāvaggadasakaṃ.
::

::centre
Dutiyasatakaṃ samattaṃ.
::

::gatha2

::gathalast

### 22. Hatthivaggo

#### 1. Hatthidāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Siddhatthassa {pb:T:1.0309}{pb:M:1.0233}{pb:V:1.0217} bhagavato, dvipadindassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Nāgaseṭṭho mayā dinno, īsādanto urūḷhavā.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uttamatthaṃ anubhomi, santipadamanuttaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nāgadānaṃ {note:aggadānaṃ (sī. ka.)} mayā dinnaṃ, sabbalokahitesino.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ nāga {note:dāna (sī. ka.)} madadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, nāgadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭhasattatikappamhi, soḷasāsiṃsu khattiyā;
::

::gathalast
Samantapāsādikā nāma, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā hatthidāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Hatthidāyakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Pānadhidāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āraññikassa isino, cirarattatapassino {note:jhāyino, mettacittatapassino (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Buddhassa {note:dhammassa (syā. ka.)} bhāvitattassa, adāsiṃ pānadhiṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:T:1.0310} kammena dvipadinda, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha;
::

::gathalast
Dibbayānaṃ {note:sabbaṃ yānaṃ (sī.)} anubhomi, pubbakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavute {pb:P:1.0209} ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pānadhissa idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattasattatito {pb:M:1.0234}{pb:V:1.0218} kappe, aṭṭha āsiṃsu khattiyā;
::

::gathalast
Suyānā nāma nāmena, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pānadhidāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Pānadhidāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Saccasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

13\.

::gatha1

14\.

::hangnum
15\.

::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Hatthi pānadhi saccañca, ekasaññi ca raṃsiko;
::

::gatha2
Sandhito tālavaṇṭañca, tathā akkantasaññako;
::

::gathalast
Sappi pāpanivārī ca, catuppaññāsa gāthakāti.

### 23. Ālambaṇadāyakavaggo

1\.

::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, aggisālāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito ca sattame kappe, ekosiṃ aparājito {note:eko āsiṃ narādhipo (syā.)};
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:T:1.0322}{pb:P:1.0216} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā abyādhiko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Abyādhikattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

### 24. Udakāsanavaggo

::gatha2

::gathalast

### 25. Tuvaradāyakavaggo

#### 1. Tuvaradāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.

::

::gathalast
Bharitvā tuvaramādāya {note:bharitvā turavamādāya (ka.), bhajjitaṃ tuvaramādāya (?) ettha tuvaranti muggakalāyasadisaṃ tuvaraṭṭhinti tadaṭṭhakathā; tuvaro dhaññabhedeti sakkatābhidhāne}, saṅghassa adadiṃ ahaṃ.

2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast

::gathalast

::

::centre

#### 2. Nāgakesariyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::gatha1
‘‘Dhanuṃ advejjhaṃ katvāna, vanamajjhogahiṃ ahaṃ;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubho hatthehi paggayha, sire katvāna añjaliṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesattatimhi {pb:T:1.0335} kappamhi {note:sattasattatime kappe (syā.)}, satta kesaranāmakā;
::

::gathalast

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Gāthāyo gaṇitā cettha, ekatālīsameva cāti.

### 27. Padumukkhipavaggo

#### 1. Ākāsukkhipiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ {pb:M:1.0260}{pb:V:1.0244} siddhatthaṃ, gacchantaṃ antarāpaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Jalajagge duve gayha, upāgacchiṃ narāsabhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekañca pupphaṃ pādesu, buddhaseṭṭhassa nikkhipiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ekañca pupphaṃ paggayha, ākāse ukkhipiṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pupphadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito chattiṃsakappamhi, eko āsiṃ mahīpati;
::

::gathalast
Antalikkhakaro nāma, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ākāsukkhipiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ākāsukkhipiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Ukkhipī telacandī ca, dīpado ca biḷālido;
::

::gatha2
Maccho javo saḷalado, rakkhaso taraṇo dasa;
::

::gathalast
Gāthāyo cettha saṅkhātā, tālīsaṃ cekameva cāti.

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ {pb:V:1.0253} sudaṃ āyasmā āluvadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Āluvadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

::

::centre
Suvaṇṇabibbohanavaggo aṭṭhavīsatimo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Suvaṇṇaṃ {pb:T:1.0363} tilamuṭṭhi ca, caṅkoṭabbhañjanañjalī;
::

::gatha2
Potthako citamāluvā, ekapuṇḍarī setunā;
::

::gathalast
Dvecattālīsa gāthāyo, gaṇitāyo vibhāvibhīti.
::

::centre
Ekādasamaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

### 29. Paṇṇadāyakavaggo

#### 4. Saddasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::

::gatha1
‘‘Anuggatamhi ādicce, panādo {note:pasādo (syā. aṭṭha.)} vipulo ahu;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ghosa {note:sadda (sī. syā.)} massosahaṃ {pb:M:1.0278} tattha, na ca passāmi taṃ jinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maraṇañca anuppatto, buddhasaññamanussariṃ.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.

::centre

::centre
Citakapūjakavaggo tiṃsatimo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Citakaṃ {pb:V:1.0265} pārichatto ca, saddagosīsasantharaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Pādo padesaṃ saraṇaṃ, ambo saṃsāvakopi ca;
::

::gathalast
Aṭṭhatālīsa gāthāyo, gaṇitāyo vibhāvibhi.
::

Atha {pb:P:1.0248} vagguddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Kaṇikāro {pb:T:1.0379} hatthidado, ālambaṇudakāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tuvaraṃ thomako ceva, ukkhepaṃ sīsupadhānaṃ.
::

::gatha1
Paṇṇado citapūjī ca, gāthāyo ceva sabbaso;
::

::gathalast
Cattāri ca satānīha, ekapaññāsameva ca.
::

::gatha1
Pañcavīsasatā sabbā, dvāsattati taduttari;
::

::gathalast
Tisataṃ apadānānaṃ, gaṇitā atthadassibhi.
::

::centre
Kaṇikāravaggadasakaṃ.
::

::centre
Tatiyasatakaṃ samattaṃ.
::

### 31. Padumakesaravaggo

#### 1. Padumakesariyattheraapadānaṃ

3\.

::gathalast

#### 9. Buddhasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::

::gatha1
‘‘Udentaṃ {pb:T:1.0386}{pb:P:1.0252} sataraṃsiṃva, pītaraṃsiṃva bhāṇumaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vanantaragataṃ santaṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addasaṃ supinantena, siddhatthaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, sugatiṃ upapajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:M:1.0287} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā buddhasaññako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Buddhasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 10. Pabbhāradāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piyadassino bhagavato, pabbhāro sodhito mayā;
::

::gathalast
Ghaṭakañca upaṭṭhāsiṃ, paribhogāya tādino.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ me buddho viyākāsi, piyadassī mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Sahassakaṇḍo satabheṇḍu {note:satageṇḍu (syā. ka.)}, dhajālu haritāmayo.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nibbattissati {pb:T:1.0387} so yūpo, ratanañca anappakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pabbhāradānaṃ datvāna, kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito bāttiṃsakappamhi, susuddho nāma khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:V:1.0271} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pabbhāradāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Pabbhāradāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Padumakesaravaggo ekatiṃsatimo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Kesaraṃ gandhamannañca, dhammasaññī phalena ca;
::

::gatha2
Pasādārāmadāyī ca, lepako buddhasaññako;
::

::gathalast
Pabbhārado ca gāthāyo, ekapaññāsa kittitā.
::

### 32. Ārakkhadāyakavaggo

2\.

::gathalast

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ārakkhadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

### 33. Umāpupphiyavaggo

#### 1. Umāpupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samāhitaṃ {pb:T:1.0397}{pb:M:1.0295}{pb:V:1.0278} samāpannaṃ, siddhatthamaparājitaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Umāpupphaṃ gahetvāna, buddhassa abhiropayiṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sucittā viya tiṭṭhante, ākāse pupphasantharā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcapaññāsito kappe, eko āsiṃ mahīpati;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.

::centre

#### 2. Pulinapūjakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kakudhaṃ {pb:T:1.0398}{pb:P:1.0259} vilasantaṃva, nisabhājāniyaṃ yathā;
::

::gathalast
Osadhiṃva virocantaṃ, obhāsantaṃ narāsabhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, avandiṃ satthuno ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Satthāraṃ parivaṇṇesiṃ, sakakammena tosayiṃ {note:tosito (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Susuddhaṃ {pb:V:1.0279} pulinaṃ gayha, gatamagge samokiriṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ucchaṅgena gahetvāna, vipassissa mahesino.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:M:1.0296} upaḍḍhapulinaṃ, vippasannena cetasā;
::

::gathalast
Divāvihāre osiñciṃ, dvipadindassa tādino.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, pulinaṃ yamasiñcahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pulinassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pulinapūjako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Pulinapūjakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 7. Nigguṇḍipupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::hangnum
40\.

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ito bho sugatiṃ gaccha, manussānaṃ sahabyataṃ;

::hangnum
41\.

‘‘‘Sā {pb:V:1.0282} te saddhā niviṭṭhāssa, mūlajātā patiṭṭhitā;

42\.

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gatha1
‘‘Imāya anukampāya, devādevaṃ yadā vidū;

::gathalast

::hangnum
45\.

::hangnum
46\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
47\.

::gatha1

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

#### 10. Saparivārachattadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhassa giramaññāya, vācāsabhimudīritaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jahitvā mānusaṃ yoniṃ, dibbaṃ yoniṃ {note:devayoniṃ (sī.), dibbayoniṃ (syā.)} majjhagaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vimānamuttamaṃ mayhaṃ, abbhuggataṃ manoramaṃ.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vimānā {pb:T:1.0409} nikkhamantassa, setacchattaṃ dharīyati;
::

::gathalast
Tadā saññaṃ paṭilabhiṃ, pubbakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devalokā cavitvāna, manussattañca āgamiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Chattiṃsakkhattuṃ cakkavattī, sattakappasatamhito.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamhā kāyā cavitvāna, āgacchiṃ {note:agañchiṃ (?)} tidasaṃ puraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṃsaritvānupubbena, mānusaṃ punarāgamiṃ.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Okkantaṃ mātukucchiṃ maṃ, settacchattaṃ adhārayuṃ;
::

::gathalast
**Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ,** pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sunando nāma nāmena, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū;
::

::gathalast
Phalikaṃ chattamādāya, sāvakaggassa so tadā.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anumodi {pb:M:1.0304} mahāvīro, sāriputto mahākathī;
::

::gathalast
Sutvānumodanaṃ tassa, pubbakammamanussariṃ.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saritvā purimaṃ kammaṃ, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uṭṭhāya āsanā tamhā, sire katvāna añjaliṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, imaṃ vācaṃ udīriyiṃ.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, buddho loke anuttaro;
::

::gathalast
Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa chattaṃ mayā dinnaṃ, vicittaṃ samalaṅkataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ubho hatthehi paggaṇhi, sayambhū aggapuggalo.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aho {pb:T:1.0410}{pb:P:1.0267} buddho aho dhammo, aho no satthusampadā;
::

::gathalast
Ekacchattassa dānena, duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:V:1.0287} jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saparivārachattadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Saparivārachattadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Umāpupphiyavaggo tettiṃsatimo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Umāpupphañca pulinaṃ, hāso yañño nimittako;
::

::gatha2
Saṃsāvako nigguṇḍī ca, sumanaṃ pupphachattako;
::

::gathalast
Saparivārachatto ca, gāthā sattasatuttarāti.
::

### 34. Gandhodakavaggo

#### 1. Gandhadhūpiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Siddhatthassa {pb:T:1.0411}{pb:M:1.0305}{pb:V:1.0288} bhagavato, gandhadhūpaṃ adāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sumanehi paṭicchannaṃ, buddhānucchavikañca taṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāsaṃ, buddhaṃ lokagganāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Indīvaraṃva jalitaṃ, ādittaṃva hutāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Byagghusabhaṃva pavaraṃ, abhijātaṃva kesariṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nisinnaṃ samaṇānaggaṃ, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhataṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvā cittaṃ pasādetvā, paggahetvāna añjaliṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vanditvā satthuno pāde, pakkāmiṃ uttarāmukho.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ gandhamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, gandhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gandhadhūpiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Gandhadhūpiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Udakapūjakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ {pb:T:1.0412} sambuddhaṃ, gacchantaṃ anilañjase;
::

::gathalast
Ghatāsanaṃva jalitaṃ, ādittaṃva hutāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṇinā udakaṃ gayha, ākāse ukkhipiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sampaṭicchi mahāvīro, buddho kāruṇiko isi.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Antalikkhe ṭhito satthā, padumuttaranāmako;
::

::gathalast
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, imaṃ gāthamabhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Iminā {pb:V:1.0289} dakadānena, pītiuppādanena ca;
::

::gathalast
Kappasatasahassampi, duggatiṃ nupapajjasi’.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:M:1.0306} kammena dvipadinda, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha;
::

::gathalast
Pattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ, hitvā jayaparājayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sahassarājanāmena, tayo ca cakkavattino;
::

::gathalast
Pañcasaṭṭhikappasate, cāturantā janādhipā.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā udakapūjako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Udakapūjakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 3. Punnāgapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kānanaṃ {pb:T:1.0413} vanamogayha, vasāmi luddako ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Punnāgaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ anussariṃ.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ pupphaṃ ocinitvāna, sugandhaṃ gandhitaṃ subhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Thūpaṃ katvāna puline, buddhassa abhiropayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekamhi navute kappe, eko āsiṃ tamonudo;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.

#### 4. Ekadussadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare haṃsavatiyā, ahosiṃ tiṇahārako;
::

::gathalast
Tiṇahārena jīvāmi, tena posemi dārake.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:T:1.0414}{pb:M:1.0307} nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Tamandhakāraṃ nāsetvā, uppajji lokanāyako.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sake {pb:V:1.0290} ghare nisīditvā, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
‘Buddho loke samuppanno, deyyadhammo ca natthi me.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Idaṃ me sāṭakaṃ ekaṃ, natthi me koci dāyako;
::

::gathalast
Dukkho nirayasamphasso, ropayissāmi dakkhiṇaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna, sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ekaṃ dussaṃ gahetvāna, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekaṃ dussaṃ daditvāna, ukkuṭṭhiṃ sampavattayiṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Mama dānaṃ pakittento, akā me anumodanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Iminā ekadussena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Kappasatasahassāni, vinipātaṃ na gacchati.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Chattiṃsakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati;
::

::gatha2
Tettiṃsakkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Devaloke manusse vā, saṃsaranto tuvaṃ bhave;
::

::gatha2
Rūpavā guṇasampanno, anavakkantadehavā;
::

::gathalast
Akkhobhaṃ amitaṃ dussaṃ, labhissasi yadicchakaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ {pb:T:1.0415} vatvāna sambuddho, jalajuttamanāmako;
::

::gathalast
Nabhaṃ abbhuggamī dhīro, haṃsarājāva ambare.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
31\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

32\.

33\.

::gathalast

34\.

::gathalast

#### 5. Phusitakampiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vipassī {pb:T:1.0416}{pb:P:1.0268} nāma {note:sabbatthapi evameva dissati}
::

Sambuddho, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho.

::gathalast
Khīṇāsavehi sahito, saṅghārāme vasī tadā.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ārāmadvārā nikkhamma, vipassī {note:sabbatthapi evameva dissati} lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Saha satasahassehi, aṭṭha {note:sahassasatasissehi, aṭṭha (ka.), aṭṭha satasahassehi, saha (?)} khīṇāsavehi so.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajinena nivatthohaṃ, vākacīradharopi ca;
::

::gathalast
Kusumodakamādāya {note:kusumbhodaka… (sī. syā.)}, sambuddhaṃ upasaṅkamiṃ.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, vedajāto katañjalī;
::

::gathalast
Kusumodakamādāya, buddhamabbhukkiriṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sambuddho, jalajuttamanāmako {note:sabbatthapi evameva dissati};
::

::gathalast
Mama kammaṃ pakittetvā, agamā yena patthitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Phusitā {pb:M:1.0309} pañcasahassā, yehi pūjesahaṃ jinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aḍḍhateyyasahassehi, devarajjaṃ akārayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aḍḍhateyyasahassehi, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Avasesena kammena, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devarājā yadā homi {note:ahosiṃ (syā. ka.)}, manujādhipatī yadā {note:tadā (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Tameva nāmadheyyaṃ me, phusito nāma homahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devabhūtassa santassa, athāpi mānusassa vā;
::

::gathalast
Samantā byāmato mayhaṃ, phusitaṃva pavassati.

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Sarīrato mama gandho, aḍḍhakose pavāyati.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantaṃ, puññakammasamaṅginaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

#### 6. Pabhaṅkarattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttarabhagavato, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Vipine cetiyaṃ āsi, vāḷamigasamākule.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:T:1.0418}{pb:M:1.0310} koci visahi gantuṃ, cetiyaṃ abhivandituṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tiṇakaṭṭhalatonaddhaṃ, paluggaṃ āsi cetiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vanakammiko tadā āsiṃ, pitumātumatenahaṃ {note:pitupetāmahenahaṃ (sī.), pitāpetāmahenahaṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Addasaṃ vipine thūpaṃ, luggaṃ tiṇalatākulaṃ.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvānāhaṃ buddhathūpaṃ, garucittaṃ upaṭṭhahiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Buddhaseṭṭhassa thūpoyaṃ, paluggo acchatī vane.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nacchannaṃ nappatirūpaṃ, jānantassa guṇāguṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Buddhathūpaṃ asodhetvā, aññaṃ kammaṃ payojaye.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṇakaṭṭhañca valliñca, sodhayitvāna cetiye;
::

::gathalast
Vanditvā aṭṭha vārāni {note:aṭṭha ṭhānāni (ka.)}, paṭikuṭiko agacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:V:1.0293} kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha me sukataṃ byamhaṃ, sovaṇṇaṃ sapabhassaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṭṭhiyojanamubbiddhaṃ, tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tisatāni ca vārāni, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pañcavīsatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavābhave saṃsaranto, mahābhogaṃ labhāmahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhoge me ūnatā natthi, sodhanāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sivikā {pb:P:1.0270} hatthikhandhena, vipine gacchato mama;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ yaṃ disāhaṃ gacchāmi, saraṇaṃ sampate {note:sijjhate (ka.)} vanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khāṇuṃ {pb:T:1.0419} vā kaṇṭakaṃ vāpi, nāhaṃ passāmi cakkhunā;
::

::gathalast
Puññakammena saṃyutto, sayamevāpanīyare.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuṭṭhaṃ gaṇḍo kilāso ca, apamāro vitacchikā;
::

::gathalast
Daddu kacchu {note:kaṇḍu (syā.)} ca me natthi, sodhanāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññampi {pb:M:1.0311} me acchariyaṃ, buddhathūpassa sodhane {note:buddhathūpamhi sodhite (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Nābhijānāmi me kāye, jātaṃ piḷakabindukaṃ.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññampi me acchariyaṃ, buddhathūpamhi sodhite {note:sabbatthapi evameva dissati, tathā uparipi};
::

::gathalast
Duve bhave saṃsarāmi, devatte atha mānuse.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññampi me acchariyaṃ, buddhathūpamhi sodhite;
::

::gathalast
Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo sabbattha, sappabhāso bhavāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññampi me acchariyaṃ, buddhathūpamhi sodhite;
::

::gathalast
Amanāpaṃ vivajjati, manāpaṃ upatiṭṭhati.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññampi me acchariyaṃ, buddhathūpamhi sodhite;
::

::gathalast
Visuddhaṃ hoti me cittaṃ, ekaggaṃ susamāhitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññampi me acchariyaṃ, buddhathūpamhi sodhite;
::

::gathalast
Ekāsane nisīditvā, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, sodhanāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:V:1.0294} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ {pb:T:1.0420} sudaṃ āyasmā pabhaṅkaro thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Pabhaṅkarattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 7. Tiṇakuṭidāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare bandhumatiyā, ahosiṃ parakammiko;
::

::gathalast
Parakammāyane yutto, parabhattaṃ apassito.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rahogato nisīditvā, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Buddho loke samuppanno, adhikāro ca natthi me.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kālo {pb:P:1.0271} me gatiṃ {note:kālo gatiṃ me (sī. syā.)} sodhetuṃ, khaṇo me paṭipādito;
::

::gathalast
Dukkho nirayasamphasso, apuññānañhi pāṇinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna, kammasāmiṃ upāgamiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ekāhaṃ kammaṃ yācitvā, vipinaṃ pāvisiṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṇakaṭṭhañca {pb:M:1.0312} valliñca, āharitvānahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Tidaṇḍake ṭhapetvāna, akaṃ tiṇakuṭiṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅghassatthāya kuṭikaṃ, niyyādetvāna {note:niyyātetvāna (sī.)} taṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tadaheyeva āgantvā, kammasāmiṃ upāgamiṃ.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tattha me sukataṃ byamhaṃ, kuṭikāya sunimmitaṃ {note:tiṇakuṭikāya nimmitaṃ (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sahassakaṇḍaṃ {pb:T:1.0421} satabheṇḍu, dhajālu haritāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Satasahassaniyyūhā, byamhe pātubhaviṃsu me.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, pāsādo upatiṭṭhati.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhayaṃ vā chambhitattaṃ vā, lomahaṃso na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Tāsaṃ mama na jānāmi, tiṇakuṭikāyidaṃ {note:tiṇakuṭiyidaṃ (ka.)} phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīhabyagghā ca dīpī ca, acchakokataracchakā {note:taracchayo (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Sabbe maṃ parivajjenti, tiṇakuṭikāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sarīsapā {pb:V:1.0295} {note:siriṃsapā (sī. syā.), sariṃsapā (ka.)} ca bhūtā ca, ahī kumbhaṇḍarakkhasā;
::

::gathalast
Tepi maṃ parivajjenti, tiṇakuṭikāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na pāpasupinassāpi, sarāmi dassanaṃ mama;
::

::gathalast
Upaṭṭhitā sati mayhaṃ, tiṇakuṭikāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāyeva tiṇakuṭikāya, anubhotvāna sampadā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1

::

Itthaṃ {pb:T:1.0422} sudaṃ āyasmā tiṇakuṭidāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre

113\.

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhaseṭṭhassa upari, gantuṃ na visahāmahaṃ;

::gathalast

::hangnum
115\.

118\.

122\.

123\.

::hangnum
124\.

#### 10. Ukkhittapadumiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
129\.

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare {pb:P:1.0275} haṃsavatiyā, ahosiṃ māliko tadā;

::hangnum
130\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
131\.
::

::

::gathalast
Mama vuddhiṃ samanvesaṃ, āgacchi mama santikaṃ {note:mama santike (sī.), purisuttamo (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
132\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvānahaṃ devadevaṃ, sayambhuṃ lokanāyakaṃ;

133\.

‘‘Yadi buddho tuvaṃ vīra, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
134\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adhiṭṭhahi mahāvīro, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
::

::gathalast
Buddhassa ānubhāvena, matthake dhārayiṃsu te.
::

::hangnum
135\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
136\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha {pb:M:1.0317}{pb:V:1.0299} me sukataṃ byamhaṃ, satapattanti vuccati;
::

::gathalast
Saṭṭhiyojanamubbiddhaṃ, tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ.
::

::hangnum
137\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sahassakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
138\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ, pubbe sukatamattano.
::

::hangnum
139\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tenevekapadumena, anubhotvāna sampadā;
::

::gathalast
Gotamassa bhagavato, dhammaṃ sacchikariṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
140\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
141\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito {pb:T:1.0428} kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ekapadumassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
142\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:P:1.0276} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ukkhittapadumiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ukkhittapadumiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Gandhodakavaggo catutiṃsatimo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Gandhadhūpo udakañca, punnāga ekadussakā;
::

::gathalast
Phusito ca pabhaṅkaro, kuṭido uttarīyako.
::

::gatha1
Savanī ekapadumī, gāthāyo sabbapiṇḍitā;
::

::gathalast
Ekaṃ gāthāsatañceva, catutālīsameva ca.
::

### 35. Ekapadumiyavaggo

#### 1. Ekapadumiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:T:1.0429}{pb:M:1.0318}{pb:V:1.0300} nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Bhavābhave vibhāvento, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Haṃsarājā tadā homi, dijānaṃ pavaro ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Jātassaraṃ samogayha, kīḷāmi haṃsakīḷitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Jātassarassa upari, āgacchi tāvade jino.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvānahaṃ devadevaṃ, sayambhuṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vaṇṭe chetvāna padumaṃ, satapattaṃ manoramaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mukhatuṇḍena paggayha, pasanno lokanāyake {note:vippasannena cetasā (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Ukkhipitvāna gagaṇe {note:ukkhipitvā nalāṭena (ka.)}, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ apūjayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Antalikkhe ṭhito satthā, akā me anumodanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Iminā ekapadumena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, vinipātaṃ na gacchasi’.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho, jalajuttamanāmako;
::

::gathalast
Mama kammaṃ pakittetvā, agamā yena patthitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito {pb:T:1.0430}{pb:P:1.0277} kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekapadumiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ekapadumiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Tīṇuppalamāliyattheraapadānaṃ

### 36. Saddasaññakavaggo

#### 1. Saddasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Migaluddo {pb:T:1.0439}{pb:M:1.0325}{pb:V:1.0307}{pb:P:1.0282} pure āsiṃ, araññe kānane ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, devasaṅghapurakkhataṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catusaccaṃ pakāsentaṃ, uddharantaṃ mahājanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Assosiṃ madhuraṃ vācaṃ, karavīkarudopamaṃ {note:rutopamaṃ (?)}.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Brahmasarassa munino, sikhino lokabandhuno;
::

::gathalast
Ghose cittaṃ pasādetvā, pattomhi āsavakkhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekattiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saddasaññako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre

::gatha1

### 38. Bodhivandanavaggo

#### 1. Bodhivandakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṭaliṃ {pb:M:1.0335}{pb:V:1.0317}{pb:P:1.0290} haritaṃ disvā, pādapaṃ dharaṇīruhaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vipassiṃ lokamahitaṃ, karuṇāñāṇasāgaraṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ bodhimabhivandahaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::centre

#### 2. Pāṭalipupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vipassī {pb:T:1.0454} nāma bhagavā, sayambhū aggapuggalo;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tīṇi pāṭalipupphāni, ucchaṅge ṭhapitāni me;
::

::gathalast
Sīsaṃ nhāyitukāmova, nadītitthaṃ agacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nikkhamma bandhumatiyā, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Indīvaraṃva jalitaṃ, ādittaṃva hutāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Byagghūsabhaṃva {pb:V:1.0318} pavaraṃ, abhijātaṃva kesariṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmiṃ {pb:M:1.0336} pasanno {note:samaṇe (ka.)} sugate, kilesamaladhovane;
::

::gathalast
Gahetvā tīṇi pupphāni, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ apūjayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pāṭalipupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Pāṭalipupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

::gathalast

### 39. Avaṭaphalavaggo

#### 1. Avaṭaphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sataraṃsi {pb:M:1.0341}{pb:V:1.0323} nāma bhagavā, sayambhū aparājito;
::

::gathalast
Vivekakāmo sambuddho, gocarāyābhinikkhami.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Phalahattho ahaṃ disvā, upagacchiṃ narāsabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto sumano, avaṭaṃ {note:avaṇṭaṃ (sī.), ambaṭaṃ (syā.)} adadiṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ phalamadadiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:P:1.0295} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ {pb:T:1.0463} sudaṃ āyasmā avaṭaphaladāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre

::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:P:1.0297} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā valliphaladāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Valliphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 7. Kadaliphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::gathalast

44\.

#### 9. Soṇakoṭivīsattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vipassino {pb:P:1.0298} pāvacane, ekaṃ leṇaṃ mayā kataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cātuddisassa saṅghassa, bandhumārājadhāniyā.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dussehi bhūmiṃ leṇassa, santharitvā pariccajiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Udaggacitto sumano, akāsiṃ paṇidhiṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ārādhayeyyaṃ sambuddhaṃ, pabbajjañca labheyyahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anuttarañca nibbānaṃ, phuseyyaṃ santimuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Teneva sukkamūlena, kappe {note:kappaṃ (sī.), kappa (ka.)} navuti saṃsariṃ;
::

::gathalast
Devabhūto manusso ca, katapuñño virocahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:T:1.0470} kammāvasesena, idha pacchimake bhave;
::

::gathalast
Campāyaṃ aggaseṭṭhissa, jātomhi ekaputtako.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jātamattassa {pb:M:1.0346} me sutvā, pitu chando ayaṃ ahu;
::

::gathalast
Dadāmahaṃ kumārassa, vīsakoṭī anūnakā.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Caturaṅgulā ca me lomā, jātā pādatale ubho;
::

::gathalast
Sukhumā mudusamphassā, tūlāpicusamā subhā.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atītā navuti kappā, ayaṃ eko ca uttari;
::

::gathalast
Nābhijānāmi nikkhitte, pāde bhūmyā asanthate.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ārādhito {pb:V:1.0328} me sambuddho, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Arahattañca me pattaṃ, sītibhūtomhi nibbuto.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aggo āraddhavīriyānaṃ, niddiṭṭho sabbadassinā;
::

::gathalast
Khīṇāsavomhi arahā, chaḷabhiñño mahiddhiko.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, leṇadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
60\.

62\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
63\.

::gatha1
‘‘Thero {pb:T:1.0471} koṭivīso {note:koṭiviso (syā. ka.), koḷiviso (aññaṭṭhānesu)} soṇo, bhikkhusaṅghassa aggato;

::gathalast

#### 10. Pubbakammapilotikabuddhaapadānaṃ

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anotattasarāsanne{pb:P:1.0299}, ramaṇīye silātale;
::

::gathalast
Nānāratanapajjote, nānāgandhavanantare.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena, pareto {note:upeto (udānaṭṭhakathāyaṃ 4 vagge, 8 sutte)} lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Āsīno byākarī tattha, pubbakammāni attano.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
{note:suṇātha bhikkhave mayhaṃ, yaṃ kammaṃ pakataṃ mayā; ekaṃ araññikaṃ bhikkhuṃ, disvā dinnaṃ pilotikaṃ; patthitaṃ paṭhamaṃ buddhaṃ, buddhattāya mayā tadā; pilotiyassa kammassa, buddhattepi vipaccati; gopālako pure āsiṃ, gāviṃ pājeti gocaraṃ; pivantiṃ udakaṃ āvilaṃ, gāviṃ disvā nivārayiṃ; tena kammavipākena, idha pacchimake bhave; vipāsito yadicchakaṃ, na hi pātuṃ labhāmahaṃ (syā.)} ‘‘Suṇātha {pb:M:1.0347} bhikkhavo mayhaṃ, yaṃ kammaṃ pakataṃ mayā;
::

::gathalast
Pilotikassa kammassa, buddhattepi vipaccati {note:suṇātha bhikkhave mayhaṃ, yaṃ kammaṃ pakataṃ mayā; ekaṃ araññikaṃ bhikkhuṃ, disvā dinnaṃ pilotikaṃ; patthitaṃ paṭhamaṃ buddhaṃ, buddhattāya mayā tadā; pilotiyassa kammassa, buddhattepi vipaccati; gopālako pure āsiṃ, gāviṃ pājeti gocaraṃ; pivantiṃ udakaṃ āvilaṃ, gāviṃ disvā nivārayiṃ; tena kammavipākena, idha pacchimake bhave; vipāsito yadicchakaṃ, na hi pātuṃ labhāmahaṃ (syā.)}.
::

::centre
[1]
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Munāḷi {pb:T:1.0472} nāmahaṃ dhutto, pubbe aññāsu jātisu {note:aññāya jātiyā (udāna aṭṭha.)};
::

::gathalast
Paccekabuddhaṃ surabhiṃ {note:sarabhuṃ (sī.)}, abbhācikkhiṃ adūsakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammavipākena, niraye saṃsariṃ ciraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bahūvassasahassāni, dukkhaṃ vedesi vedanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammāvasesena, idha pacchimake bhave;
::

::gathalast
Abbhakkhānaṃ mayā laddhaṃ, sundarikāya kāraṇā.
::

::centre
[2]
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbābhibhussa {pb:V:1.0329} buddhassa, nando nāmāsi sāvako;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ abbhakkhāya niraye, ciraṃ saṃsaritaṃ mayā.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dasavassasahassāni, niraye saṃsariṃ ciraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Manussabhāvaṃ laddhāhaṃ, abbhakkhānaṃ bahuṃ labhiṃ.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammāvasesena, ciñcamānavikā mamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Abbhācikkhi abhūtena, janakāyassa aggato.
::

::centre
[3]
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Brāhmaṇo sutavā āsiṃ, ahaṃ sakkatapūjito;
::

::gathalast
Mahāvane pañcasate, mante vācemi māṇave.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatthāgato {pb:M:1.0348} {note:tamāgato (ka.)} isi bhīmo, pañcābhiñño mahiddhiko;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ cāhaṃ āgataṃ disvā, abbhācikkhiṃ adūsakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatohaṃ avacaṃ sisse, kāmabhogī ayaṃ isi;
::

::gathalast
Mayhampi bhāsamānassa, anumodiṃsu māṇavā.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato māṇavakā sabbe, bhikkhamānaṃ kule kule;
::

::gathalast
Mahājanassa āhaṃsu, kāmabhogī ayaṃ isi.

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:T:1.0473}{pb:P:1.0300} kammavipākena, pañca bhikkhusatā ime;
::

::gathalast

[4]

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vemātubhātaraṃ pubbe, dhanahetu haniṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
79\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

[5]

80\.

::

::gathalast
Paccekabuddhaṃ disvāna, magge sakalikaṃ {note:sakkhalikaṃ (ka.)} khipiṃ {note:dahiṃ (syā.)}.

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammavipākena, idha pacchimake bhave;
::

::gathalast

::centre
[6]
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthāroho {pb:V:1.0330} pure āsiṃ, paccekamunimuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Piṇḍāya vicarantaṃ taṃ, āsādesiṃ gajenahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammavipākena, bhanto {note:danto (ka.)} nāḷāgirī gajo;
::

::gathalast

[7]

84\.
::

‘‘Rājāhaṃ {pb:M:1.0349} patthivo {note:pattiko (syā. ka.), khattiyo (udāna aṭṭha.)} āsiṃ, sattiyā purisaṃ haniṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tena kammavipākena, niraye paccisaṃ bhusaṃ.

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kammuno tassa sesena, idāni sakalaṃ mama;
::

::gathalast
Pāde chaviṃ pakappesi {note:pakopesi (sī.)}, na hi kammaṃ vinassati.

::centre

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ kevaṭṭagāmasmiṃ, ahuṃ kevaṭṭadārako;
::

::gathalast
Macchake ghātite disvā, janayiṃ somanassakaṃ {note:somanassahaṃ (udāna aṭṭha.)}.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:T:1.0474} kammavipākena, sīsadukkhaṃ ahū mama;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe sakkā ca haññiṃsu, yadā hani viṭaṭūbho {note:viṭaṭubho (syā. ka.)}.
::

::centre
[9]
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Phussassāhaṃ pāvacane, sāvake paribhāsayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yavaṃ khādatha bhuñjatha, mā ca bhuñjatha sālayo.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammavipākena, temāsaṃ khāditaṃ yavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nimantito brāhmaṇena, verañjāyaṃ vasiṃ tadā.
::

::centre
[10]
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nibbuddhe vattamānamhi, mallaputtaṃ niheṭhayiṃ {note:nisedhayiṃ (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Tena kammavipākena, piṭṭhidukkhaṃ ahū mama.
::

[11]

91\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tikicchako ahaṃ āsiṃ, seṭṭhiputtaṃ virecayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tena kammavipākena, hoti pakkhandikā mama.
::

::centre
[12]

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Avacāhaṃ jotipālo, sugataṃ kassapaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Kuto nu bodhi muṇḍassa, bodhi paramadullabhā.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:M:1.0350}{pb:V:1.0331}{pb:P:1.0301} kammavipākena, acariṃ dukkaraṃ bahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Chabbassānuruveḷāyaṃ, tato bodhimapāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhaṃ etena maggena, pāpuṇiṃ bodhimuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kummaggena gavesissaṃ, pubbakammena vārito.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puññapāpaparikkhīṇo, sabbasantāpavajjito;
::

::gathalast
Asoko anupāyāso, nibbāyissamanāsavo.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ jino viyākāsi, bhikkhusaṅghassa aggato;
::

::gathalast
Sabbābhiññābalappatto, anotatte mahāsare’’ti.
::

Itthaṃ {pb:T:1.0475} sudaṃ bhagavā attano pubbacaritaṃ kammapilotikaṃ nāma buddhāpadānadhammapariyāyaṃ abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Pubbakammapilotikaṃ nāma buddhāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Avaṭaphalavaggo ekūnacattālīsamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Avaṭaṃ labujañceva, udumbarapilakkhu ca;
::

::gathalast
Phāru vallī ca kadalī, panaso koṭivīsako.
::

::gatha1
Pubbakammapiloti ca, apadānaṃ mahesino;
::

::gathalast
Gāthāyo ekanavuti, gaṇitāyo vibhāvibhi.
::

::centre
Cuddasamaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.
::

### 40. Pilindavacchavaggo

#### 1. Pilindavacchattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare {pb:T:1.0476}{pb:M:1.0351}{pb:V:1.0332}{pb:P:1.0302} haṃsavatiyā, āsiṃ dovāriko ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Akkhobhaṃ amitaṃ bhogaṃ, ghare sannicitaṃ mama.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rahogato nisīditvā, pahaṃsitvāna mānasaṃ {note:sampahaṃsitva mānasaṃ (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Nisajja pāsādavare, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā.
::

::centre
(Cintanākāro)
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Bahū medhigatā bhogā, phītaṃ antepuraṃ mama;
::

::gathalast
Rājāpi {note:rājisi (ka.)} sannimantesi, ānando pathavissaro.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ayañca buddho uppanno, adhiccuppattiko muni;
::

::gathalast
Saṃvijjanti ca me bhogā, dānaṃ dassāmi satthuno.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Padumena rājaputtena, dinnaṃ dānavaraṃ jine;
::

::gathalast
Hatthināge ca pallaṅke, apassenañcanappakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ahampi dānaṃ dassāmi, saṅghe gaṇavaruttame;
::

::gathalast
Adinnapubbamaññesaṃ, bhavissaṃ ādikammiko.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Cintetvāhaṃ bahuvidhaṃ, yāge yassa sukhaṃphalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Parikkhāradānamaddakkhiṃ, mama saṅkappapūraṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Parikkhārāni dassāmi, saṅghe gaṇavaruttame;
::

::gathalast
Adinnapubbamaññesaṃ, bhavissaṃ ādikammiko’.
::

::centre
(Dānavatthusampādanaṃ)
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Naḷakāre {pb:T:1.0477} upāgamma, chattaṃ kāresi tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Chattasatasahassāni, ekato sannipātayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dussasatasahassāni, ekato sannipātayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pattasatasahassāni, ekato sannipātayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vāsiyo {pb:M:1.0352}{pb:V:1.0333} satthake cāpi, sūciyo nakhachedane;
::

::gathalast
Heṭṭhāchatte ṭhapāpesiṃ, kāretvā tadanucchave.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vidhūpane tālavaṇṭe, morahatthe ca cāmare;
::

::gathalast
Parissāvane teladhāre {note:teladhare (sī.)}, kārayiṃ tadanucchave.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sūcighare aṃsabaddhe, athopi kāyabandhane;
::

::gathalast
Ādhārake ca sukate, kārayiṃ tadanucchave.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paribhogabhājane ca, athopi lohathālake;
::

::gathalast
Bhesajje {pb:P:1.0303} pūrayitvāna, heṭṭhāchatte ṭhapesahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vacaṃ usīraṃ laṭṭhimadhuṃ, pipphalī maricāni ca;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upāhanā pādukāyo, atho udakapuñchane;
::

::gathalast
Kattaradaṇḍe sukate, kārayiṃ tadanucchave.

::hangnum

::gatha1

::gatha1

::hangnum
21\.

#### 2. Selattheraapadānaṃ

Vimutti asadisā yassa, so me buddho nimantito.
::

::hangnum
258\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassa dhīti asadisā, thāmo yassa acintiyo;
::

::gathalast
Yassa parakkamo jeṭṭho, so me buddho nimantito.

259\.

#### 3. Sabbakittikattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
304\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kaṇikāraṃva {pb:M:1.0378}{pb:P:1.0323} jalitaṃ {note:jotantaṃ (sī.)}, dīparukkhaṃva ujjalaṃ {note:jotitaṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Osadhiṃva virocantaṃ, vijjutaṃ gagane yathā.
::

::hangnum
305\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asambhītaṃ anuttāsiṃ, migarājaṃva kesariṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ñāṇālokaṃ pakāsentaṃ, maddantaṃ titthiye gaṇe.
::

::hangnum
306\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uddharantaṃ imaṃ lokaṃ, chiddantaṃ sabbasaṃsayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Gajjantaṃ {note:asambhītaṃ (syā.), gacchantaṃ (ka.)} migarājaṃva, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
307\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jaṭājinadharo āsiṃ, brahā uju patāpavā;
::

::gathalast
Vākacīraṃ gahetvāna, pādamūle apatthariṃ.
::

::hangnum
308\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāḷānusāriyaṃ gayha, anulimpiṃ tathāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sambuddhamanulimpetvā, santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
309\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samuddharasimaṃ {pb:T:1.0508} lokaṃ, oghatiṇṇa {note:oghatiṇṇo (syā. ka.)} mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Ñāṇālokena jotesi, nāvaṭaṃ {note:pavaraṃ (syā.), vajira (pī.)} ñāṇamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
310\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammacakkaṃ {note:tuvaṃ cakkaṃ (ka.)} pavattesi, maddase paratitthiye;
::

::gathalast
Usabho jitasaṅgāmo, sampakampesi medaniṃ.
::

::hangnum
311\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahāsamudde ūmiyo, velantamhi pabhijjare;
::

::gathalast
Tatheva tava ñāṇamhi, sabbadiṭṭhī pabhijjare.
::

::hangnum
312\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sukhumacchikajālena, saramhi sampatānite;
::

::gathalast
Antojālikatā {note:jālagatā (sī.)} pāṇā, pīḷitā honti tāvade.
::

::hangnum
313\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatheva titthiyā loke, puthupāsaṇḍanissitā {note:mūḷhā saccavinissaṭā (syā.), muṭṭhasaccavinissaṭā (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Antoñāṇavare tuyhaṃ, parivattanti mārisa.
::

::hangnum
314\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Patiṭṭhā {pb:V:1.0357} vuyhataṃ oghe, tvañhi nātho abandhunaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhayaṭṭitānaṃ saraṇaṃ, muttitthīnaṃ parāyaṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
315\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekavīro {pb:M:1.0379} asadiso, mettākaruṇasañcayo {note:saññuto (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Asamo susamo santo {note:susīlo asamo santo (sī.), paññavā yuttacāgo ca (syā.)}, vasī tādī jitañjayo.
::

::hangnum
316\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhīro {pb:P:1.0324} vigatasammoho, anejo akathaṃkathī;
::

::gathalast
Tusito {note:vusito (sī.)} vantadososi, nimmalo saṃyato suci.
::

::hangnum
317\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅgātigo hatamado {note:gatamado (syā.), tamanudo (ka.)}, tevijjo tibhavantago;
::

::gathalast
Sīmātigo dhammagaru, gatattho hitavabbhuto {note:hitavappatho (sī. syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
318\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tārako {pb:T:1.0509} tvaṃ yathā nāvā, nidhīvassāsakārako;
::

::gathalast
Asambhīto yathā sīho, gajarājāva dappito.
::

::hangnum
319\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Thometvā dasagāthāhi, padumuttaraṃ mahāyasaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
320\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satthā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
321\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.

322\.

‘‘‘Saṭṭhi kappasahassāni, devaloke ramissati;

323\.

324\.

::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo’.

::hangnum
325\.

::gatha1
‘‘Yathāpi megho thanayaṃ, tappeti mediniṃ imaṃ;
::

::

::hangnum
326\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīlaṃ paññañca dhammañca, thavitvā lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pattomhi paramaṃ santiṃ, nibbānaṃ padamaccutaṃ.
::

::hangnum
327\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aho {pb:M:1.0380} nūna sa bhagavā, ciraṃ tiṭṭheyya cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast
Aññātañca vijāneyyuṃ, phuseyyuṃ {note:aññātañcāpi jāneyya, passeyya (ka.)} amataṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
328\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ayaṃ {pb:T:1.0510}{pb:V:1.0358} me pacchimā jāti, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.

::hangnum
329\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ buddhamabhithomayiṃ
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
330\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:P:1.0325} jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.

331\.
::

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
332\.
::

::gatha1

#### 4. Madhudāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
333\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sindhuyā nadiyā tīre, sukato assamo mama;
::

::gathalast
Tattha vācemahaṃ sisse, itihāsaṃ salakkhaṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
334\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammakāmā vinītā te, sotukāmā susāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷaṅge pāramippattā, sindhukūle vasanti te.
::

::hangnum
335\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uppātagamane {pb:T:1.0511} ceva, lakkhaṇesu ca kovidā;
::

::gathalast
Uttamatthaṃ gavesantā, vasanti vipine tadā.
::

::hangnum
336\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sumedho nāma sambuddho, loke uppajji tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Amhākaṃ anukampanto, upāgacchi vināyako.
::

::hangnum
337\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upāgataṃ mahāvīraṃ, sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tiṇasanthārakaṃ katvā, lokajeṭṭhassadāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
338\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vipināto {pb:M:1.0381} madhuṃ gayha, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sambuddho paribhuñjitvā, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
::

::hangnum
339\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo taṃ adāsi madhuṃ me, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
::

::hangnum
340\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Iminā madhudānena, tiṇasanthārakena ca;
::

::gathalast
Tiṃsa kappasahassāni, devaloke ramissati.
::

::hangnum
341\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tiṃsa {pb:V:1.0359} kappasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
342\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.
::

::hangnum
343\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Devalokā idhāgantvā, mātukucchiṃ upāgate;
::

::gathalast
Madhuvassaṃ pavassittha, chādayaṃ madhunā mahiṃ’.
::

::hangnum
344\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mayi nikkhantamattamhi, kucchiyā ca suduttarā;
::

::gathalast
Tatrāpi madhuvassaṃ me, vassate niccakālikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
345\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Agārā {pb:T:1.0512}{pb:P:1.0326} abhinikkhamma, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Lābhī annassa pānassa, madhudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
346\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbakāmasamiddhohaṃ, bhavitvā devamānuse;
::

::gathalast
Teneva madhudānena, pattomhi āsavakkhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
347\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vuṭṭhamhi deve caturaṅgule tiṇe, sampupphite {note:supupphite (syā.)} dharaṇīruhe sañchanne {note:vappadese (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Suññe ghare maṇḍaparukkhamūlake, vasāmi niccaṃ sukhito anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
348\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Majjhe mahante hīne ca {note:majjhe mayhaṃ bhavā assu (syā. pī. ka.)}, bhave sabbe atikkamiṃ {note:ye bhave samatikkamiṃ (syā. ka.), yo bhavesu pakittayi (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Ajja me āsavā khīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
::

::hangnum
349\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, madhudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
350\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:M:1.0382} jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
::

::hangnum
351\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
352\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā madhudāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Madhudāyakattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Padumakūṭāgāriyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gatha1
‘‘Vanasaṇḍaṃ {pb:V:1.0360} samogayha, piyadassī mahāmuni;

::gathalast

::hangnum
355\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::gatha1
‘‘Tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ;

::gathalast

::hangnum
357\.

::gatha1

360\.

::gatha1

#### 6. Bākulattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::gatha1
‘‘Maṇḍapā ca bahū tattha, pupphitā sinduvārakā;

::hangnum
