#### 7. Girimānandattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
419\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhariyā me kālaṅkatā, putto sīvathikaṃ gato;
::

::gathalast
Mātā pitā matā bhātā, ekacitamhi {note:mātā pitā ca bhātā ca, ekacitakamhi (sī. syā.)} ḍayhare.
::

::hangnum
420\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena sokena santatto, kiso paṇḍu ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cittakkhepo ca me āsi, tena sokena aṭṭito.
::

::hangnum
421\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sokasallaparetohaṃ{pb:P:1.0331}, vanantamupasaṅkamiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pavattaphalaṃ bhuñjitvā, rukkhamūle vasāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
422\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sumedho {pb:M:1.0388}{pb:V:1.0365} nāma sambuddho, dukkhassantakaro jino;
::

::gathalast
Mamuddharitukāmo so, āgañchi mama santikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
423\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padasaddaṃ suṇitvāna, sumedhassa mahesino;
::

::gathalast
Paggahetvānahaṃ sīsaṃ, ullokesiṃ mahāmuniṃ.
::

::hangnum
424\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upāgate mahāvīre, pīti me udapajjatha;
::

::gathalast
Tadāsimekaggamano, disvā taṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
425\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satiṃ paṭilabhitvāna, paṇṇamuṭṭhimadāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nisīdi bhagavā tattha, anukampāya cakkhumā.
::

::hangnum
426\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nisajja {pb:T:1.0521} tattha bhagavā, sumedho lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṃ me kathayī buddho, sokasallavinodanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
427\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Anavhitā tato āguṃ, ananuññātā ito gatā;
::

::gathalast
Yathāgatā tathā gatā, tattha kā paridevanā.
::

::hangnum
428\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yathāpi pathikā sattā, vassamānāya vuṭṭhiyā;
::

::gathalast
Sabhaṇḍā upagacchanti, vassassāpatanāya te.
::

::hangnum
429\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Vasse ca te oramite, sampayanti yadicchakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ mātā pitā tuyhaṃ, tattha kā paridevanā.
::

::hangnum
430\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Āgantukā pāhunakā, caliteritakampitā;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ mātā pitā tuyhaṃ, tattha kā paridevanā.
::

::hangnum
431\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yathāpi urago jiṇṇaṃ, hitvā gacchati saṃ tacaṃ {note:saṃtanuṃ (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ mātā pitā tuyhaṃ, saṃ tanuṃ idha hīyare’.
::

::hangnum
432\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhassa giramaññāya, sokasallaṃ vivajjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pāmojjaṃ janayitvāna, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ avandahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
433\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vanditvāna mahānāgaṃ, pūjayiṃ girimañjariṃ {note:girimañjarimapūjayiṃ (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantaṃ {note:dibbagandhena sampannaṃ (sī. syā.)}, sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
434\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pūjayitvāna sambuddhaṃ, sire katvāna añjaliṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
435\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nittiṇṇosi {pb:M:1.0389}{pb:P:1.0332} {note:nittaṇhosi (sī.), vitiṇṇosi (syā.)} mahāvīra, sabbaññu lokanāyaka;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe satte uddharasi, ñāṇena tvaṃ mahāmune.

::hangnum
436\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
437\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
438\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
439\.
::

::gatha1

::hangnum

442\.

#### 10. Ajitattheraapadānaṃ

::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ajito thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ajitattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Pilindavacchavaggo cattālīsamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ {pb:M:1.0396} –

::gatha1
Pilindavaccho selo ca, sabbakittī madhuṃdado;
::

::gathalast
Kūṭāgārī bākulo ca, giri saḷalasavhayo.
::

::gatha1
Sabbado {pb:P:1.0338} ajito ceva, gāthāyo gaṇitā iha;
::

::gathalast
Satāni pañca gāthānaṃ, vīsati ca taduttarīti.
::

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Padumārakkhado {pb:T:1.0532} ceva, umā gandhodakena ca;
::

::gathalast
Ekapadma saddasaññī, mandāraṃ bodhivandako.
::

::gatha1
Avaṭañca pilindi {note:evameva dissati} ca, gāthāyo gaṇitā iha;
::

::gathalast
Catusattati gāthāyo, ekādasa satāni ca.
::

::centre
Padumavaggadasakaṃ.
::

::centre
Catutthasatakaṃ samattaṃ.
::

### 41. Metteyyavaggo

#### 1. Tissametteyyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabbhārakūṭaṃ {pb:T:1.0533}{pb:M:1.0397}{pb:V:1.0373}{pb:P:2.0339} nissāya, sobhito nāma tāpaso;
::

::gathalast
Pavattaphalaṃ bhuñjitvā, vasati pabbatantare.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aggiṃ dāruṃ āharitvā, ujjālesiṃ ahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Uttamatthaṃ gavesanto, brahmalokūpapattiyā.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Mamuddharitukāmo so, āgacchi mama santike.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ karosi mahāpuñña, dehi me aggidārukaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ahamaggiṃ paricare, tato me suddhi hohiti {note:hehiti (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Subhaddako tvaṃ manuje, devate tvaṃ pajānasi;
::

::gathalast
Tuvaṃ aggiṃ paricara, handa te aggidārukaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato kaṭṭhaṃ gahetvāna, aggiṃ ujjālayī jino;
::

::gathalast
Na tattha kaṭṭhaṃ pajjhāyi, pāṭiheraṃ mahesino.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na te aggi pajjalati, āhutī te na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Niratthakaṃ vataṃ tuyhaṃ, aggiṃ paricarassu me.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kīdiso so {note:te (syā. ka.)} mahāvīra, aggi tava pavuccati;
::

::gathalast
Mayhampi kathayassetaṃ, ubho paricarāmase.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hetudhammanirodhāya{pb:T:1.0534}, kilesasamaṇāya ca;
::

::gathalast
Issāmacchariyaṃ hitvā, tayo ete mamāhutī.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kīdiso tvaṃ mahāvīra, kathaṃ gottosi mārisa;
::

::gathalast
Ācārapaṭipatti te, bāḷhaṃ kho mama ruccati.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khattiyamhi {pb:P:2.0340} kule jāto, abhiññāpāramiṃ gato;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇo, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadi {pb:M:1.0398}{pb:V:1.0374} buddhosi sabbaññū, pabhaṅkara tamonuda;
::

::gathalast
Namassissāmi taṃ deva, dukkhassantakaro tuvaṃ.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pattharitvājinacammaṃ, nisīdanamadāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nisīda nātha sabbaññu, upaṭṭhissāmahaṃ tuvaṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nisīdi bhagavā tattha, ajinamhi suvitthate;
::

::gathalast
Nimantayitvā sambuddhaṃ, pabbataṃ agamāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khāribhārañca pūretvā, tindukaphalamāhariṃ;
::

::gathalast
Madhunā yojayitvāna, phalaṃ buddhassadāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama nijjhāyamānassa, paribhuñji tadā jino;
::

::gathalast
Tattha cittaṃ pasādesiṃ, pekkhanto lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Mamassame nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo maṃ phalena tappesi, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Pañcavīsatikkhattuṃ {pb:T:1.0535} so, devarajjaṃ karissati;
::

::gathalast
Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa saṅkappamaññāya, pubbakammasamaṅgino;
::

::gathalast
Annaṃ pānañca vatthañca, sayanañca mahārahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Puññakammena saṃyuttā, nibbattissanti tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Sadā pamudito cāyaṃ, bhavissati anāmayo.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Upapajjati yaṃ yoniṃ, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha sukhito hutvā, manussattaṃ gamissati.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ajjhāyako mantadharo, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Sambuddhaṃ upagantvāna, arahā so bhavissati’.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yato sarāmi attānaṃ, yato pattosmi viññutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhoge me ūnatā natthi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Varadhammamanuppatto, rāgadose samūhaniṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇo, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:M:1.0399} jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:V:1.0375} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ {pb:T:1.0536} sudaṃ āyasmā tissametteyyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Tissametteyyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Puṇṇakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabbhārakūṭaṃ {pb:P:2.0341} nissāya, sayambhū aparājito;
::

::gathalast
Ābādhiko ca so {note:ābādhiko garu (sī.)} buddho, vasati pabbatantare.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama assamasāmantā, panādo āsi tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Buddhe nibbāyamānamhi, āloko udapajjatha {note:āsi tāvade (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāvatā vanasaṇḍasmiṃ, acchakokataracchakā;
::

::gathalast
Vāḷā ca {note:byagghā (sī.)} kesarī sabbe, abhigajjiṃsu tāvade.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uppātaṃ tamahaṃ disvā, pabbhāraṃ agamāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tatthaddassāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, nibbutaṃ aparājitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suphullaṃ sālarājaṃva, sataraṃsiṃva uggataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vītaccikaṃva aṅgāraṃ, nibbutaṃ aparājitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṇaṃ kaṭṭhañca pūretvā, citakaṃ tatthakāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Citakaṃ sukataṃ katvā, sarīraṃ jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sarīraṃ jhāpayitvāna, gandhatoyaṃ samokiriṃ;
::

::gathalast
Antalikkhe ṭhito yakkho, nāmamaggahi tāvade.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:T:1.0537}{pb:M:1.0400} pūritaṃ {note:taṃ pūritaṃ (syā.), sappurisa (ka.)} tayā kiccaṃ, sayambhussa mahesino;
::

::gathalast
Puṇṇako nāma nāmena, sadā hohi tuvaṃ {note:yadā hosi tuvaṃ (syā.), sadā hohiti tvaṃ (ka.)} mune.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamhā kāyā cavitvāna, devalokaṃ agacchahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tattha dibbamayo gandho, antalikkhā pavassati {note:antalikkhe pavāyati (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatrāpi nāmadheyyaṃ me, puṇṇakoti ahū tadā;
::

::gathalast
Devabhūto manusso vā, saṅkappaṃ pūrayāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ, carimo vattate bhavo;
::

::gathalast
Idhāpi puṇṇako nāma, nāmadheyyaṃ pakāsati.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tosayitvāna {pb:V:1.0376} sambuddhaṃ, gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, tanukiccassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā puṇṇako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Puṇṇakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 3. Mettaguttheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre{pb:T:1.0538}{pb:P:2.0342}, asoko nāma pabbato;
::

::gathalast
Tatthāsi assamo mayhaṃ, vissakammena {note:visukammena (sī. syā. ka.)} māpito.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sumedho nāma sambuddho, aggo kāruṇiko muni;
::

::gathalast
Nivāsayitvā pubbaṇhe, piṇḍāya me {note:maṃ (sī.)} upāgami.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upāgataṃ {pb:M:1.0401} mahāvīraṃ, sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paggayha sugatapattaṃ {note:sugataṃ pattaṃ (sī.), subhakaṃ pattaṃ (pī.)}, sappitelaṃ apūrayiṃ {note:sappitelena pūrayiṃ (sī.), sappitelassa’pūrayiṃ (?)}.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Datvānahaṃ buddhaseṭṭhe, sumedhe lokanāyake;
::

::gathalast
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, bhiyyo {note:bhīyo (sī.), bhīyyo (pī.)} hāsaṃ janesahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iminā sappidānena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Devabhūto manusso vā, labhāmi vipulaṃ sukhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vinipātaṃ vivajjetvā, saṃsarāmi bhavābhave;
::

::gathalast
Tattha cittaṃ paṇidhitvā, labhāmi acalaṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lābhā tuyhaṃ suladdhaṃ te, yaṃ maṃ addakkhi brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Mama dassanamāgamma, arahattaṃ bhavissati {note:arahā tvaṃ bhavissasi (sī. pī.), arahattaṃ gamissasi (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vissattho {note:vissaṭṭho (syā. pī.), visaṭṭho (ka.)} hohi mā bhāyi, adhigantvā mahāyasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mamañhi sappiṃ datvāna, parimokkhasi jātiyā.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iminā {pb:V:1.0377} sappidānena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Devabhūto manusso vā, labhase vipulaṃ sukhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iminā {pb:T:1.0539} sappidānena, mettacittavatāya ca;
::

::gathalast
Aṭṭhārase kappasate, devaloke ramissasi.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭhatiṃsatikkhattuñca, devarājā bhavissasi;
::

::gathalast
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekapaññāsakkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissasi;
::

::gathalast
Cāturanto vijitāvī, jambumaṇḍassa {note:jambusaṇḍassa (sī. pī.)} issaro.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahāsamuddovakkhobho, duddharo pathavī yathā;
::

::gathalast
Evameva ca te bhogā, appameyyā bhavissare.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṭṭhikoṭī hiraññassa, cajitvā {note:catvāna (sī. ka.), datvāna (syā. pī.)} pabbajiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ kusalaṃ gavesanto, bāvariṃ upasaṅkamiṃ.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha {pb:M:1.0402}{pb:P:2.0343} mante adhīyāmi, chaḷaṅgaṃ nāma lakkhaṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tamandhakāraṃ vidhamaṃ, uppajji tvaṃ mahāmuni.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tava dassanakāmohaṃ, āgatomhi mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Tava dhammaṃ suṇitvāna, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, sappiṃ buddhassadāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etthantare nābhijāne, sappiṃ viññāpitaṃ {note:viññāpitā (?)} mayā.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, uppajjati yadicchakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cittamaññāya nibbattaṃ, sabbe santappayāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aho buddhā aho dhammā {note:aho buddho aho dhammo (sī.) theragā. 201 theragāthāya tadaṭṭhakathāya ca saṃsandetabbaṃ}, aho no satthu sampadā;
::

::gathalast
Thokañhi sappiṃ datvāna, appameyyaṃ labhāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahāsamudde {pb:T:1.0540} udakaṃ, yāvatā nerupassato;
::

::gathalast
Mama sappiṃ upādāya, kalabhāgaṃ na hessati {note:hissati (syā. ka.), essati (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāvatā cakkavāḷassa, kariyantassa {note:kārayantassa (syā.), kayirantassa (pī.), āharantassa (ka.)} rāsito;
::

::gathalast
Mama nibbattavatthānaṃ {note:mayā nivatthavatthānaṃ (pī.)}, okāso so na sammati.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabbatarājā himavā, pavaropi siluccayo;
::

::gathalast
Mamānulittagandhassa, upanidhiṃ {note:upanidhaṃ (sī. syā. ka.), upanīyaṃ (pī.)} na hessati.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vatthaṃ {pb:V:1.0378} gandhañca sappiñca, aññañca diṭṭhadhammikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asaṅkhatañca nibbānaṃ, sappidānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satipaṭṭhānasayano, samādhijhānagocaro;
::

::gathalast
Bojjhaṅgabhojano {note:… janano (syā. ka.)} ajja, sappidānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mettagū thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Mettaguttherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Dhotakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gaṅgā {pb:T:1.0541}{pb:M:1.0403} bhāgīrathī nāma, himavantā pabhāvitā {note:himavantappabhāvitā (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Haṃsavatiyā dvārena, anusandati tāvade.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sobhito nāma ārāmo, gaṅgākūle sumāpito;
::

::gathalast
Tattha padumuttaro buddho, vasate lokanāyako.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tidasehi {pb:P:2.0344} yathā indo, manujehi purakkhato;
::

::gathalast
Nisīdi tattha bhagavā, asambhītova kesarī.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare haṃsavatiyā, vasāmi {note:ahosiṃ (syā.)} brāhmaṇo ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷaṅgo nāma nāmena, evaṃnāmo mahāmuni.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭhārasa sissasatā, parivārenti maṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Tehi sissehi samito, gaṅgātīraṃ upāgamiṃ.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatthaddasāsiṃ samaṇe, nikkuhe dhotapāpake;
::

::gathalast
Bhāgīrathiṃ tarantehaṃ {note:tarantohaṃ (syā. pī.)}, evaṃ cintesi tāvade.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāyaṃ pātaṃ {note:sāyapātaṃ (pī.)} tarantāme, buddhaputtā mahāyasā;
::

::gathalast
Vihesayanti attānaṃ, tesaṃ attā vihaññati.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sadevakassa lokassa, buddho aggo pavuccati;
::

::gathalast
Natthi me dakkhiṇe kāraṃ, gatimaggavisodhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃnūna {pb:V:1.0379} buddhaseṭṭhassa, setuṃ gaṅgāya kāraye;
::

::gathalast
Kārāpetvā imaṃ kammaṃ {note:setuṃ (syā.)}, santarāmi imaṃ bhavaṃ.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassaṃ {pb:T:1.0542} datvāna, setuṃ kārāpayiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saddahanto kataṃ kāraṃ, vipulaṃ me bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kārāpetvāna taṃ setuṃ, upesiṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sirasi añjaliṃ katvā, imaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Satasahassassa vayaṃ {note:vayaṃ satasahassaṃva (ka.)}, datvā {note:katvā (sī. pī.)} kārāpito mayā;
::

::gathalast
Tavatthāya mahāsetu, paṭiggaṇha mahāmune.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:M:1.0404} lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo me setuṃ akāresi, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
::

::centre
(Setudānaānisaṃso)
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Darito pabbatato vā, rukkhato patitopiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cutopi lacchatī ṭhānaṃ, setudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Virūḷhamūlasantānaṃ, nigrodhamiva māluto;
::

::gathalast
Amittā nappasahanti, setudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Nāssa corā pasahanti, nātimaññanti khattiyā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe tarissatāmitte, setudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Abbhokāsagataṃ {pb:P:2.0345} santaṃ, kaṭhinātapatāpitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Puññakammena saṃyuttaṃ, na bhavissati vedanā {note:tāvade (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Devaloke manusse vā, hatthiyānaṃ sunimmitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassa saṅkappamaññāya, nibbattissati tāvade.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sahassassā {pb:T:1.0543} vātajavā, sindhavā sīghavāhanā;
::

::gathalast
Sāyaṃ pātaṃ upessanti, setudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Āgantvāna manussattaṃ, sukhitoyaṃ bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Vehāsaṃ {note:ihāpi (sī. syā. pī.)} manujasseva, hatthiyānaṃ bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa {pb:V:1.0380} dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ, jalajuttamanāmake;
::

::gathalast
Tattha kāraṃ karitvāna, pattohaṃ āsavakkhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padhānaṃ pahitattomhi, upasanto nirūpadhi;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:M:1.0405} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhotako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Dhotakattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Upasīvattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre{pb:T:1.0544}, anomo nāma pabbato;
::

::gathalast
Assamo sukato mayhaṃ, paṇṇasālā sumāpitā.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nadī ca sandatī tattha, supatitthā manoramā;
::

::gathalast
Anūpatitthe jāyanti, padumuppalakā bahū.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṭhīnā pāvusā macchā, balajā muñjarohitā;
::

::gathalast
Macchakacchapasañchannā {note:macchakacchapasampannā (?)}, nadikā sandate tadā.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Timirā pupphitā tattha, asokā khuddamālakā;
::

::gathalast
Punnāgā giripunnāgā, sampavanti mamassamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuṭajā {pb:P:2.0346} pupphitā tattha, tiṇasūlavanāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Sālā ca saḷalā tattha, campakā pupphitā bahū.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjunā atimuttā ca, mahānāmā ca pupphitā;
::

::gathalast
Asanā madhugandhī ca, pupphitā te mamassame.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uddālakā pāṭalikā, yūthikā ca piyaṅgukā;
::

::gathalast
Bimbijālakasañchannā, samantā aḍḍhayojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mātaggārā {pb:V:1.0381} {note:mātaṅgavā (sī.), mātakarā (syā.), mātaṅgā vā (pī.)} sattaliyo, pāṭalī sinduvārakā;
::

::gatha2
Aṅkolakā bahū tattha, tālakuṭṭhi {note:tālakūṭā (sī. syā.), tālakuṭṭhā (pī.)} ca pupphitā;
::

::gathalast
Seleyyakā bahū tattha, pupphitā mama assame.
::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etesu {pb:M:1.0406} pupphajātesu {note:pupphamānesu (sī. pī.)}, sobhanti pādapā bahū;
::

::gathalast
Samantā {pb:T:1.0545} tena gandhena, vāyate mama assamo.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Harītakā āmalakā, ambajambuvibhītakā {note:vibhiṭakā (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Kolā bhallātakā billā, phārusakaphalāni ca.
::

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tindukā ca piyālā ca, madhukā kāsumārayo;
::

::gathalast
Labujā panasā tattha, kadalī badarīphalā {note:mandariphalā (ka.), candarīphalā (syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ambāṭakā bahū tattha, vallikāraphalāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Bījapūrasapāriyo {note:cirasaṃrasapākā ca (syā.), viṭapā ca sapākā ca (pī), vidaparapadādayo (ka.)}, phalitā mama assame.
::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āḷakā isimuggā ca, tato modaphalā bahū;
::

::gathalast
Avaṭā pakkabharitā {note:sakkarāritā (ka.)}, pilakkhudumbarāni ca.
::

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pipphilī marīcā tattha, nigrodhā ca kapitthanā;
::

::gathalast
Udumbarakā bahavo, kaṇḍupaṇṇā ca hariyo {note:kaṇḍapakkā ca pāriyo (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
114\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ete caññe ca bahavo, phalitā assame mama;
::

::gathalast
Puppharukkhāpi bahavo, pupphitā mama assame.
::

::hangnum
115\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āluvā ca kaḷambā ca, biḷālī takkalāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Ālakā tālakā ceva, vijjanti assame mama.

116\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::gathalast

#### 6. Nandakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
161\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Migaluddo {pb:P:2.0350} pure āsiṃ, araññe kānane ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pasadaṃ migamesanto, sayambhuṃ addasaṃ ahaṃ {note:jinaṃ (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
162\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anuruddho {pb:V:1.0385} nāma sambuddho, sayambhū aparājito;
::

::gathalast
Vivekakāmo so dhīro, vanamajjhogahī tadā.
::

::hangnum
163\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catudaṇḍe gahetvāna, catuṭṭhāne ṭhapesahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maṇḍapaṃ sukataṃ katvā, padmapupphehi chādayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
164\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maṇḍapaṃ {pb:T:1.0551} chādayitvāna, sayambhuṃ abhivādayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhanuṃ tattheva nikkhippa, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
165\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Naciraṃ pabbajitassa {note:pabbajitassa aciraṃ (sī.)}, byādhi me udapajjatha;
::

::gathalast
Pubbakammaṃ saritvāna, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
166\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pubbakammena saṃyutto, tusitaṃ agamāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
167\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::gathalast

::gatha1

::hangnum

::gatha1

::gatha1

#### 7. Hemakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
183\.

::gatha1

::gatha1

#### 8. Todeyyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::gatha1

225\.

226\.

::gatha1

227\.

::hangnum

::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama assamasāmantā, yakkho āsi mahiddhiko;

#### 9. Jatukaṇṇittheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
277\.

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:P:2.0358} {note:tayo (sī.)} pāsādamāruyha, mahābhoge valañjako {note:ubbiddhā gehaluñjakā (ka.), ubbiddhāgehalañchakā (sī.)};
::

::gathalast

::gathalast

::gatha1

#### 10. Udenattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
330\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre{pb:P:2.0362}, padumo nāma pabbato;
::

::gathalast
Assamo sukato mayhaṃ, paṇṇasālā sumāpitā.
::

::hangnum
331\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nadiyo sandare tattha, supatitthā manoramā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
332\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṭhīnā {pb:T:1.0569} pāvusā macchā, balajā muñjarohitā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
333\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ambajambūhi sañchannā, kareritilakā tathā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
334\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṅkolakā bimbijālā, māyākārī ca pupphitā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
335\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atimuttā sattalikā, nāgā sālā ca pupphitā;
::

::gathalast
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
336\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kosambā saḷalā nīpā, aṭṭhaṅgāpi ca pupphitā {note:aṭṭhaṅgā ca supupphitā (sī.), kaṭṭhaṅgā ca supupphitā (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
337\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Harītakā āmalakā, ambajambuvibhītakā;
::

::gathalast
Kolā bhallātakā billā, phalāni bahu assame.
::

::hangnum
338\.
::

Udenattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

::centre
Metteyyavaggo ekacattālīsamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Metteyyo puṇṇako thero, mettagū dhotakopi ca;
::

::gathalast
Upasivo {pb:T:1.0574} ca nando ca, hemako sattamo tahiṃ.
::

::gatha1
Todeyyo jatukaṇṇī ca, udeno ca mahāyaso;
::

::gathalast
Tīṇi gāthāsatānettha, asīti tīṇi cuttariṃ.
::

### 42. Bhaddālivaggo

#### 1. Bhaddālittheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sumedho {pb:T:2.0001}{pb:M:1.0429}{pb:V:1.0401} nāma sambuddho, aggo kāruṇiko muni;
::

::gathalast
Vivekakāmo lokaggo, himavantamupāgami.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjhogāhetvā himavaṃ, sumedho lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvāna, nisīdi purisuttamo.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samādhiṃ so samāpanno, sumedho lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Sattarattindivaṃ buddho, nisīdi purisuttamo.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khāribhāraṃ {note:khārikājaṃ (sī.)} gahetvāna, vanamajjhogahiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sammajjaniṃ gahetvāna, sammajjitvāna assamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Catudaṇḍe ṭhapetvāna, akāsiṃ maṇḍapaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sālapupphaṃ {pb:P:2.0366} āharitvā, maṇḍapaṃ chādayiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto sumano, abhivandiṃ tathāgataṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:T:2.0002} vadanti sumedhoti, bhūripaññaṃ sumedhasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Buddhassa giramaññāya, sabbe devā samāgamuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asaṃsayaṃ buddhaseṭṭho, dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sumedho nāma sambuddho, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Devasaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo me sattāhaṃ maṇḍapaṃ, dhārayī sālachāditaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Devabhūto manusso vā, hemavaṇṇo bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Pahūtabhogo hutvāna, kāmabhogī bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Saṭṭhi {pb:M:1.0430}{pb:V:1.0402} nāgasahassāni, sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā;
::

::gathalast
Suvaṇṇakacchā mātaṅgā, hemakappanavāsasā.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ārūḷhā gāmaṇīyehi, tomaraṅkusapāṇibhi;
::

::gathalast
Sāyaṃ pāto {note:sāyapāto (pī.)} upaṭṭhānaṃ, āgamissantimaṃ naraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tehi nāgehi parivuto, ramissati ayaṃ naro.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Saṭṭhi assasahassāni, sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā;
::

::gathalast
Ājānīyāva jātiyā, sindhavā sīghavāhino.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ārūḷhā gāmaṇīyehi, illiyācāpadhāribhi;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Saṭṭhi rathasahassāni, sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ārūḷhā gāmaṇīyehi, cāpahatthehi vammibhi;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Saṭṭhi gāmasahassāni, paripuṇṇāni sabbaso;
::

::gatha2

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Hatthī assā rathā pattī, senā ca caturaṅginī;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, devaloke ramissati;

::hangnum
21\.

::hangnum
22\.

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;

::hangnum
23\.

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi{pb:M:1.0431}, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;

::gathalast

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lābhā {pb:V:1.0403} mayhaṃ suladdhaṃ me, yamahaññāsi sāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Namo {pb:T:2.0004} te purisājañña, namo te purisuttama;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha sukhito homi, phalaṃ me ñāṇakittane.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ, carimo vattate bhavo;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bhaddālitthero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Bhaddālittherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Ekachattiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Candabhāgānadītīre, assamo sukato mama;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uttānakūlā nadikā, supatitthā manoramā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Acchā {pb:T:2.0005}{pb:M:1.0432} dīpī ca mayūrā, karavīkā ca sāḷikā;

::gathalast
Kūjanti sabbadā ete, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kokilā mañjubhāṇī ca, haṃsā ca madhurassarā;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīhā byagghā varāhā ca, accha {note:vaka (sī. pī.), bakā (syā.), vakā (ka.)} kokataracchakā;
::

::gathalast
Giriduggamhi nādenti, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ.

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Eṇīmigā {pb:V:1.0404}{pb:P:2.0368} ca sarabhā, bheraṇḍā sūkarā bahū;

::gathalast
Giriduggamhi nādenti, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uddālakā campakā ca, pāṭalī sinduvārakā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṅkolā yūthikā ceva, sattalī bimbijālikā;
::

::gathalast
Kaṇikārā ca pupphanti, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ {note:kaṇikākaṇikārā ca, pupphanti mama assame (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāgā sālā ca saḷalā, puṇḍarīkettha pupphitā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjunā asanā cettha, mahānāmā ca pupphitā;
::

::gathalast
Sālā ca kaṅgupupphā ca, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ambā jambū ca tilakā, nimbā ca sālakalyāṇī;
::

::gathalast
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asokā ca kapiṭṭhā ca, girimālettha {note:bhaginimālettha (sī. pī.), bhaginimālā ca (syā.)} pupphitā;
::

::gathalast
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kadambā {pb:T:2.0006} kadalī ceva, isimuggā ca ropitā;
::

::gathalast
Dhuvaṃ phalāni dhārenti, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Harītakā āmalakā, ambajambuvibhītakā;
::

::gathalast
Kolā bhallātakā billā, phalino mama assame.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Avidūre {pb:M:1.0433} pokkharaṇī, supatitthā manoramā;
::

::gathalast
Mandālakehi sañchannā, padumuppalakehi ca.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gabbhaṃ gaṇhanti padumā, aññe pupphanti kesarī;
::

::gathalast

48\.

::gatha1

::gatha1

::gathalast

::gathalast

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
58\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

#### 3. Tiṇasūlakachādaniyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
79\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
80\.

::gatha1
‘‘Caramānonupubbena, gaṅgātīraṃ upāgamiṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
81\.

::gatha1
‘‘Assamaṃ tattha māpetvā, vasāmi assame ahaṃ;
::

::hangnum
82\.

::gatha1
‘‘Mamupenti ca vissatthā, kūjanti ca manoharaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama {pb:T:2.0010} assamasāmantā, migarājā catukkamo;

84\.

::gatha1
‘‘Nadite {pb:M:1.0436}{pb:P:2.0371} migarāje ca, hāso me udapajjatha;

::hangnum
85\.

::gatha1
‘‘Disvānāhaṃ devadevaṃ, tissaṃ lokagganāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uggacchantaṃva sūriyaṃ, sālarājaṃva pupphitaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tava ñāṇena sabbaññu, mocesimaṃ sadevakaṃ;

::gathalast

88\.

::gatha1

89\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sīsaṃnhāto cayaṃ poso, pupphamākaṅkhate yadi {note:sāyaṃ pāto cayaṃ poso, pupphehi maṃ achādayi (syā.)};

::gathalast

::gathalast

Aṭṭhārasamaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

::gatha1

#### 4. Madhumaṃsadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare {pb:V:1.0409} bandhumatiyā, sūkariko ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ukkoṭaṃ randhayitvāna {note:ukkoṭakaṃ randhayitvā (sī. syā.)}, madhumaṃsamhi {note:madhusappimhi (pī.), madhuṃ maṃsamhi (ka.)} okiriṃ.

107\.

‘‘Sannipātaṃ {pb:M:1.0438} ahaṃ gantvā, ekaṃ pattaṃ gahesahaṃ;

111\.

112\.

113\.

#### 6. Ekadīpiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
124\.

::gatha1
‘‘Parinibbute sugate, siddhatthe lokanāyake;

::gathalast

::hangnum
125\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āropite {pb:T:2.0015} ca citake, siddhatthe lokanāyake;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
126\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Avidūre citakassa, dīpaṃ ujjālayiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
127\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;

::hangnum
128\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha me sukataṃ byamhaṃ, ekadīpīti ñāyati;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
129\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Udayantova {pb:P:2.0374} sūriyo, deho me jotate sadā;
::

::gathalast
Sappabhāhi sarīrassa, āloko hoti me sadā.
::

::hangnum
130\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tirokuṭṭaṃ {pb:V:1.0411} {note:tirokuḍḍaṃ (sī. syā. ka.)} tiroselaṃ, samatiggayha {note:sabbatthapi evameva dissati} pabbataṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
131\.

132\.

::gatha1

133\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
134\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jātiyā catuvassohaṃ, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
135\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dibbacakkhuṃ {pb:T:2.0016} visodhesiṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
136\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tirokuṭṭaṃ tiroselaṃ, pabbatañcāpi kevalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samatikkamma {note:sabbatthapī evameva dissati} passāmi, ekadīpassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
137\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Visamā me samā honti, andhakāro na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Nāhaṃ passāmi timiraṃ, ekadīpassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
138\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ dīpamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ekadīpassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
139\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
140\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
141\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekadīpiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ekadīpiyattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 7. Ucchaṅgapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
142\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare bandhumatiyā, ahosiṃ māliko tadā;
::

::gathalast
Ucchaṅgaṃ pūrayitvāna, agamaṃ antarāpaṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
143\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhagavā {pb:T:2.0017}{pb:M:1.0441}{pb:V:1.0412} tamhi samaye, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato;
::

::gathalast
Mahatā ānubhāvena, niyyāti lokanāyako.
::

::hangnum
144\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvāna {pb:P:2.0375} lokapajjotaṃ, vipassiṃ lokatāraṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pupphaṃ paggayha ucchaṅgā, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ apūjayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
145\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.

#### 8. Yāgudāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
149\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atithiṃ {note:atītaṃ (ka.)} me gahetvāna, agacchiṃ gāmakaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Sampuṇṇanadikaṃ disvā, saṅghārāmaṃ upāgamiṃ.
::

::hangnum
150\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āraññakā dhutadharā, jhāyino lūkhacīvarā;
::

::gathalast
Vivekābhiratā dhīrā, saṅghārāme vasanti te.
::

::hangnum
151\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gati {pb:T:2.0018} tesaṃ upacchinnā, suvimuttāna tādinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Piṇḍāya te na gacchanti, oruddhanaditāya hi {note:oruddhanadikāyatiṃ (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
152\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, vedajāto katañjalī;
::

::gathalast
Taṇḍulaṃ me gahetvāna, yāgudānaṃ adāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
153\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcannaṃ yāguṃ datvāna, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi;
::

::gathalast
Sakakammābhiraddhohaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
154\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maṇimayañca {pb:M:1.0442} me byamhaṃ, nibbatti tidase gaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Nārīgaṇehi sahito, modāmi byamhamuttame.
::

::hangnum
155\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tettiṃsakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tiṃsakkhattuṃ cakkavattī, mahārajjamakārayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
156\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padesarajjaṃ {pb:V:1.0413} vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Devaloke manusse vā, anubhotvā sayaṃ {note:yasaṃ (syā.)} ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
157\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pacchime bhave sampatte, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saha oropite kese, sabbaṃ sampaṭivijjhahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
158\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khayato vayato cāpi, sammasanto kaḷevaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pure sikkhāpadādānā, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
159\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sudinnaṃ {pb:P:2.0376} me dānavaraṃ, vāṇijjaṃ sampayojitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Teneva yāgudānena, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
160\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sokaṃ pariddavaṃ byādhiṃ, darathaṃ cittatāpanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nābhijānāmi uppannaṃ, yāgudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
161\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāguṃ {pb:T:2.0019} saṅghassa datvāna, puññakkhette anuttare;
::

::gathalast
Pañcānisaṃse anubhomi, aho yāgusuyiṭṭhatā.
::

::hangnum
162\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abyādhitā rūpavatā, khippaṃ dhammanisantitā {note:nibujjhitā (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Lābhitā annapānassa, āyu pañcamakaṃ mama.
::

::hangnum
163\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo koci vedaṃ janayaṃ, saṅghe yāguṃ dadeyya so;
::

::gathalast
Imāni pañca ṭhānāni, paṭigaṇheyya paṇḍito.
::

::hangnum
164\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Karaṇīyaṃ kataṃ sabbaṃ, bhavā ugghāṭitā mayā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
::

::hangnum
165\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So ahaṃ vicarissāmi, gāmā gāmaṃ purā puraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Namassamāno sambuddhaṃ, dhammassa ca sudhammataṃ.
::

::hangnum
166\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, yāgudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
167\.
::

::gatha1

::hangnum

#### 9. Patthodanadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
170\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vanacārī {pb:T:2.0020}{pb:V:1.0414} pure āsiṃ, satataṃ vanakammiko;
::

::gathalast
Patthodanaṃ gahetvāna, kammantaṃ agamāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
171\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vanā piṇḍāya nikkhantaṃ, disvā cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
172\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Parakammāyane {note:vayakammāyane (ka.)} yutto, puññañca me na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Ayaṃ patthodano atthi, bhojayissāmahaṃ {note:bhojayissāmi maṃ (syā.)} muniṃ.
::

::hangnum
173\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Patthodanaṃ gahetvāna, sayambhussa adāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mama nijjhāyamānassa, paribhuñji tadā muni.
::

::hangnum
174\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
175\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chattiṃsakkhattuṃ {pb:P:2.0377} devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
176\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sukhito yasavā homi, patthodanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
177\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavābhave saṃsaranto, labhāmi amitaṃ dhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhoge me ūnatā natthi, patthodanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
178\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nadīsotapaṭibhāgā{pb:M:1.0444}, bhogā nibbattare mama;
::

::gathalast
Parimetuṃ na sakkomi, patthodanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
179\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imaṃ {pb:T:2.0021} khāda imaṃ bhuñja, imamhi sayane saya;
::

::gathalast
Tenāhaṃ sukhito homi, patthodanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
180\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast

#### 10. Mañcadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
184\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Parinibbute kāruṇike, siddhatthe lokanāyake;
::

::gathalast
Vitthārike pāvacane, devamānusasakkate.
::

::hangnum
185\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Caṇḍālo āsahaṃ tattha, āsandipīṭhakārako;
::

::gathalast
Tena kammena jīvāmi, tena posemi dārake.
::

::hangnum
186\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āsandiṃ sukataṃ katvā, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi;
::

::gathalast
Sayamevupagantvāna, bhikkhusaṅghassadāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
187\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:T:2.0022} kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
188\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devalokagato santo, modāmi tidase gaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Sayanāni mahagghāni, nibbattanti yadicchakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
189\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paññāsakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asītikkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
190\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padesarajjaṃ {pb:M:1.0445}{pb:P:2.0378} vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sukhito yasavā homi, mañcadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
191\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devalokā cavitvāna, emi ce mānusaṃ bhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mahārahā susayanā, sayameva bhavanti me.
::

::hangnum
192\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ayaṃ pacchimako mayhaṃ, carimo vattate bhavo;
::

::gathalast
Ajjāpi sayane kāle {note:sayanakāle (syā.)}, sayanaṃ upatiṭṭhati.
::

::hangnum
193\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, mañcadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
194\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:V:1.0416} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
195\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
196\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ {pb:T:2.0023} sudaṃ āyasmā mañcadāyako thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Mañcadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Bhaddālivaggo bācattālīsamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Bhaddālī ekachatto ca, tiṇasūlo ca maṃsado;
::

::gathalast
Nāgapallaviko dīpī, ucchaṅgi yāgudāyako.
::

::gatha1
Patthodanī mañcadado, gāthāyo gaṇitā ciha;
::

::gathalast
Dvesatāni ca gāthānaṃ, gāthā cekā taduttari.
::
